<!-- ══ NOTIFICACIÓN DE LOGRO DESBLOQUEADO ══ -->
<div id="achievNotif" class="an-hidden">
  <span class="an-icon">🏅</span>
  <div class="an-info">
    <div class="an-header">
      <span class="an-label">LOGRO DESBLOQUEADO</span>
      <span class="an-rarity">Común</span>
    </div>
    <div class="an-name">Nombre del logro</div>
    <div class="an-desc">Descripción del logro</div>
  </div>

<script>
/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   🔊 OCHO LOCOS PRO – Motor de Audio Profesional v8.0
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   100% sintetizado · sin URLs externas · Web Audio API
   Arquitectura:
     AudioContext → FX chains → DynamicsCompressor (master) → output
   Técnicas:
     • Síntesis FM (frecuencia modulada) para timbres ricos
     • Síntesis aditiva + substractiva en capas
     • Convolver reverb sintético (IR noise decay)
     • Filtros dinámicos (sweep, resonancia, formantes)
     • Ruido blanco/rosado/marrón para percusión realista
     • ADSR preciso por capa
     • Compresión dinámica maestra para mezcla limpia
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

let muted = false;
let _actx = null;
let _masterComp = null;
let _reverbNode  = null;

/* ── Obtener / crear contexto ── */
function getCtx() {
  if (!_actx) _actx = new (window.AudioContext || window.webkitAudioContext)();
  if (_actx.state === 'suspended') _actx.resume();
  return _actx;
}

/* ── Master bus: compresor dinámico (evita clipping, mezcla suave) ── */
function getMaster(ctx) {
  if (!_masterComp || _masterComp.context !== ctx) {
    const comp = ctx.createDynamicsCompressor();
    comp.threshold.value = -14;   // comienza a comprimir a -14 dBFS
    comp.knee.value      = 10;    // transición suave de 10 dB
    comp.ratio.value     = 5;     // 5:1
    comp.attack.value    = 0.003; // 3 ms
    comp.release.value   = 0.12;  // 120 ms
    comp.connect(ctx.destination);
    _masterComp = comp;
  }
  return _masterComp;
}

/* ── Reverb sintético: IR de ruido con decaimiento exponencial ── */
function getReverb(ctx) {
  if (_reverbNode && _reverbNode.context === ctx) return _reverbNode;
  const len = Math.ceil(ctx.sampleRate * 1.2);
  const ir  = ctx.createBuffer(2, len, ctx.sampleRate);
  for (let ch = 0; ch < 2; ch++) {
    const d = ir.getChannelData(ch);
    for (let i = 0; i < len; i++) {
      d[i] = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * Math.pow(1 - i / len, 3.5);
    }
  }
  const conv = ctx.createConvolver();
  conv.buffer = ir;
  _reverbNode = conv;
  // La salida del convolver va al master
  const reverbGain = ctx.createGain();
  reverbGain.gain.value = 0.22;
  conv.connect(reverbGain);
  reverbGain.connect(getMaster(ctx));
  return conv;
}

/* ── Generadores de ruido ── */
function makeNoise(ctx, dur, type = 'white') {
  const n   = Math.ceil(ctx.sampleRate * dur);
  const buf = ctx.createBuffer(1, n, ctx.sampleRate);
  const d   = buf.getChannelData(0);
  if (type === 'white') {
    for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) d[i] = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
  } else if (type === 'pink') {
    // Algoritmo de Voss-McCartney simplificado
    let b0=0,b1=0,b2=0,b3=0,b4=0,b5=0,b6=0;
    for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
      const w = Math.random() * 2 - 1;
      b0 = 0.99886*b0 + w*0.0555179; b1 = 0.99332*b1 + w*0.0750759;
      b2 = 0.96900*b2 + w*0.1538520; b3 = 0.86650*b3 + w*0.3104856;
      b4 = 0.55000*b4 + w*0.5329522; b5 = -0.7616*b5 - w*0.0168980;
      d[i] = (b0+b1+b2+b3+b4+b5+b6+w*0.5362) * 0.11;
      b6 = w * 0.115926;
    }
  } else if (type === 'brown') {
    let last = 0;
    for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
      const w = (Math.random() * 2 - 1) * 0.02;
      last += w; if (last > 1) last = 1; if (last < -1) last = -1;
      d[i] = last;
    }
  }
  return buf;
}

/* ── Helper: conectar osc/src con filtro, ganancia → destino ── */
function chain(ctx, src, ...nodes) {
  const master = getMaster(ctx);
  let last = src;
  for (const n of nodes) { last.connect(n); last = n; }
  last.connect(master);
  return last;
}

/* ── Helper: crear oscilador con envolvente ADSR ── */
function makeOsc(ctx, freq, type, startT, attack, decay, sustain, release, vol, dest) {
  const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
  const g   = ctx.createGain();
  osc.type = type;
  if (typeof freq === 'function') freq(osc.frequency, ctx, startT);
  else osc.frequency.value = freq;
  g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startT);
  g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, startT + attack);
  g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol * sustain, startT + attack + decay);
  g.gain.setValueAtTime(vol * sustain, startT + attack + decay);
  g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, startT + attack + decay + release);
  osc.connect(g); g.connect(dest || getMaster(ctx));
  osc.start(startT);
  osc.stop(startT + attack + decay + release + 0.01);
  return osc;
}

/* ── Helper: síntesis FM (carrier + modulator) ── */
function makeFM(ctx, carrierFreq, modRatio, modIndex, startT, dur, vol, dest) {
  const master = dest || getMaster(ctx);
  const carrier = ctx.createOscillator();
  const modOsc  = ctx.createOscillator();
  const modGain = ctx.createGain();
  carrier.type = 'sine';
  modOsc.type  = 'sine';
  carrier.frequency.value = carrierFreq;
  modOsc.frequency.value  = carrierFreq * modRatio;
  modGain.gain.value = carrierFreq * modIndex;
  modOsc.connect(modGain);
  modGain.connect(carrier.frequency);
  const envGain = ctx.createGain();
  envGain.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startT);
  envGain.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, startT + 0.01);
  envGain.gain.setValueAtTime(vol, startT + dur * 0.7);
  envGain.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.0001, startT + dur);
  carrier.connect(envGain);
  envGain.connect(master);
  carrier.start(startT); modOsc.start(startT);
  carrier.stop(startT + dur); modOsc.stop(startT + dur);
  return { carrier, modOsc };
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MÚSICA DE FONDO — completamente remodelada
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
let _menuMusicNodes = [];
let _gameMusicNodes = [];
let _menuMusicOn    = false;
let _gameMusicOn    = false;

/* ── Nota musical simple (para arreglos) ── */
function playNote(ctx, freq, startT, dur, vol = 0.07, type = 'triangle', dest) {
  const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
  const g   = ctx.createGain();
  osc.type = type; osc.frequency.value = freq;
  g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startT);
  g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(vol, startT + 0.025);
  g.gain.setValueAtTime(vol, startT + dur - 0.05);
  g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, startT + dur);
  osc.connect(g); g.connect(dest || getMaster(ctx));
  osc.start(startT); osc.stop(startT + dur + 0.02);
}

/* ── MÚSICA DE MENÚ: Jazz de casino ── */
function startMenuMusic() {
  if (muted || _menuMusicOn) return;
  _menuMusicOn = true;
  const ctx = getCtx();
  const master = getMaster(ctx);
  let loopTimer;

  // Notas de jazz en Am pentatónica (casino lounge feel)
  const MELODY = [
    // Frase 1: subida
    {f:440,d:0.35,v:0.10},{f:493.88,d:0.20,v:0.08},{f:523.25,d:0.35,v:0.10},
    {f:587.33,d:0.20,v:0.08},{f:659.25,d:0.55,v:0.12},
    // Frase 2: bajada ornamentada
    {f:587.33,d:0.18,v:0.08},{f:523.25,d:0.18,v:0.08},{f:493.88,d:0.35,v:0.10},
    {f:440,d:0.20,v:0.07},{f:392,d:0.55,v:0.11},
    // Frase 3: giro
    {f:349.23,d:0.25,v:0.09},{f:392,d:0.20,v:0.08},{f:440,d:0.20,v:0.09},
    {f:493.88,d:0.20,v:0.08},{f:523.25,d:0.45,v:0.11},
    // Pausa + resolución
    {f:0,d:0.25,v:0},{f:659.25,d:0.20,v:0.09},{f:587.33,d:0.20,v:0.08},
    {f:523.25,d:0.20,v:0.09},{f:493.88,d:0.20,v:0.08},{f:440,d:0.70,v:0.10},
  ];
  // Acordes (Am9 - Fmaj7 - C - E7)
  const CHORDS = [
    {notes:[220,261.63,329.63,392],  t:0,    dur:1.8},
    {notes:[174.61,220,261.63,349.23],t:1.9, dur:1.8},
    {notes:[261.63,329.63,392,493.88],t:3.8, dur:1.8},
    {notes:[164.81,207.65,329.63,415.3],t:5.7,dur:1.8},
  ];
  // Línea de bajo (contrabajo → sawtooth filtrado)
  const BASS = [110,110,130.81,110,87.31,87.31,98,87.31,82.41,82.41,98,110];

  function playMenuLoop() {
    if (!_menuMusicOn || muted) return;
    const base = ctx.currentTime + 0.06;
    const beat = 0.42; // ~143 bpm

    // Bajo
    BASS.forEach((f, i) => {
      if (!f) return;
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const lp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter();
      const g   = ctx.createGain();
      osc.type = 'sawtooth'; osc.frequency.value = f;
      lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 320;
      const t = base + i * beat * 0.5;
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
      g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.14, t + 0.03);
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.14, t + beat * 0.35);
      g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + beat * 0.48);
      osc.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(master);
      osc.start(t); osc.stop(t + beat * 0.5);
    });

    // Acordes de piano (FM para timbre de piano)
    CHORDS.forEach(chord => {
      chord.notes.forEach(f => {
        makeFM(ctx, f, 3.5, 0.7, base + chord.t, chord.dur * 0.9, 0.05, master);
      });
    });

    // Melodía principal (vibraphone: FM con ratio 3.5)
    let melT = base + 0.05;
    MELODY.forEach(note => {
      if (note.f > 0) {
        makeFM(ctx, note.f, 3.5, 0.45, melT, note.d * 0.95, note.v, master);
        // Pequeña segunda voz (harmonizando en terceras)
        if (note.v > 0.08) makeFM(ctx, note.f * 1.26, 3.5, 0.3, melT + 0.01, note.d * 0.8, note.v * 0.45, master);
      }
      melT += note.d;
    });

    // Hi-hat metálico (ruido rosado + HP + ataque rápido)
    for (let h = 0; h < 16; h++) {
      const ht = base + h * beat * 0.25;
      const nb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.06, 'pink');
      const ns = ctx.createBufferSource(); ns.buffer = nb;
      const hf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); hf.type = 'highpass'; hf.frequency.value = 7000;
      const hg = ctx.createGain();
      const vel = h % 4 === 0 ? 0.09 : (h % 2 === 0 ? 0.055 : 0.03);
      hg.gain.setValueAtTime(vel, ht);
      hg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ht + 0.055);
      ns.connect(hf); hf.connect(hg); hg.connect(master);
      ns.start(ht); ns.stop(ht + 0.06);
    }

    // Bombo en tiempos 1 y 3 (ruido marrón + osc grave)
    [0, 2, 4, 6].forEach(b => {
      const bt = base + b * beat * 0.5;
      // Componente tonal
      makeOsc(ctx, (freq,_,t)=>{freq.setValueAtTime(120,t);freq.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(50,t+0.15);},
              'sine', bt, 0.005, 0.08, 0, 0.12, 0.16, master);
      // Ruido de bombo
      const db = makeNoise(ctx, 0.18, 'brown');
      const ds = ctx.createBufferSource(); ds.buffer = db;
      const dlp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); dlp.type = 'lowpass'; dlp.frequency.value = 160;
      const dg = ctx.createGain();
      dg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.18, bt); dg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bt + 0.18);
      ds.connect(dlp); dlp.connect(dg); dg.connect(master);
      ds.start(bt); ds.stop(bt + 0.18);
    });

    // Caja en tiempos 2 y 4
    [1, 3, 5, 7].forEach(b => {
      const st = base + b * beat * 0.5;
      const sb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.14, 'white');
      const ss = ctx.createBufferSource(); ss.buffer = sb;
      const sf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); sf.type = 'bandpass'; sf.frequency.value = 1800; sf.Q.value = 0.9;
      const sg = ctx.createGain();
      sg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.12, st); sg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, st + 0.14);
      ss.connect(sf); sf.connect(sg); sg.connect(master);
      ss.start(st); ss.stop(st + 0.14);
    });

    const loopDur = BASS.length * beat * 0.5;
    loopTimer = setTimeout(playMenuLoop, (loopDur - 0.12) * 1000);
  }

  playMenuLoop();
  _menuMusicNodes = [{ stop: () => { _menuMusicOn = false; clearTimeout(loopTimer); } }];
}

function stopMenuMusic() {
  _menuMusicOn = false;
  _menuMusicNodes.forEach(n => { try { n.stop && n.stop(); } catch(e){} });
  _menuMusicNodes = [];
}

/* ── MÚSICA DE JUEGO: Suspense de casino / thriller ── */
function startGameMusic() {
  if (muted || _gameMusicOn) return;
  _gameMusicOn = true;
  const ctx = getCtx();
  const master = getMaster(ctx);
  let loopTimer2;

  // Bajo ostinato (5 notas cromaticas)
  const GBASS  = [98, 103.83, 110, 116.54, 123.47, 116.54, 110, 103.83];
  // Arpegio de tensión
  const GARP   = [293.66, 369.99, 440, 493.88, 523.25, 493.88, 440, 369.99,
                  349.23, 392.00, 466.16, 523.25, 554.37, 523.25, 466.16, 392.00];
  // Contramelodía (violines / flautas)
  const GMELÓ  = [440,0,493.88,0,523.25,493.88,440,392, 369.99,0,392,0,440,0,493.88,0];

  function playGameLoop() {
    if (!_gameMusicOn || muted) return;
    const base  = ctx.currentTime + 0.06;
    const beat  = 0.38; // ~158 bpm – más urgente que el menú

    // Bajo pulsante (staccato, sawtooth)
    GBASS.forEach((f, i) => {
      const t = base + i * beat * 0.5;
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const lp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter();
      const g   = ctx.createGain();
      osc.type = 'sawtooth'; osc.frequency.value = f;
      lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 280; lp.Q.value = 1.2;
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
      g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.18, t + 0.015);
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.18, t + 0.1);
      g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + beat * 0.38);
      osc.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(master);
      osc.start(t); osc.stop(t + beat * 0.5);
    });

    // Arpegio de piano (FM synthesis)
    GARP.forEach((f, i) => {
      const t = base + i * beat * 0.25;
      makeFM(ctx, f, 3.0, 0.6, t, beat * 0.4, 0.055, master);
    });

    // Contramelodía (flautín: FM ratio 5.0)
    GMELÓ.forEach((f, i) => {
      if (!f) return;
      const t = base + i * beat * 0.5;
      makeFM(ctx, f * 2, 5.0, 0.2, t, beat * 0.45, 0.04, master);
    });

    // Hi-hat 16avos (muy preciso, como máquina de ritmo)
    for (let h = 0; h < 16; h++) {
      const ht  = base + h * beat * 0.25;
      const nb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.04, 'pink');
      const ns  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ns.buffer = nb;
      const hpf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); hpf.type = 'highpass'; hpf.frequency.value = 9000;
      const hg  = ctx.createGain();
      const vel = h % 4 === 0 ? 0.10 : (h % 2 === 0 ? 0.06 : 0.035);
      hg.gain.setValueAtTime(vel, ht); hg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ht + 0.038);
      ns.connect(hpf); hpf.connect(hg); hg.connect(master);
      ns.start(ht); ns.stop(ht + 0.04);
    }

    // Bombo "electro" (click + tono grave)
    [0, 1.5, 2.5, 3.5].forEach(b => {
      const bt = base + b * beat;
      makeOsc(ctx, (freq,_,t)=>{freq.setValueAtTime(200,t);freq.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(45,t+0.20);},
              'sine', bt, 0.004, 0.12, 0, 0.08, 0.22, master);
      const click = makeNoise(ctx, 0.04, 'white');
      const cs = ctx.createBufferSource(); cs.buffer = click;
      const cg = ctx.createGain();
      cg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.28, bt); cg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bt + 0.04);
      cs.connect(cg); cg.connect(master); cs.start(bt); cs.stop(bt + 0.04);
    });

    // Caja + reverb
    [1, 3].forEach(b => {
      const st = base + b * beat;
      const rev = getReverb(ctx);
      const sb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.18, 'white');
      const ss  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ss.buffer = sb;
      const sf  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); sf.type = 'bandpass'; sf.frequency.value = 2000; sf.Q.value = 0.8;
      const sg  = ctx.createGain();
      sg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.16, st); sg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, st + 0.18);
      ss.connect(sf); sf.connect(sg); sg.connect(master);
      // Reverb send (15%)
      const svSend = ctx.createGain(); svSend.gain.value = 0.15;
      sg.connect(svSend); svSend.connect(rev);
      ss.start(st); ss.stop(st + 0.18);
    });

    const loopDur = GBASS.length * beat * 0.5;
    loopTimer2 = setTimeout(playGameLoop, (loopDur - 0.1) * 1000);
  }

  playGameLoop();
  _gameMusicNodes = [{ stop: () => { _gameMusicOn = false; clearTimeout(loopTimer2); } }];
}

function stopGameMusic() {
  _gameMusicOn = false;
  _gameMusicNodes.forEach(n => { try { n.stop && n.stop(); } catch(e){} });
  _gameMusicNodes = [];
}

function toggleMute() {
  muted = !muted;
  document.getElementById('muteBtn').textContent = muted ? '🔇' : '🔊';
  if (muted) { stopMenuMusic(); stopGameMusic(); }
  else {
    const gs = document.getElementById('gameScreen');
    if (!gs.classList.contains('hidden')) startGameMusic();
    else startMenuMusic();
  }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   EFECTOS DE SONIDO — Síntesis profesional por capas
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── 🔀 BARAJAR — 3 pasadas de riffle + corte ── */
function sfxShuffle() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t0     = ctx.currentTime;

    function riffle(startT, dur, speed) {
      // Ruido rosa filtrado (textura de papel)
      const nb  = makeNoise(ctx, dur, 'pink');
      const src = ctx.createBufferSource(); src.buffer = nb;
      const bp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); bp.type = 'bandpass'; bp.frequency.value = 1800; bp.Q.value = 0.8;
      const hp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); hp.type = 'highpass'; hp.frequency.value = 900;
      // LFO tremolo (simula cartas pasando)
      const lfo  = ctx.createOscillator();
      const lfoG = ctx.createGain();
      lfo.type = 'sine'; lfo.frequency.value = speed;
      lfoG.gain.value = 0.22;
      const envG = ctx.createGain();
      envG.gain.setValueAtTime(0, startT);
      envG.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.40, startT + 0.08);
      envG.gain.setValueAtTime(0.40, startT + dur - 0.18);
      envG.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, startT + dur);
      lfo.connect(lfoG); lfoG.connect(envG.gain);
      src.connect(hp); hp.connect(bp); bp.connect(envG); envG.connect(master);
      src.start(startT); lfo.start(startT);
      src.stop(startT + dur); lfo.stop(startT + dur);

      // Impacto de juntado de mazo (al final de cada riffle)
      const imp = makeNoise(ctx, 0.06, 'white');
      const is  = ctx.createBufferSource(); is.buffer = imp;
      const ibp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); ibp.type = 'bandpass'; ibp.frequency.value = 1200; ibp.Q.value = 1.5;
      const ig  = ctx.createGain();
      ig.gain.setValueAtTime(0.32, startT + dur - 0.05);
      ig.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, startT + dur + 0.06);
      is.connect(ibp); ibp.connect(ig); ig.connect(master);
      is.start(startT + dur - 0.05); is.stop(startT + dur + 0.06);
    }

    riffle(t0,        1.35, 9);
    riffle(t0 + 1.6,  1.30, 11);
    riffle(t0 + 3.1,  1.25, 13);

    // Whoosh de corte final
    const wsb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.28, 'pink');
    const ws  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ws.buffer = wsb;
    const wf  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); wf.type = 'bandpass';
    wf.frequency.setValueAtTime(3500, t0 + 4.5);
    wf.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(700, t0 + 4.78);
    wf.Q.value = 0.7;
    const wg  = ctx.createGain();
    wg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t0 + 4.5);
    wg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.38, t0 + 4.55);
    wg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t0 + 4.78);
    ws.connect(wf); wf.connect(wg); wg.connect(master);
    ws.start(t0 + 4.5); ws.stop(t0 + 4.82);

    // Clicks finales (cartas igualadas)
    [0, 0.08, 0.17, 0.27].forEach((d, i) => {
      const ct  = t0 + 4.82 + d;
      const cb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.05, 'white');
      const cs  = ctx.createBufferSource(); cs.buffer = cb;
      const chp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); chp.type = 'highpass'; chp.frequency.value = 4000;
      const cg  = ctx.createGain();
      cg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.30 - i * 0.05, ct);
      cg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ct + 0.05);
      cs.connect(chp); chp.connect(cg); cg.connect(master);
      cs.start(ct); cs.stop(ct + 0.05);
    });
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxShuffle:', e); }
}

/* ── 📤 REPARTIR — click de papel + deslizamiento rápido ── */
function sfxDeal() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // 1) Fricción del pulgar (ruido HP muy corto, 0-8ms)
    const tb   = makeNoise(ctx, 0.022, 'pink');
    const ts   = ctx.createBufferSource(); ts.buffer = tb;
    const thp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); thp.type = 'highpass'; thp.frequency.value = 6000;
    const tg   = ctx.createGain();
    tg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.28, t); tg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.022);
    ts.connect(thp); thp.connect(tg); tg.connect(master);
    ts.start(t); ts.stop(t + 0.025);

    // 2) Deslizamiento de carta (swoosh, 8-55ms)
    const swb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.06, 'pink');
    const sws  = ctx.createBufferSource(); sws.buffer = swb;
    const swbp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); swbp.type = 'bandpass';
    swbp.frequency.setValueAtTime(3200, t + 0.008);
    swbp.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(900, t + 0.055);
    swbp.Q.value = 1.2;
    const swg  = ctx.createGain();
    swg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t + 0.008);
    swg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.22, t + 0.018);
    swg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 0.055);
    sws.connect(swbp); swbp.connect(swg); swg.connect(master);
    sws.start(t + 0.008); sws.stop(t + 0.06);

    // 3) Impacto de aterrizaje (golpe seco, 55-100ms)
    const ib  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.06, 'white');
    const is  = ctx.createBufferSource(); is.buffer = ib;
    const ibp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); ibp.type = 'bandpass'; ibp.frequency.value = 650; ibp.Q.value = 2.0;
    const ig  = ctx.createGain();
    ig.gain.setValueAtTime(0.38, t + 0.055); ig.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.11);
    is.connect(ibp); ibp.connect(ig); ig.connect(master);
    is.start(t + 0.055); is.stop(t + 0.12);

    // 4) Resonancia del tapete (~C4: 261Hz, suavísima)
    makeOsc(ctx, 261.63, 'sine', t + 0.055, 0.004, 0.02, 0, 0.08, 0.04, master);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxDeal:', e); }
}

/* ── 🃏 COLOCAR CARTA — capas: whip + golpe + resonancia tapete ── */
function sfxPlace() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // 1) Whip: lanzamiento de carta (ruido HP descendente, 0-40ms)
    const wb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.05, 'pink');
    const ws  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ws.buffer = wb;
    const wf  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); wf.type = 'bandpass';
    wf.frequency.setValueAtTime(4500, t); wf.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(1200, t + 0.04);
    wf.Q.value = 0.8;
    const wg  = ctx.createGain();
    wg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); wg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.28, t + 0.008);
    wg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 0.04);
    ws.connect(wf); wf.connect(wg); wg.connect(master);
    ws.start(t); ws.stop(t + 0.05);

    // 2) Golpe principal (impacto sobre tapete, 35-130ms)
    const hb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.12, 'white');
    const hs  = ctx.createBufferSource(); hs.buffer = hb;
    const hbp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); hbp.type = 'bandpass'; hbp.frequency.value = 800; hbp.Q.value = 1.5;
    const hg  = ctx.createGain();
    hg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.44, t + 0.035); hg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.13);
    hs.connect(hbp); hbp.connect(hg); hg.connect(master);
    // Reverb send (10%)
    const hRevSend = ctx.createGain(); hRevSend.gain.value = 0.10;
    hg.connect(hRevSend); hRevSend.connect(rev);
    hs.start(t + 0.035); hs.stop(t + 0.14);

    // 3) Tono resonante del tapete (F3: ~174Hz)
    makeOsc(ctx, 174.61, 'sine', t + 0.035, 0.003, 0.04, 0.3, 0.14, 0.09, master);

    // 4) Brillo de alta frecuencia (HF snap, muy corto)
    const hfb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.025, 'white');
    const hfs = ctx.createBufferSource(); hfs.buffer = hfb;
    const hff = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); hff.type = 'highpass'; hff.frequency.value = 7000;
    const hfg = ctx.createGain();
    hfg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.18, t + 0.035); hfg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.06);
    hfs.connect(hff); hff.connect(hfg); hfg.connect(master);
    hfs.start(t + 0.035); hfs.stop(t + 0.065);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxPlace:', e); }
}

/* ── 📥 ROBAR CARTA — scrape + deslizamiento + pop ── */
function sfxDraw() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // 1) Scrape inicial (fricción con el tapete)
    const sb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.09, 'pink');
    const ss  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ss.buffer = sb;
    const slp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); slp.type = 'lowpass'; slp.frequency.value = 1800;
    const sg  = ctx.createGain();
    sg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t); sg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.24, t + 0.04);
    sg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.18, t + 0.07); sg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 0.09);
    ss.connect(slp); slp.connect(sg); sg.connect(master);
    ss.start(t); ss.stop(t + 0.1);

    // 2) Deslizamiento (papel sobre tapete) — BP sweeping up
    const db  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.10, 'pink');
    const ds  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ds.buffer = db;
    const dbp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); dbp.type = 'bandpass';
    dbp.frequency.setValueAtTime(800, t + 0.03);
    dbp.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(2800, t + 0.13);
    dbp.Q.value = 1.0;
    const dg  = ctx.createGain();
    dg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t + 0.03); dg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.28, t + 0.06);
    dg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 0.13);
    ds.connect(dbp); dbp.connect(dg); dg.connect(master);
    ds.start(t + 0.03); ds.stop(t + 0.15);

    // 3) Pop de separación (cuando la carta se levanta del mazo)
    const pb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.04, 'white');
    const ps  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ps.buffer = pb;
    const pbp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); pbp.type = 'bandpass'; pbp.frequency.value = 1400; pbp.Q.value = 2.5;
    const pg  = ctx.createGain();
    pg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.35, t + 0.12); pg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.16);
    ps.connect(pbp); pbp.connect(pg); pg.connect(master);
    ps.start(t + 0.12); ps.stop(t + 0.17);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxDraw:', e); }
}

/* ── 🏆 VICTORIA — fanfarria + lluvia de fichas + campanas ── */
function sfxVictory() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Fanfarria ascendente: C4-E4-G4-C5-E5 con FM
    const FANF = [
      {f:523.25, d:0, dur:0.50},
      {f:659.25, d:0.18, dur:0.45},
      {f:783.99, d:0.34, dur:0.45},
      {f:1046.5, d:0.52, dur:0.65},
      {f:1318.5, d:0.72, dur:0.85},
    ];
    FANF.forEach(note => {
      const nt = t + note.d;
      // Capa 1: sinusoidal principal
      makeOsc(ctx, note.f, 'sine', nt, 0.012, 0.05, 0.75, note.dur - 0.07, 0.25, master);
      // Capa 2: FM timbre de trompeta
      makeFM(ctx, note.f, 2.0, 1.2, nt, note.dur, 0.16, master);
      // Capa 3: segunda armónica (octava)
      makeOsc(ctx, note.f * 2, 'sine', nt, 0.015, 0.04, 0.5, note.dur * 0.6, 0.06, master);
      // Reverb send
      const rSend = ctx.createGain(); rSend.gain.value = 0.18;
      // (conectar indirectamente vía master ya tiene reverb)
    });

    // Glissando final brillante (C5→C6, violín)
    const glissFreqs = [1046.5, 1174.66, 1318.51, 1480.00, 1567.98, 2093.00];
    glissFreqs.forEach((f, i) => {
      const gt = t + 0.72 + i * 0.09;
      makeOsc(ctx, f, 'triangle', gt, 0.008, 0.02, 0.4, 0.18, 0.10, master);
    });

    // Lluvia de fichas de casino (12-18 clicks espaciados irregularmente)
    const chipCount = 15;
    for (let i = 0; i < chipCount; i++) {
      const delay = 0.9 + Math.random() * 1.4;
      const ct    = t + delay;
      // Fricción metálica de ficha
      const freq1 = 2000 + Math.random() * 3000;
      const freq2 = 800  + Math.random() * 600;
      const cb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.055, 'pink');
      const cs  = ctx.createBufferSource(); cs.buffer = cb;
      const chp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); chp.type = 'highpass'; chp.frequency.value = freq1;
      const clp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); clp.type = 'lowpass';  clp.frequency.value = freq2 + 4000;
      const cg  = ctx.createGain();
      cg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.22 + Math.random() * 0.12, ct);
      cg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ct + 0.055);
      cs.connect(chp); chp.connect(clp); clp.connect(cg); cg.connect(master);
      // Reverb send
      const cRev = ctx.createGain(); cRev.gain.value = 0.2;
      cg.connect(cRev); cRev.connect(rev);
      cs.start(ct); cs.stop(ct + 0.06);
      // Tono metálico de la ficha (breve)
      makeOsc(ctx, 800 + Math.random() * 400, 'sine', ct, 0.002, 0.005, 0, 0.05, 0.08, master);
    }

    // Tañido de campana final (C6, larga resonancia)
    const bellT = t + 1.05;
    const bOsc1 = ctx.createOscillator();
    const bOsc2 = ctx.createOscillator();
    const bG    = ctx.createGain();
    bOsc1.type = 'sine'; bOsc1.frequency.value = 2093.0;  // C7
    bOsc2.type = 'sine'; bOsc2.frequency.value = 2793.8;  // F7 (inarmónico)
    bG.gain.setValueAtTime(0, bellT);
    bG.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.20, bellT + 0.01);
    bG.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bellT + 2.2);
    bOsc1.connect(bG); bOsc2.connect(bG); bG.connect(master);
    // Reverb send
    const bRevSend = ctx.createGain(); bRevSend.gain.value = 0.30;
    bG.connect(bRevSend); bRevSend.connect(rev);
    bOsc1.start(bellT); bOsc2.start(bellT);
    bOsc1.stop(bellT + 2.3); bOsc2.stop(bellT + 2.3);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxVictory:', e); }
}

/* ── 💀 DERROTA — trombón descend. + golpe timbal + silencio ── */
function sfxDefeat() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Trombón descendente (G4-F4-Eb4-C4) con vibrato
    const TROM = [
      {f:392.00, d:0.00, dur:0.50},
      {f:349.23, d:0.30, dur:0.50},
      {f:311.13, d:0.60, dur:0.50},
      {f:261.63, d:0.90, dur:0.80},
    ];
    TROM.forEach(note => {
      const nt = t + note.d;
      // Carrier
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      osc.type = 'sawtooth'; osc.frequency.value = note.f;
      // Vibrato LFO
      const vib  = ctx.createOscillator();
      const vibG = ctx.createGain();
      vib.type = 'sine'; vib.frequency.value = 5.5;
      vibG.gain.value = note.f * 0.014; // vibrato ~1.4%
      vib.connect(vibG); vibG.connect(osc.frequency);
      // LP para timbre trombón
      const lp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); lp.type = 'lowpass';
      lp.frequency.value = 700; lp.Q.value = 0.8;
      const g  = ctx.createGain();
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, nt);
      g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.28, nt + 0.06);
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0.28, nt + note.dur - 0.12);
      g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, nt + note.dur);
      osc.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(master);
      // Reverb (35%)
      const rSend = ctx.createGain(); rSend.gain.value = 0.35;
      g.connect(rSend); rSend.connect(rev);
      osc.start(nt); vib.start(nt);
      osc.stop(nt + note.dur + 0.02); vib.stop(nt + note.dur + 0.02);
    });

    // Golpe de timbal (bombo grande)
    const drumT = t + 0.96;
    makeOsc(ctx, (f,_,dt)=>{f.setValueAtTime(95,dt);f.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(35,dt+0.35);},
            'sine', drumT, 0.004, 0.10, 0, 0.30, 0.30, master);
    // Ruido de timbal
    const db  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.45, 'brown');
    const ds  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ds.buffer = db;
    const dlp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); dlp.type = 'lowpass'; dlp.frequency.value = 280;
    const dg  = ctx.createGain();
    dg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.28, drumT); dg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, drumT + 0.45);
    ds.connect(dlp); dlp.connect(dg); dg.connect(master);
    const dRev = ctx.createGain(); dRev.gain.value = 0.25; dg.connect(dRev); dRev.connect(rev);
    ds.start(drumT); ds.stop(drumT + 0.46);

    // "Wah" final (filtro resonante pulsante)
    const wahT = t + 1.0;
    for (let w = 0; w < 3; w++) {
      const wt = wahT + w * 0.22;
      const wb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.18, 'pink');
      const ws = ctx.createBufferSource(); ws.buffer = wb;
      const wf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); wf.type = 'bandpass'; wf.Q.value = 6;
      wf.frequency.setValueAtTime(300 + w * 80, wt);
      wf.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(160, wt + 0.18);
      const wg = ctx.createGain();
      wg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.18 - w * 0.04, wt);
      wg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, wt + 0.18);
      ws.connect(wf); wf.connect(wg); wg.connect(master);
      ws.start(wt); ws.stop(wt + 0.2);
    }
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxDefeat:', e); }
}

/* ── 🎴 COMODÍN (8 jugado) — magia: sweep + arpegio + shimmer ── */
function sfxWildcard() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Sweep mágico ascendente (ruido BP + freq sweep)
    const swb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.40, 'pink');
    const sws = ctx.createBufferSource(); sws.buffer = swb;
    const swf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); swf.type = 'bandpass'; swf.Q.value = 2.5;
    swf.frequency.setValueAtTime(300, t);
    swf.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(4000, t + 0.36);
    const swg = ctx.createGain();
    swg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, t);
    swg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.38, t + 0.04);
    swg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + 0.38);
    sws.connect(swf); swf.connect(swg); swg.connect(master);
    sws.start(t); sws.stop(t + 0.40);

    // Arpegio ascendente mágico (pentatónica C: C5-E5-G5-C6-E6)
    const MAGIC = [523.25, 659.25, 783.99, 1046.5, 1318.51];
    MAGIC.forEach((f, i) => {
      const nt = t + i * 0.072;
      // Timbre: dos sinusoidales (fundamental + séptima armónica)
      makeOsc(ctx, f,       'sine',     nt, 0.008, 0.02, 0.5, 0.28, 0.22, master);
      makeOsc(ctx, f * 7.0, 'sine',     nt, 0.008, 0.01, 0.3, 0.08, 0.04, master);
      // Brillo
      makeFM(ctx, f * 2, 4.0, 0.4, nt, 0.20, 0.08, master);
      // Reverb
      const rS = ctx.createGain(); rS.gain.value = 0.22;
      // ya incluido vía master → reverb
    });

    // Campanilla de polvo de estrellas (shimmer: 3 notas agudas aleatorias)
    for (let s = 0; s < 6; s++) {
      const st = t + 0.28 + s * 0.06;
      const sf = 2000 + Math.random() * 1500;
      makeOsc(ctx, sf, 'sine', st, 0.004, 0.01, 0.2, 0.18, 0.05, master);
    }
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxWildcard:', e); }
}

/* ── 🎨 CAMBIO DE COLOR/PALO — campanillas modales ── */
function sfxColorChange() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Tres campanillas afinadas (modelo campana: fundamental + 2.76 inarmónico)
    const BELLS = [523.25, 698.46, 880.00]; // C5-F5-A5 (Do Mayor)
    BELLS.forEach((f, i) => {
      const bt = t + i * 0.115;
      // Fundamental
      const o1 = ctx.createOscillator();
      const g1 = ctx.createGain();
      o1.type = 'sine'; o1.frequency.value = f;
      g1.gain.setValueAtTime(0, bt); g1.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.24, bt + 0.012);
      g1.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bt + 0.72);
      o1.connect(g1); g1.connect(master);
      // Inarmónico (2.76× freq — característico de campanas)
      const o2 = ctx.createOscillator();
      const g2 = ctx.createGain();
      o2.type = 'sine'; o2.frequency.value = f * 2.756;
      g2.gain.setValueAtTime(0, bt); g2.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.10, bt + 0.010);
      g2.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bt + 0.35);
      o2.connect(g2); g2.connect(master);
      // Octava (5× freq)
      const o3 = ctx.createOscillator();
      const g3 = ctx.createGain();
      o3.type = 'sine'; o3.frequency.value = f * 5.4;
      g3.gain.setValueAtTime(0, bt); g3.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.04, bt + 0.008);
      g3.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, bt + 0.18);
      o3.connect(g3); g3.connect(master);
      // Reverb
      const rS = ctx.createGain(); rS.gain.value = 0.35;
      g1.connect(rS); rS.connect(rev);
      o1.start(bt); o2.start(bt); o3.start(bt);
      o1.stop(bt + 0.74); o2.stop(bt + 0.36); o3.stop(bt + 0.20);
    });

    // Destello brillante (G6 sostenida)
    const sparkT = t + 0.32;
    makeOsc(ctx, 1567.98, 'sine', sparkT, 0.008, 0.02, 0.4, 0.45, 0.12, master);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxColorChange:', e); }
}

/* ── 🤖 IA ESPECIAL — advertencia grave + impacto ── */
function sfxAiSpecial() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Dos pulsos de alarma (sawtooth + lowpass resonante)
    [0, 0.19].forEach((delay, i) => {
      const nt  = t + delay;
      const osc = ctx.createOscillator();
      const lp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter();
      const g   = ctx.createGain();
      osc.type = 'sawtooth';
      osc.frequency.setValueAtTime(195, nt);
      osc.frequency.linearRampToValueAtTime(125, nt + 0.15);
      lp.type = 'lowpass'; lp.frequency.value = 500; lp.Q.value = 4.0;
      g.gain.setValueAtTime(0, nt); g.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.30, nt + 0.02);
      g.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, nt + 0.16);
      osc.connect(lp); lp.connect(g); g.connect(master);
      osc.start(nt); osc.stop(nt + 0.17);
    });

    // Impacto percusivo (chasquido agresivo)
    const impT = t + 0.38;
    const ib   = makeNoise(ctx, 0.10, 'white');
    const is   = ctx.createBufferSource(); is.buffer = ib;
    const ibp  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); ibp.type = 'bandpass'; ibp.frequency.value = 1100; ibp.Q.value = 1.8;
    const ig   = ctx.createGain();
    ig.gain.setValueAtTime(0.40, impT); ig.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, impT + 0.10);
    is.connect(ibp); ibp.connect(ig); ig.connect(master);
    is.start(impT); is.stop(impT + 0.11);

    // Sub-grave (rumble ominoso)
    makeOsc(ctx, (f,_,nt)=>{f.setValueAtTime(85,nt);f.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(45,nt+0.30);},
            'sine', t + 0.35, 0.005, 0.08, 0.4, 0.22, 0.18, master);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxAiSpecial:', e); }
}

/* ── 🔘 BOTÓN UI — click limpio ── */
function sfxButton() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Ruido HP muy corto (click digital)
    const cb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.028, 'white');
    const cs  = ctx.createBufferSource(); cs.buffer = cb;
    const chp = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); chp.type = 'bandpass'; chp.frequency.value = 3200; chp.Q.value = 1.5;
    const cg  = ctx.createGain();
    cg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.26, t); cg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, t + 0.028);
    cs.connect(chp); chp.connect(cg); cg.connect(master);
    cs.start(t); cs.stop(t + 0.03);

    // Micro-tono de confirmación (E6 brevísima)
    makeOsc(ctx, 1318.51, 'sine', t, 0.004, 0.01, 0, 0.04, 0.08, master);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxButton:', e); }
}

/* ── 🔥 JUGADA MÚLTIPLE (combo) — notas ascend. rápidas ── */
function sfxCombo(count) {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;
    const n      = Math.min(count || 2, 6);
    // Escala pentatónica ascendente
    const PENTA = [523.25, 659.25, 783.99, 880.0, 1046.5, 1318.51];
    for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
      const nt = t + i * 0.07;
      makeFM(ctx, PENTA[i], 3.0, 0.5, nt, 0.22, 0.16, master);
      makeOsc(ctx, PENTA[i], 'sine', nt, 0.006, 0.02, 0.5, 0.12, 0.08, master);
    }
    // Whoosh de remate
    const swb = makeNoise(ctx, 0.18, 'pink');
    const sws = ctx.createBufferSource(); sws.buffer = swb;
    const swf = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); swf.type = 'bandpass';
    swf.frequency.setValueAtTime(1200, t + n * 0.07);
    swf.frequency.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(3800, t + n * 0.07 + 0.16);
    swf.Q.value = 1.0;
    const swg = ctx.createGain();
    swg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.26, t + n * 0.07);
    swg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0, t + n * 0.07 + 0.18);
    sws.connect(swf); swf.connect(swg); swg.connect(master);
    sws.start(t + n * 0.07); sws.stop(t + n * 0.07 + 0.2);
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxCombo:', e); }
}

/* ── 🏆 FANFARRIA DE TORNEO — victoria épica extendida ── */
function sfxTournamentFanfare() {
  try {
    const ctx    = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const rev    = getReverb(ctx);
    const t      = ctx.currentTime;

    // Fanfarria heroica completa (8 notas)
    const FANF = [
      {f:523.25, d:0.00, dur:0.35},  // C5
      {f:523.25, d:0.30, dur:0.20},  // C5
      {f:659.25, d:0.52, dur:0.20},  // E5
      {f:783.99, d:0.72, dur:0.25},  // G5
      {f:1046.5, d:0.98, dur:0.55},  // C6
      {f:880.00, d:1.48, dur:0.30},  // A5
      {f:1046.5, d:1.78, dur:0.30},  // C6
      {f:1318.5, d:2.08, dur:1.20},  // E6 (resolución)
    ];

    FANF.forEach(note => {
      const nt = t + note.d;
      // Trompeta (FM: carrier + modulación 2:1)
      makeFM(ctx, note.f, 2.0, 1.8, nt, note.dur, 0.20, master);
      // Capa de brillo
      makeOsc(ctx, note.f * 2, 'sine', nt, 0.01, 0.03, 0.4, note.dur * 0.7, 0.07, master);
      // Reverb
      const rS = ctx.createGain(); rS.gain.value = 0.28;
      getMaster(ctx).connect && rS.connect && rS.connect(rev); // intentar reverb
    });

    // Redoble de tambor (snare rápido crescendo → fortíssimo)
    for (let r = 0; r < 12; r++) {
      const rt  = t + 0.9 + r * 0.08;
      const vol = 0.08 + r * 0.018;
      const sb  = makeNoise(ctx, 0.07, 'white');
      const ss  = ctx.createBufferSource(); ss.buffer = sb;
      const sf  = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); sf.type = 'bandpass'; sf.frequency.value = 1800; sf.Q.value = 1.2;
      const sg  = ctx.createGain();
      sg.gain.setValueAtTime(vol, rt); sg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, rt + 0.07);
      ss.connect(sf); sf.connect(sg); sg.connect(master);
      ss.start(rt); ss.stop(rt + 0.08);
    }

    // Platillo crash al final
    const crashT = t + 1.95;
    const crb    = makeNoise(ctx, 1.5, 'pink');
    const crs    = ctx.createBufferSource(); crs.buffer = crb;
    const crhp   = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); crhp.type = 'highpass'; crhp.frequency.value = 5000;
    const crg    = ctx.createGain();
    crg.gain.setValueAtTime(0, crashT); crg.gain.linearRampToValueAtTime(0.38, crashT + 0.008);
    crg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, crashT + 1.5);
    crs.connect(crhp); crhp.connect(crg); crg.connect(master);
    const crRevS = ctx.createGain(); crRevS.gain.value = 0.45;
    crg.connect(crRevS); crRevS.connect(rev);
    crs.start(crashT); crs.stop(crashT + 1.55);

    // Lluvia de fichas (igual que victoria pero más densa)
    for (let i = 0; i < 22; i++) {
      const delay = 2.1 + Math.random() * 1.8;
      const ct    = t + delay;
      const cb    = makeNoise(ctx, 0.05, 'pink');
      const cs    = ctx.createBufferSource(); cs.buffer = cb;
      const chp   = ctx.createBiquadFilter(); chp.type = 'highpass';
      chp.frequency.value = 2500 + Math.random() * 3000;
      const cg    = ctx.createGain();
      cg.gain.setValueAtTime(0.24 + Math.random() * 0.10, ct);
      cg.gain.exponentialRampToValueAtTime(0.001, ct + 0.055);
      cs.connect(chp); chp.connect(cg); cg.connect(master);
      const chipRev = ctx.createGain(); chipRev.gain.value = 0.22;
      cg.connect(chipRev); chipRev.connect(rev);
      cs.start(ct); cs.stop(ct + 0.06);
      makeOsc(ctx, 900 + Math.random() * 500, 'sine', ct, 0.002, 0.004, 0, 0.04, 0.07, master);
    }
  } catch(e) { console.warn('sfxTournamentFanfare:', e); }
}

/* ── noiseBuffer (retrocompatibilidad con código existente) ── */
function noiseBuffer(ctx, dur) { return makeNoise(ctx, dur, 'white'); }

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   DISPATCHER CENTRAL — playSound(name, vol)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function playSound(name, vol = 1) {
  if (muted) return;
  switch (name) {
    case 'shuffle':          sfxShuffle();              break;
    case 'deal':             sfxDeal();                 break;
    case 'place':            sfxPlace();                break;
    case 'draw':             sfxDraw();                 break;
    case 'victory':          sfxVictory();              break;
    case 'defeat':           sfxDefeat();               break;
    case 'wildcard':         sfxWildcard();             break;
    case 'colorChange':      sfxColorChange();          break;
    case 'aiSpecial':        sfxAiSpecial();            break;
    case 'button':           sfxButton();               break;
    case 'combo':            sfxCombo(vol);             break;
    case 'tournamentFanfare':sfxTournamentFanfare();    break;
  }
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   DIFICULTADES DE IA

   thinkDelay : ms de "pausa pensamiento"

   bluffRate  : prob. de NO usar la mejor carta
   cardSave8  : guarda el 8 para situación crítica
   multiPlay  : usa jugadas múltiples del mismo valor
   suitSmarts : elige palo óptimo al jugar 8
   lookAhead  : heurística de adelanto de jugada
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

function selectMode(m) {
  currentMode = m;
  document.querySelectorAll('.mode-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
  const btn = document.getElementById('mode-' + m);
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('selected');
  // Modo "IA Difícil" fuerza nivel mínimo Difícil
  if (m === 'dificil' && ['facil','normal'].includes(currentDiff)) selectDiff('dificil');
  // Toggle special panels
  const dailyPan = document.getElementById('dailyPanel');
  const pracPan  = document.getElementById('practicePanel');
  if (dailyPan) dailyPan.style.display  = (m === 'diario')   ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (pracPan)  pracPan.style.display   = (m === 'practica') ? 'block' : 'none';
  if (m === 'diario') renderDailyCard();
  if (m === 'practica') updatePracSlider(document.getElementById('pracSlider')?.value || 30);
}

function selectDiff(d) {
  currentDiff = d;
  document.querySelectorAll('.diff-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
  document.querySelector(`.diff-btn[data-d="${d}"]`).classList.add('selected');
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   SISTEMA DE PUNTUACIÓN & RÉCORDS (localStorage)
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const LS_SCORES = 'ol_scores_v1';
const LS_STATS  = 'ol_stats_v1';

function loadScores() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_SCORES))||[]; } catch(e){ return []; }
}
function saveScore(entry) {
  const scores = loadScores();
  scores.push(entry);
  scores.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);
  if (scores.length>50) scores.length=50;
  localStorage.setItem(LS_SCORES, JSON.stringify(scores));
}

function loadStats() {
  try {
    return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_STATS)) || {
      totalGames:0, wins:0, losses:0,
      winsByDiff:{facil:0,normal:0,dificil:0,experto:0},
      gamesPlayed:{facil:0,normal:0,dificil:0,experto:0},
      totalTime:0, totalTurns:0,
      cardFreq:{}, specialsPlayed:0
    };
  } catch(e) {
    return {totalGames:0,wins:0,losses:0,winsByDiff:{facil:0,normal:0,dificil:0,experto:0},
      gamesPlayed:{facil:0,normal:0,dificil:0,experto:0},totalTime:0,totalTurns:0,cardFreq:{},specialsPlayed:0};
  }
}
function saveStats(st) { localStorage.setItem(LS_STATS, JSON.stringify(st)); }

let gameStartTime = 0;

/* Calcular puntuación de partida */
function calcScore(playerWon, turnsN, pDrawsN, handSize, diffKey, timeSec) {
  if (!playerWon) return 0;
  let base = 1000;
  // Bonus por dificultad
  const diffBonus = {facil:1.0, normal:1.5, dificil:2.2, experto:3.5};
  base *= (diffBonus[diffKey]||1);
  // Penalización por cartas robadas
  base -= pDrawsN * 30;
  // Bonus por rapidez (menos turnos)
  base += Math.max(0, 200 - turnsN * 4);
  // Bonus velocidad (menos de 90s)
  if (timeSec < 90) base += Math.round((90 - timeSec) * 2);
  return Math.max(50, Math.round(base));
}

/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MULTIPLAYER LOCAL
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
let mpMode       = false;      // true cuando hay partida multi
let mpPlayers    = [];         // [{name, hand, score, totalScore}]
let mpCurrent    = 0;          // índice del jugador activo
let mpDirection  = 1;          // 1=horario, -1=antihorario
let mpCount      = 2;
let mpHandsEl    = {};         // refs a elementos DOM por jugador
let mpAccumDraw  = 0;          // cartas acumuladas (A y 2 encadenados)
let mpAccumType  = null;       // 'A' o '2' (tipo de acumulado activo)
let mpSilenceOn  = false;      // modo silencio (carta 7 activa)
let mpSilenceTimer = null;

function setMpCount(n) {
  mpCount = n;
  document.querySelectorAll('.mp-cnt-btn').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('selected'));
  document.getElementById('mpCnt'+n).classList.add('selected');
  // Mostrar/ocultar filas de nombre
  for (let i=0;i<4;i++) {
    const row = document.getElementById('mpN'+i);
    if (row) row.closest('.mp-player-row').style.display = i<n?'flex':'none';
  }
}

function openMultiplayer() {
  // Ensure rows 2-3 are hidden initially
  for (let i=2;i<4;i++) {
    const row = document.getElementById('mpN'+i);
    if (row) row.closest('.mp-player-row').style.display='none';
  }
  document.getElementById('multiModal').classList.add('open');
}
function closeMultiplayer() { document.getElementById('multiModal').classList.remove('open'); }

function startMultiplayer() {
  closeMultiplayer();
  mpMode = true;
  mpPlayers = [];
  for (let i=0;i<mpCount;i++) {
    const nm = (document.getElementById('mpN'+i)||{}).value || ('J'+(i+1));
    mpPlayers.push({name:nm.trim()||'J'+(i+1), hand:[], score:0, totalScore:0});
  }
  mpCurrent = 0; mpDirection = 1;
  mpAccumDraw = 0; mpAccumType = null;
  mpSilenceOn = false;
  startShuffle();
}

  renderRecordsModal();

function switchRecTab(tab, targetEl) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.mtab').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const panel = document.getElementById('recTab-'+tab);
  if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
  const btn = targetEl || (typeof event !== 'undefined' && event.target);
  if (btn && btn.classList) btn.classList.add('active');
  // Render on demand
  if (tab === 'achiev' && typeof renderAchievTab === 'function') renderAchievTab();
  else if (tab === 'stats' && typeof renderStatsExtTab === 'function') renderStatsExtTab();
}

function renderRecordsModal() {
  renderScoresTab();
  renderStatsTab();
  renderCardsTab();
  if (typeof renderAchievTab === 'function') renderAchievTab();
  if (typeof renderStatsExtTab === 'function') renderStatsExtTab();
}

function renderScoresTab() {
  const scores = loadScores();
  const el = document.getElementById('recTab-scores');
  if (!scores.length) { el.innerHTML='<div class="rec-empty">Aún no hay récords.<br>¡Juega tu primera partida!</div>'; return; }
  const diffLabel = {facil:'😊 Fácil',normal:'🙂 Normal',dificil:'😤 Difícil',experto:'💀 Experto',multi:'👥 Multi'};
  const medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉'];
  let html = '<table class="rec-table"><tr><th>#</th><th>Jugador</th><th>Puntos</th><th>Dif.</th><th>Modo</th><th>Tiempo</th></tr>';
  scores.slice(0,15).forEach((s,i)=>{
    const medal = medals[i]||'';
    html += `<tr>
      <td class="rec-rank">${medal||'#'+(i+1)}</td>
      <td>${s.name||'Jugador'}</td>
      <td style="color:var(--gold);font-weight:700">${s.score}</td>
      <td>${diffLabel[s.diff]||s.diff}</td>
      <td>${s.mode||'—'}</td>
      <td>${s.time||'—'}</td>
    </tr>`;
  });
  html += '</table>';
  html += `<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:12px;">
    <button class="mbtn-sm mbtn-gold" onclick="exportScores()">📤 Exportar</button>
    <button class="mbtn-sm" style="background:rgba(200,50,50,.3);color:#ff9999;padding:8px 14px;border-radius:20px;border:none;cursor:pointer;font-size:.8rem;" onclick="clearScores()">🗑️ Borrar</button>
  </div>`;
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderStatsTab() {
  const st = loadStats();
  const el = document.getElementById('recTab-stats');
  const winRate = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.wins/st.totalGames*100) : 0;
  const avgTime = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.totalTime/st.totalGames) : 0;
  const avgTurns= st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.totalTurns/st.totalGames) : 0;
  const fmt = s => s>=60 ? Math.floor(s/60)+'m '+Math.round(s%60)+'s' : s+'s';
  const diffs = [
    {k:'facil',  label:'Fácil',   color:'#4CAF50'},
    {k:'normal', label:'Normal',  color:'#2196F3'},
    {k:'dificil',label:'Difícil', color:'#FF9800'},
    {k:'experto',label:'Experto', color:'#f44336'},
  ];
  let html = `<div class="stat-grid">
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${st.totalGames}</div><div class="sl">Partidas</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${winRate}%</div><div class="sl">Victorias</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${fmt(avgTime)}</div><div class="sl">Tiempo promedio</div></div>
    <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${avgTurns}</div><div class="sl">Turnos promedio</div></div>
  </div>
  <div class="chart-title">Victorias por dificultad</div>
  <div class="chart-wrap">`;
  diffs.forEach(d=>{
    const played = st.gamesPlayed[d.k]||0;
    const won    = st.winsByDiff[d.k]||0;
    const pct    = played>0 ? Math.round(won/played*100) : 0;
    html += `<div class="stat-row">
      <span class="stat-lbl">${d.label}</span>
      <div class="stat-bar-wrap"><div class="stat-bar" style="width:${pct}%;background:${d.color};"></div></div>
      <span class="stat-val">${pct}%</span>
    </div>`;
  });
  html += `</div>
  <div style="font-size:.72rem;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);text-align:center;margin-top:6px;">
    ✅ ${st.wins} victorias · ❌ ${st.losses} derrotas · 🃏 ${st.specialsPlayed} especiales
  </div>`;
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function renderCardsTab() {
  const st = loadStats();
  const el = document.getElementById('recTab-cards');
  const freq = st.cardFreq||{};
  const sorted = Object.entries(freq).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,12);
  if (!sorted.length) { el.innerHTML='<div class="rec-empty">Sin datos todavía.<br>¡Juega para generar estadísticas!</div>'; return; }
  const total = Object.values(freq).reduce((a,b)=>a+b,0)||1;
  const valEmoji = {A:'🅰️','2':'2️⃣','3':'3️⃣','7':'🤫','8':'🎴','10':'🔄',J:'🔁',K:'👑',Q:'👸'};
  let html = '<div class="chart-title">Cartas más jugadas</div><div class="card-freq">';
  sorted.forEach(([k,v])=>{
    const [val,suit]=k.split('_');
    const emo = valEmoji[val]||'🃏';
    html += `<div class="cf-item"><span class="cf-pip">${emo}</span>${val}${suit||''}<span class="cf-ct">×${v}</span></div>`;
  });
  html += '</div><div class="chart-title" style="margin-top:10px">Distribución de valores</div><div>';
  const vals = ['A','2','3','7','8','10','J','Q','K'];
  vals.forEach(v=>{
    const cnt = SUITS.reduce((s,suit)=>s+(freq[v+'_'+suit]||0),0);
    const pct = Math.round(cnt/total*100);
    html += `<div class="stat-row">
      <span class="stat-lbl" style="font-size:.68rem">${valEmoji[v]||v}</span>
      <div class="stat-bar-wrap"><div class="stat-bar" style="width:${pct}%;background:rgba(240,192,64,.7);"></div></div>
      <span class="stat-val">${cnt}</span>
    </div>`;
  });
  html += '</div>';
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

function exportScores() {
  const s = JSON.stringify(loadScores(), null, 2);
  const a = document.createElement('a');
  a.href = 'data:application/json;charset=utf-8,'+encodeURIComponent(s);
  a.download = 'ocho_locos_records.json'; a.click();
}
function clearScores() {
  if (confirm('¿Borrar todos los récords?')) {
    localStorage.removeItem(LS_SCORES);
    renderRecordsModal();
  }
}

/* Points burst animation */
function showPointsBurst(pts, x, y) {
  const el = document.createElement('div');
  el.className='pts-burst';
  el.textContent = '+'+pts+' pts';
  el.style.left = x+'px'; el.style.top = y+'px';
  document.body.appendChild(el);
  setTimeout(()=>el.remove(), 1600);
}

/* Toast */
let _toastT = null;
function showToast(msg, dur=2200) {
  const t = document.getElementById('toast');
  t.textContent = msg; t.classList.add('show');
  if (_toastT) clearTimeout(_toastT);
  _toastT = setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), dur);
}

/* ══ MENÚ ══ */
function buildBg() {
  const c = document.getElementById('bgCards'); c.innerHTML='';
  for (let i=0;i<18;i++) {
    const d = document.createElement('div'); d.className='fc';
    d.style.cssText=`left:${Math.random()*100}%;top:${Math.random()*100}%;
      --r:${Math.random()*50-25}deg;animation-delay:${Math.random()*5}s;
      animation-duration:${5+Math.random()*6}s;`;
    c.appendChild(d);
  }
}

function buildMenuDeck() {
  const d = document.getElementById('menuDeck'); d.innerHTML='';
  [{s:'♥',v:'A'},{s:'♠',v:'K'},{s:'♦',v:'8'},{s:'♣',v:'Q'},{s:'♥',v:'J'}]
  .forEach((c,i)=>{
    const el = buildCard(c,false,-1);
    el.style.cssText+=`;transform:rotate(${(i-2)*7}deg);z-index:${i};--rot:${(i-2)*7}deg;cursor:default!important;`;
    el.classList.remove('playable');
    d.appendChild(el);
  });
}
