function closeRules() { document.getElementById('rulesModal').classList.remove('open'); }

function showMenu() {
  // App nav: hide game screen, show home screen
  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('homeScreen').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('bottomNav').style.display = 'flex';
  document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.getElementById('bnav-home').classList.add('active');
  renderMenuStats();
  // original showMenu continues:

  stopGameMusic();
  mpMode = false;
  gameOver = true;
  selectedIndices = [];
  tournamentScore = {player:0, ai:0};
  tournamentGames = 0;
  document.getElementById('tournHud').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('resultScreen').classList.remove('show');
  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('homeScreen').classList.remove('hidden');
  buildBg(); buildMenuDeck();
  setTimeout(startMenuMusic, 400);
}

/* Botón "Jugar de nuevo" desde resultado */
function restartGame() {
  /* En torneo: si volvemos a jugar, reiniciar score */
  tournamentScore = {player:0, ai:0};
  tournamentGames = 0;
  startShuffle();
}

/* ══ ANIMACIÓN BARAJADO ══ */
async function startShuffle() {
  // App: switch to game screen
  document.getElementById('homeScreen').classList.remove('active');
  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.add('active');
  document.getElementById('bottomNav').style.display = 'none';

  stopMenuMusic();
  document.getElementById('homeScreen').classList.add('hidden');
  document.getElementById('resultScreen').classList.remove('show');
  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.add('hidden');
  const ss = document.getElementById('shuffleScreen');
  ss.classList.add('show');
  playSound('shuffle', 0.9);
  await runShuffleAnimation();
  // Fade out shuffle screen smoothly
  ss.classList.add('hiding');
  await wait(420);
  ss.classList.remove('show','hiding');
  await wait(80);
  await startGame();
  setTimeout(startGameMusic, 600);
}

async function runShuffleAnimation() {
  const canvas = document.getElementById('shuffleCanvas');
  canvas.innerHTML = '';
  const total = 26, cards = [];
  for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
    const el = document.createElement('div'); el.className='sh-card';
    const cx = canvas.offsetWidth/2-28, cy = canvas.offsetHeight/2-41;
    el.style.cssText=`left:${cx}px;top:${cy}px;transform:rotate(0deg);transition:none;`;
    canvas.appendChild(el); cards.push(el);
  }
  await wait(80);
  const lX=canvas.offsetWidth/2-80, rX=canvas.offsetWidth/2+24, mY=canvas.offsetHeight/2-41;
  for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
    const side=i%2===0, off=(Math.floor(i/2))*1.2, rot=(Math.random()-.5)*6;
    cards[i].style.transition=`all ${0.18+Math.random()*.08}s ease-out`;
    cards[i].style.left=(side?lX:rX)+'px';
    cards[i].style.top=(mY-off)+'px';
    cards[i].style.transform=`rotate(${rot}deg)`;
    await wait(28);
  }
  await wait(350);
  for (let pass=0;pass<3;pass++) {
    const cx2=canvas.offsetWidth/2-28; let del=0;
    for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
      const t=del;
      setTimeout(()=>{
        cards[i].style.transition='all .11s cubic-bezier(.22,.61,.36,1)';
        cards[i].style.left=cx2+'px';
        cards[i].style.top=(mY-i*1.4)+'px';
        cards[i].style.transform=`rotate(${(Math.random()-.5)*4}deg)`;
      },t);
      del+=26;
    }
    await wait(del+250);
    if (pass<2) {
      for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
        cards[i].style.transition='all .14s ease-in-out';
        cards[i].style.left=(i%2===0?lX:rX)+'px';
        cards[i].style.top=(mY-(Math.floor(i/2))*1.2)+'px';
        await wait(22);
      }
      await wait(300);
    }
  }
  for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
    cards[i].style.transition='all .09s ease-in';
    cards[i].style.left=(canvas.offsetWidth/2-28)+'px';
    cards[i].style.top=(mY-i*.7)+'px';
    cards[i].style.transform=`rotate(${(Math.random()-.5)*1.5}deg)`;
  }
  await wait(350);
  for (let i=0;i<total;i++) {
    cards[i].style.transition='all .25s ease-in';
    cards[i].style.transform=`rotate(${(Math.random()-.5)*28}deg) scale(0)`;
    cards[i].style.opacity='0';
    await wait(12);
  }
  await wait(350);
}

/* ══ INICIO DE PARTIDA ══ */
async function startGame() {
  // Reiniciar estado
  deck=[]; player=[]; ai=[]; discard=[];
  turns=0; pDraws=0; aiDraws=0; drawnThisTurn=0;
  playerTurn=false; gameOver=false;
  selectedIndices=[]; firstCardIsEight=false;

  // Mostrar pantalla
  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.remove('hidden');
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('drawInfo').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('suitInd').style.display  = 'none';

  const mode = MODES[currentMode];
  document.getElementById('modeBadge').textContent = mode.icon + ' ' + mode.name;
  // Actualizar badge de dificultad en pantalla de juego
  const dConf = DIFFICULTIES[currentDiff];
  const dEl   = document.getElementById('diffBadge');
  dEl.textContent = dConf.label;
  dEl.className   = dConf.cssClass;

  // Construir mazo(s)
  const numDecks = (currentMode === 'torneo') ? 2 : 1;
  for (let d=0; d<numDecks; d++)
    for (const s of SUITS) for (const v of VALS) deck.push({s,v});
  deck.sort(() => Math.random() - .5);
  gameStartTime = Date.now();
  // Reset accum state
  mpAccumDraw=0; mpAccumType=null; mpSilenceOn=false;

  // ─── Repartir cartas ───
  setStatus('Repartiendo cartas...');
  if (mpMode) {
    // Multiplayer: repartir a todos los jugadores
    mpPlayers.forEach(p => p.hand = []);
    for (let i=0; i<mode.cards; i++) {
      for (let pi=0; pi<mpPlayers.length; pi++) {
        mpPlayers[pi].hand.push(deck.pop());
        playSound('deal', 0.5);
        await wait(60);
      }
    }
    // Asignar referencias: player = mano del jugador activo, ai = mano del siguiente
    player = mpPlayers[0].hand;
    ai     = mpPlayers[1] ? mpPlayers[1].hand : [];
    document.getElementById('mpScoreBar').style.display = 'flex';
    document.getElementById('diffBadge').style.display  = 'none';
    document.getElementById('opponentLabel').textContent = '👥 ' + (mpPlayers[1]?.name||'J2');
    updateMpScoreBar();
  } else {
    // VS IA clásico – animación de reparto con vuelo de cartas
    for (let i=0; i<mode.cards; i++) {
      player.push(deck.pop());
      renderHands();
      playSound('deal', 0.55);
      animDealCard('player');   // lanza carta visual volando
      await wait(120);
      ai.push(deck.pop());
      renderHands();
      playSound('deal', 0.50);
      animDealCard('ai');
      await wait(120);
    }
    document.getElementById('mpScoreBar').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('diffBadge').style.display  = '';
    document.getElementById('opponentLabel').textContent = '🤖 Inteligencia Artificial';
  }

  // ─── Primera carta del descarte (nunca un 8) ───
  let first;
  do { first = deck.pop(); } while (first.v === '8');
  discard.push(first);
  currentSuit = first.s;
  playSound('place', 0.75);

  // ─── Torneo HUD ───
  if (currentMode === 'torneo') {
    tournamentGames++;
    document.getElementById('tournHud').style.display = 'block';
    updateTournHud();
  }

  playerTurn = true;
  drawnThisTurn = 0;
  setStatus('¡Tu turno! Selecciona carta(s) válida(s)');
  updateUI();
  updateDrawBtn();
}

function updateTournHud() {
  document.getElementById('tournHud').textContent =
    `🏆 Torneo · Partida ${tournamentGames}/3 · Tú: ${tournamentScore.player} — IA: ${tournamentScore.ai}`;
}

/* ══ RENDERS SEPARADOS ══ */

/* Renderiza SOLO las manos sin necesitar discard válido */
function renderHands() {
  if (mpMode) {
    // In multiplayer, show current player's hand as 'player' hand
    player = mpPlayers[mpCurrent]?.hand || player;
    ai     = mpPlayers[(mpCurrent+mpDirection+mpPlayers.length)%mpPlayers.length]?.hand || ai;
  }
  const aiA = document.getElementById('aiArea'); aiA.innerHTML='';
  ai.forEach(() => aiA.appendChild(buildBack()));
  const pA = document.getElementById('playerArea'); pA.innerHTML='';
  player.forEach((c,i) => {
    const el = buildCardSimple(c, i);
    pA.appendChild(el);
  });
  document.getElementById('aiCount').innerText  = ai.length + ' cartas';
  document.getElementById('pCount').innerText   = player.length + ' cartas';
  document.getElementById('deckCount').textContent = deck.length + ' en mazo';
}

/* Carta SIN lógica de jugabilidad (usada durante reparto) */
function buildCardSimple(card, idx) {
  const el = document.createElement('div');
  const suitClass = card.s==='♠' ? 'spade-card' : card.s==='♣' ? 'club-card' : (REDS.has(card.s)?'red-card':'black-card');
  el.className = 'card ' + suitClass + (REDS.has(card.s) ? ' red-card' : ' black-card');
  el.style.zIndex = idx + 1;
  const color = REDS.has(card.s) ? 'color:var(--red)' : 'color:var(--black)';
  el.innerHTML = `
    <div class="ci tl" style="${color}"><span class="cv">${card.v}</span><span class="cs">${card.s}</span></div>
    <div class="ci br" style="${color}"><span class="cv">${card.v}</span><span class="cs">${card.s}</span></div>`;
  const cc = document.createElement('div');
  cc.className = 'cc'; cc.style.cssText = color;
  if (FACES[card.v]) {
    const f = FACES[card.v];
    cc.innerHTML=`<div class="face-inner" style="${color}">
      <div class="face-top">${f.top}&nbsp;${card.s}</div>
      <div class="face-emoji">${f.emoji}</div>
      <div class="face-bot">${f.top}&nbsp;${card.s}</div></div>`;
  } else { cc.innerHTML = buildPips(card.v, card.s, color); }
  el.appendChild(cc);
  return el;
}

/* ══ UI COMPLETA (solo cuando hay descarte) ══ */
function updateUI() {
  // IA
  const aiA = document.getElementById('aiArea'); aiA.innerHTML='';
  ai.forEach(() => aiA.appendChild(buildBack()));
  // Jugador con lógica de jugabilidad
  const pA = document.getElementById('playerArea'); pA.innerHTML='';
  player.forEach((c,i) => pA.appendChild(buildCard(c, true, i)));
  // Descarte
  const dz = document.getElementById('discardZone'); dz.innerHTML='';
  if (discard.length > 0) dz.appendChild(buildCard(discard[discard.length-1], false, -1));
  // Refresh preview
  if (typeof updateSelectedPreview === 'function') updateSelectedPreview();
  // Palo indicador
  const si = document.getElementById('suitInd');
  if (discard.length > 0 && discard[discard.length-1].v === '8') {
    si.style.display = 'block';
    si.innerHTML = `Palo activo: <strong>${currentSuit}</strong>`;
  } else { si.style.display = 'none'; }
  document.getElementById('aiCount').innerText  = ai.length + ' cartas';
  document.getElementById('pCount').innerText   = player.length + ' cartas';
  document.getElementById('deckCount').textContent = deck.length + ' en mazo';
  updatePlayBtn();
  if (playerTurn && !gameOver) updateDrawBtn();
}

/* ══ LÓGICA DE JUGABILIDAD ══ */
/* *** BUG FIX: guardia para discard vacío *** */
function isPlayable(card) {
  if (!discard.length) return false;                      // ← FIX CRÍTICO
  if (firstCardIsEight && discard.length === 1) return true;
  const top = discard[discard.length-1];
  return card.v === '8' || card.s === currentSuit || card.v === top.v;
}

function hasPlayableCard() {
  if (!discard.length) return false;
  if (firstCardIsEight && discard.length === 1) return true;
  const top = discard[discard.length-1];
  return player.some(c => c.v==='8' || c.s===currentSuit || c.v===top.v);
}

function updateDrawBtn() {
  const mode = MODES[currentMode];
  const canDraw = playerTurn && !gameOver && deck.length>0
    && !hasPlayableCard() && drawnThisTurn < mode.maxDraw;
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = !canDraw;
  const di = document.getElementById('drawInfo');
  if (playerTurn && !gameOver) {
    if (hasPlayableCard()) {
      di.style.display = 'none';
      document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
    } else {
      di.style.display = 'block';
      if (drawnThisTurn >= mode.maxDraw || deck.length === 0) {
        di.textContent = `Robaste ${drawnThisTurn}/${mode.maxDraw} — Debes pasar`;
        document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        di.textContent = `Robadas: ${drawnThisTurn}/${mode.maxDraw}`;
        document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
      }
    }
  } else {
    di.style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
  }
}

/* ══ SELECCIÓN DE CARTAS ══ */
function toggleCardSelect(idx) {
  if (!playerTurn || gameOver) return;
  const card = player[idx];
  if (selectedIndices.includes(idx)) {
    selectedIndices = selectedIndices.filter(i => i !== idx);
    updateUI(); updatePlayBtn(); updateSelectedPreview(); return;
  }
  if (selectedIndices.length === 0) {
    if (!isPlayable(card)) {
      showToast('⚠️ Carta no válida para jugar');
      shakeCard(idx);
      return;
    }
    selectedIndices = [idx];
    updateUI(); updatePlayBtn(); updateSelectedPreview(); return;
  }
  const firstCard = player[selectedIndices[0]];
  if (card.v === firstCard.v) {
    selectedIndices.push(idx);
    updateUI(); updatePlayBtn(); updateSelectedPreview();
  } else {
    showToast('Solo puedes combinar cartas del mismo valor 🃏');
    shakeCard(idx);
  }
}

function shakeCard(idx) {
  try {
    const cards = document.querySelectorAll('#playerArea .card');
    if (cards[idx]) {
      cards[idx].style.animation = 'cardShake .35s ease';
      setTimeout(() => { if(cards[idx]) cards[idx].style.animation = ''; }, 400);
    }
  } catch(e) {}
}

function updateSelectedPreview() {
  const zone  = document.getElementById('playZone');
  const slot  = document.getElementById('pzSlot');
  if (!zone || !slot) return;

  slot.innerHTML = '';
  if (selectedIndices.length === 0) {
    zone.classList.remove('active');
    return;
  }
  zone.classList.add('active');

  // Label above cards
  const lbl = document.createElement('div');
  lbl.className = 'pz-label';
  lbl.textContent = selectedIndices.length > 1
    ? selectedIndices.length + ' CARTAS LISTAS'
    : 'CARTA LISTA';
  slot.appendChild(lbl);

  // Show selected cards in the zone
  selectedIndices.forEach(i => {
    const c = player[i];
    const clone = buildCard(c, false, -1);
    clone.classList.add('pz-card');
    clone.onclick = () => playSelected();
    slot.appendChild(clone);
  });
}

function updatePlayBtn() {
  const pb = document.getElementById('playBtn');
  if (selectedIndices.length > 0) {
    pb.style.display = 'block';
    pb.textContent = selectedIndices.length > 1
      ? `▶ Jugar ${selectedIndices.length} cartas`
      : '▶ Jugar';
  } else { pb.style.display = 'none'; }
}

/* ══ JUGAR CARTAS ══ */
function playSelected() {
  if (!playerTurn || gameOver || selectedIndices.length === 0) return;
  const indices = [...selectedIndices].sort((a,b) => b-a);
  const cards   = selectedIndices.map(i => player[i]);
  if (!isPlayable(cards[0])) { showToast('⚠️ Carta no válida'); selectedIndices=[]; updateUI(); return; }
  // Clear playZone
  const pzone = document.getElementById('playZone');
  const pslot = document.getElementById('pzSlot');
  if (pzone) pzone.classList.remove('active');
  if (pslot) pslot.innerHTML='';
  if (cards.some(c => c.v==='8') && cards.length > 1) {
    showToast('El Ocho Loco se juega solo 🎴'); return;
  }
  // Remover del array (índices desc para no alterar posiciones)
  indices.forEach(i => player.splice(i,1));
  selectedIndices = [];

  if (cards.length === 1 && cards[0].v === '8') {
    playSound('wildcard', 0.9);  // 🎴 Sonido comodín al jugar el 8
    pendingSuit = (suit) => {
      currentSuit = suit; firstCardIsEight = false;
      cards.forEach(c => discard.push(c));
      playSound('colorChange', 1.0);  // 🎨 Sonido al elegir palo
      setStatus(`¡Ocho Loco! Palo elegido: ${suit}`);
      updateUI(); if (checkWin()) return;
      endPlayerTurn();
    };
    document.getElementById('suitPicker').classList.add('open');
    return;
  }

  // Cartas normales
  firstCardIsEight = false;
  const lastCard = cards[cards.length-1];
  // Track card frequency
  const st2 = loadStats();
  cards.forEach(c => {
    const k=c.v+'_'+c.s; st2.cardFreq[k]=(st2.cardFreq[k]||0)+1;
    if (['A','2','3','7','10','J'].includes(c.v)) st2.specialsPlayed++;
  });
  saveStats(st2);

  const isSpecial = ['2','A','J','3','10'].includes(lastCard.v);
  playSound(isSpecial?'aiSpecial':'place', isSpecial?0.95:0.8);
  cards.forEach(c => discard.push(c));
  currentSuit = lastCard.s;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').style.display = 'none';
  turns++;
  if (cards.length > 1) { showToast(`¡Jugada múltiple! ${cards.length} cartas 🔥`, 2000); sfxCombo(cards.length); }

  updateUI(); if (checkWin()) return;

  // Carta A: acumulado +3
  if (lastCard.v === 'A') {
    if (mpAccumType === 'A' || mpAccumType === null) {
      mpAccumType = 'A'; mpAccumDraw += 3;
    }
    setStatus(`¡AS! IA debe responder o robar ${mpAccumDraw} cartas`);
    updateUI(); endPlayerTurn(); return;
  }
  // Carta 2: acumulado +2
  if (lastCard.v === '2') {
    if (mpAccumType === '2' || mpAccumType === null) {
      mpAccumType='2'; mpAccumDraw+=2;
    }
    setStatus(`¡2! IA debe responder o robar ${mpAccumDraw} cartas`);
    updateUI(); endPlayerTurn(); return;
  }
  // Carta 3: salta turno IA
  if (lastCard.v === '3') {
    applyThree();
    setStatus('3️⃣ ¡IA pierde turno! Vuelves a jugar');
    setTimeout(()=>{ startPlayerTurn(); }, 1400); return;
  }
  // Carta 7: silencio
  if (lastCard.v === '7') {
    activateSilence();
    endPlayerTurn(); return;
  }
  // Carta 10: invierte dirección
  if (lastCard.v === '10') {
    applyTen(true);
    setStatus('🔄 ¡Dirección invertida! Vuelves a jugar');
    setTimeout(()=>{ startPlayerTurn(); }, 1400); return;
  }
  // Carta J: repite turno (juega otra del mismo palo)
  if (lastCard.v === 'J') {
    setStatus('J: ¡Repites turno! Juega otra carta del mismo palo');
    setTimeout(()=>{ startPlayerTurn(); }, 1200); return;
  }
  endPlayerTurn();
}

function updateMpScoreBar() {
  if (!mpMode) return;
  const bar = document.getElementById('mpScoreBar');
  bar.innerHTML = mpPlayers.map((p,i)=>
    `<div class="mp-score-pill ${i===mpCurrent?'active':''}">${p.name}: ${p.totalScore} pts</div>`
  ).join('');
}

function endPlayerTurn() {
  playerTurn = false; drawnThisTurn = 0;
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('drawInfo').style.display = 'none';
  setStatus('IA pensando...');
  setTimeout(aiTurn, 1000);
}

function startPlayerTurn() {
  playerTurn = true; drawnThisTurn = 0;
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = false;
  updateDrawBtn();
  setStatus('¡Tu turno! Selecciona carta(s)');
}

/* ══ ROBAR CARTA ══ */
function drawCard() {
  if (!playerTurn || gameOver) return;
  const mode = MODES[currentMode];
  // If there's an active accumulation (A or 2 chain), player draws all and resets
  if (mpAccumType && mpAccumDraw > 0) {
    const n = mpAccumDraw;
    for(let i=0;i<n;i++) if(deck.length>0){player.push(deck.pop());pDraws++;}
    mpAccumDraw=0; mpAccumType=null;
    playSound('draw',0.85); updateUI();
    showToast(`😱 Robaste ${n} cartas del acumulado!`, 2500);
    endPlayerTurn(); return;
  }
  if (hasPlayableCard()) { showToast('Tienes cartas jugables 🃏'); return; }
  if (drawnThisTurn >= mode.maxDraw) { showToast(`Máximo ${mode.maxDraw} robo(s) por turno`); return; }
  if (deck.length === 0) { setStatus('¡Mazo vacío!'); return; }
  player.push(deck.pop()); pDraws++; drawnThisTurn++;
  playSound('draw', 0.8);
  updateUI();
  if (hasPlayableCard()) {
    setStatus('¡Carta jugable! Selecciónala o sigue robando');
  } else {
    setStatus(`Robaste ${drawnThisTurn}/${mode.maxDraw}. ${drawnThisTurn>=mode.maxDraw||deck.length===0?'¡Debes pasar!':'Sigue robando o pasa'}`);
  }
  updateDrawBtn();
}

/* ══ PASAR TURNO ══ */
function passTurn() {
  if (!playerTurn || gameOver) return;
  const mode = MODES[currentMode];
  if (drawnThisTurn < mode.maxDraw && deck.length > 0 && !hasPlayableCard()) {
    showToast(`Aún puedes robar (${drawnThisTurn}/${mode.maxDraw})`); return;
  }
  showToast('Turno pasado ⏭', 1500);
  selectedIndices = [];
  endPlayerTurn();
}

function chooseSuit(s) {
  document.getElementById('suitPicker').classList.remove('open');
  if (pendingSuit) { pendingSuit(s); pendingSuit = null; }
}

/* ══ TURNO DE IA ══ */
/* ══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MOTOR DE IA — 4 NIVELES DE DIFICULTAD
══════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* Cartas jugables por la IA en este momento */
function aiGetPlayable() {
  const top = discard[discard.length-1];
  return ai.map((c,i)=>({c,i})).filter(({c}) =>
    c.v==='8' || c.s===currentSuit || c.v===top.v
  );
}

/* Cuántas cartas del jugador son jugables con un palo dado */
function playerPlayableCount(suit) {
  const top = discard[discard.length-1];
  return player.filter(c => c.v==='8' || c.s===suit || c.v===top.v).length;
}

/* Elige el palo óptimo para un 8 */
function aiChooseSuit(diff) {
  if (!diff.suitSmarts) return SUITS[Math.floor(Math.random()*SUITS.length)];
  const cnt = {}; SUITS.forEach(s => cnt[s]=0);
  ai.forEach(c => { if (c.v!=='8') cnt[c.s]++; });
  if (diff.lookAhead >= 1) {  // Difícil/Experto: lookahead heurística
    const scored = SUITS.map(s => ({s, score: cnt[s]*3 - playerPlayableCount(s)}));
    scored.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);
    return scored[0].s;
  }
  return SUITS.reduce((a,b)=>cnt[a]>=cnt[b]?a:b);
}

/* Ordena las cartas jugables por prioridad según nivel */
function aiCardPriority(diff, playable) {
  if (diff.aiLevel <= 1) return [...playable].sort(()=>Math.random()-0.48);

  if (diff.aiLevel === 2) {
    const prio=['2','J','Q','K','A','10','9','7','6','5','4','3','8'];
    return [...playable].sort((a,b)=>{
      const ia=prio.indexOf(a.c.v); const ib=prio.indexOf(b.c.v);
      return (ia<0?99:ia)-(ib<0?99:ib);
    });
  }

  if (diff.aiLevel === 3) {
    const prio=['2','J','Q','A','K','10','9','7','6','5','4','3','8'];
    const sorted=[...playable].sort((a,b)=>{
      const ia=prio.indexOf(a.c.v); const ib=prio.indexOf(b.c.v);
      return (ia<0?99:ia)-(ib<0?99:ib);
    });
    if (diff.cardSave8 && sorted.length>1) {
      const non8=sorted.filter(x=>x.c.v!=='8');
      if (non8.length) return non8.concat(sorted.filter(x=>x.c.v==='8'));
    }
    return sorted;
  }

  // EXPERTO (aiLevel 4): heurística de puntuación
  const scored = playable.map(({c,i})=>{
    let score = 0;
    if (c.v==='2') score+=30;
    if (c.v==='J'||c.v==='Q') score+=22;
    score += (20-ai.length)*1.5;
    if (c.v!=='8') {
      const adv=player.filter(p=>p.s===c.s).length;
      score -= adv*4;
    }
    if (c.v==='8'&&ai.length>3) score-=18;
    const sameVal=ai.filter(x=>x.v===c.v&&x.v!=='8').length;
    if (sameVal>=2) score+=sameVal*5;
    return {c,i,score};
  });
  scored.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);
  return scored;
}

function aiTurn() {
  if (gameOver) return;
  const diff = DIFFICULTIES[currentDiff];
  const mode = MODES[currentMode];
  const playable = aiGetPlayable();

  // Fácil: a veces roba aunque tenga carta válida (torpeza)
  // Fácil: IA "olvida" que tiene carta y roba de todas formas
  if (diff.drawEarly>0 && playable.length>0 && Math.random()<diff.drawEarly) {
    if (deck.length>0) {
      ai.push(deck.pop()); aiDraws++;
      playSound('draw',0.4); updateUI();
      setStatus('IA pensando...');
      setTimeout(()=>aiPlayCard(diff,mode), diff.thinkDelay);
      return;
    }
  }

  if (playable.length===0) {
    let drew=0, found=false;
    while (drew<mode.maxDraw && deck.length>0 && !found) {
      const drawn=deck.pop(); ai.push(drawn); aiDraws++; drew++;
      playSound('draw',0.45); updateUI();
      if (drawn.v==='8'||drawn.s===currentSuit||drawn.v===discard[discard.length-1].v) found=true;
      // Fácil: para de robar antes de agotar (torpeza)
      if (diff.aiLevel<=1 && drew>=1 && Math.random()<0.4) break;
    }
    const p2=aiGetPlayable();
    if (p2.length===0) {
      setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();setStatus('IA pasó. ¡Tu turno!');}, Math.round(diff.thinkDelay*0.5));
      return;
    }
    setTimeout(()=>aiPlayCard(diff,mode), Math.round(diff.thinkDelay*0.7));
    return;
  }

  setTimeout(()=>aiPlayCard(diff,mode), diff.thinkDelay);
}

function aiPlayCard(diff, mode) {
  const playable = aiGetPlayable();
  if (!playable.length) { startPlayerTurn(); setStatus('¡Tu turno!'); return; }

  // Jugadas múltiples (Difícil y Experto)
  if (diff.multiPlay) {
    const vcounts={};
    playable.forEach(({c})=>{ if(c.v!=='8') vcounts[c.v]=(vcounts[c.v]||0)+1; });
    const bv=Object.keys(vcounts)
      .filter(v=>vcounts[v]>=2)
      .sort((a,b)=>{
        const bonus=v=>['2','J','Q'].includes(v)?10:0;
        return (vcounts[b]+bonus(b))-(vcounts[a]+bonus(a));
      })[0];
    if (bv) {
      const multi=playable.filter(({c})=>c.v===bv);
      const idxs=multi.map(({i})=>i).sort((a,b)=>b-a);
      const cards=multi.map(({c})=>c);
      idxs.forEach(i=>ai.splice(i,1));
      cards.forEach(c=>discard.push(c));
      currentSuit=cards[cards.length-1].s;
      const last=cards[cards.length-1];
      (last.v==='2'||last.v==='J'||last.v==='Q')
        ? playSound('aiSpecial',0.85) : playSound('place',0.65);
      turns++;
      setStatus(`IA jugó ${cards.length}×${bv} 🃏`);
      updateUI(); if (checkWin()) return;
      if (last.v==='2') {
        for(let i=0;i<2;i++) if(deck.length>0) player.push(deck.pop());
        pDraws+=2; updateUI();
        setTimeout(()=>{setStatus('IA juega de nuevo…');setTimeout(aiTurn,800);},1200);
      } else if(last.v==='J'||last.v==='Q') {
        setTimeout(()=>{setStatus('IA juega de nuevo…');setTimeout(aiTurn,800);},1200);
      } else {
        setTimeout(()=>startPlayerTurn(),900);
      }
      return;
    }
  }

  // Bluff: a veces no usa la mejor carta (niveles bajos)
  const ranked = aiCardPriority(diff, playable);
  let chosen = ranked[0];
  if (diff.bluffRate>0 && ranked.length>1 && Math.random()<diff.bluffRate)
    chosen = ranked[Math.floor(Math.random()*Math.min(ranked.length,3))];

  const {c:card, i:idx} = chosen;
  ai.splice(idx,1);

  // Comodín 8
  if (card.v==='8') {
    currentSuit = aiChooseSuit(diff);
    discard.push(card);
    playSound('wildcard',0.75);
    setTimeout(()=>playSound('colorChange',0.85),350);
    setStatus(`IA: Ocho Loco → ${currentSuit}`);
    updateUI(); if(checkWin()) return;
    setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();setStatus('¡Tu turno!');},1100);
    return;
  }

  // Carta normal / especial
  discard.push(card); currentSuit=card.s;
  const isAiSpecial=['A','2','3','7','10','J'].includes(card.v);
  isAiSpecial ? playSound('aiSpecial',0.85) : playSound('place',0.6);
  turns++;
  updateUI(); if(checkWin()) return;

  if (card.v==='A') {
    if (mpAccumType==='A'||mpAccumType===null){mpAccumType='A';mpAccumDraw+=3;}
    setStatus(`¡IA juega AS! Debes responder o robar ${mpAccumDraw} cartas`);
    setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();},1300); return;
  }
  if (card.v==='2') {
    if (mpAccumType==='2'||mpAccumType===null){mpAccumType='2';mpAccumDraw+=2;}
    setStatus(`¡IA juega 2! Debes responder o robar ${mpAccumDraw} cartas`);
    setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();},1300); return;
  }
  if (card.v==='3') {
    applyThree(); setStatus('3️⃣ ¡IA salta TU turno! IA juega de nuevo…');
    setTimeout(()=>{setStatus('IA juega de nuevo…');setTimeout(aiTurn,800);},1300); return;
  }
  if (card.v==='7') {
    activateSilence(); setStatus('🤫 IA jugó el 7 — ¡SILENCIO!');
    setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();},1300); return;
  }
  if (card.v==='10') {
    applyTen(false); setStatus('🔄 IA invirtió la dirección');
    setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();},1300); return;
  }
  if (card.v==='J') {
    setStatus('¡IA repite turno con J!');
    setTimeout(()=>{setStatus('IA juega de nuevo…');setTimeout(aiTurn,800);},1300); return;
  }
  setTimeout(()=>{startPlayerTurn();setStatus('¡Tu turno! Selecciona carta(s)');},900);
}

/* ══ FIN DE PARTIDA ══ */
function checkWin() {
  if (player.length===0) { endGame(true);  return true; }
  if (ai.length===0)     { endGame(false); return true; }
  return false;
}

function endGame(playerWon) {
  gameOver = true;
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';

  // Record stats
  const timeSec = Math.round((Date.now()-gameStartTime)/1000);
  const st = loadStats();
  st.totalGames++;
  st.totalTime += timeSec;
  st.totalTurns += turns;
  if (!mpMode) {
    st.gamesPlayed[currentDiff] = (st.gamesPlayed[currentDiff]||0)+1;
    if (playerWon) { st.wins++; st.winsByDiff[currentDiff]=(st.winsByDiff[currentDiff]||0)+1; }
    else st.losses++;
  }
  saveStats(st);

  // Save score
  if (playerWon && !mpMode) {
    const score = calcScore(true, turns, pDraws, MODES[currentMode].cards, currentDiff, timeSec);
    const mins=Math.floor(timeSec/60), secs=timeSec%60;
    saveScore({
      name:'Jugador', score, diff:currentDiff, mode:MODES[currentMode].name,
      time: mins>0?`${mins}m ${secs}s`:`${secs}s`,
      date: new Date().toLocaleDateString('es')
    });
  }

  if (currentMode === 'torneo') {
    if (playerWon) tournamentScore.player++; else tournamentScore.ai++;
    updateTournHud();
    const done = tournamentScore.player >= 2 || tournamentScore.ai >= 2 || tournamentGames >= 3;
    if (!done) {
      const msg = playerWon ? '¡Ganaste esta partida! 🎉' : '¡IA ganó esta partida!';
      showToast(msg + ' → Siguiente en 3s...', 3000);
      setTimeout(() => {
        document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.add('hidden');
        startShuffle();
      }, 3100);
      return;
    }
    // Fin torneo
    showResult(tournamentScore.player > tournamentScore.ai, true);
  } else {
    showResult(playerWon, false);
  }
}

/* ══ PANTALLA DE RESULTADO ══ */
function showResult(win, isTournament=false) {
  gameOver = true;
  setTimeout(() => playSound(win?'victory':'defeat',1), 400);
  const cc = document.getElementById('ccc'); cc.innerHTML='';
  let icon, title, sub;
  if (isTournament) {
    icon  = win ? '🏆' : '💀';
    title = win ? '<span class="rt-win">¡CAMPEÓN!</span>' : '<span class="rt-lose">¡DERROTADO!</span>';
    sub   = win
      ? `¡Ganaste el torneo ${tournamentScore.player}-${tournamentScore.ai}! 👑`
      : `La IA dominó el torneo ${tournamentScore.ai}-${tournamentScore.player} 🤖`;
  } else {
    icon  = win ? '🏆' : '💀';
    title = win ? '<span class="rt-win">¡GANASTE!</span>' : '<span class="rt-lose">¡PERDISTE!</span>';
    sub   = win ? '¡Maestro de las cartas! 🎉' : 'La IA te superó esta vez... 🤖';
  }
  document.getElementById('resIcon').textContent    = icon;
  document.getElementById('resTitle').innerHTML     = title;
  document.getElementById('resSub').textContent     = sub;
  document.getElementById('resStats').innerHTML = `
    <div><div class="st-v">${turns}</div><div class="st-l">Turnos</div></div>
    <div><div class="st-v">${pDraws}</div><div class="st-l">Robaste</div></div>
    <div><div class="st-v">${win?ai.length:player.length}</div>
         <div class="st-l">${win?'Cartas IA':'Tus cartas'}</div></div>`;
  document.getElementById('resCard').className = 'res-card ' + (win?'rwin':'rlose');
  document.getElementById('resBackdrop').className = 'res-backdrop ' + (win?'res-win':'res-lose');
  if (win) {
    launchVictoryParticles(cc, isTournament);
  } else {
    launchDefeatParticles(cc);
  }
  if (isTournament) {
    tournamentScore={player:0,ai:0}; tournamentGames=0;
    document.getElementById('tournHud').style.display='none';
  }
  document.getElementById('resultScreen').classList.add('show');
}

/* ══ CARTAS REALISTAS ══ */
const FACES = {
  J:{top:'JACK', bot:'JACK', emoji:'🤴'},
  Q:{top:'QUEEN',bot:'QUEEN',emoji:'👸'},
  K:{top:'KING', bot:'KING', emoji:'👑'}
};

function buildCard(card, isPlayer, idx) {
  const el = document.createElement('div');
  const sc2 = card.s==='♠'?'spade-card':card.s==='♣'?'club-card':(REDS.has(card.s)?'red-card':'black-card');
  el.className = 'card ' + sc2 + (REDS.has(card.s)?' red-card':' black-card');
  el.style.zIndex = idx+1;
  const isSelected  = isPlayer && selectedIndices.includes(idx);
  const firstSel    = selectedIndices.length>0 ? player[selectedIndices[0]] : null;
  const canAdd      = isPlayer && idx>=0 && !isSelected && selectedIndices.length>0
                      && firstSel && card.v===firstSel.v;
  const playableCard= isPlayer && idx>=0 && isPlayable(card);
  if (isSelected)       el.classList.add('selected');
  else if (canAdd)      el.classList.add('can-add','playable');
  else if (playableCard)el.classList.add('playable');
  if (isPlayer && idx>=0) el.onclick = () => toggleCardSelect(idx);
  const color = REDS.has(card.s) ? 'color:var(--red)' : 'color:var(--black)';
  el.innerHTML=`
    <div class="ci tl" style="${color}"><span class="cv">${card.v}</span><span class="cs">${card.s}</span></div>
    <div class="ci br" style="${color}"><span class="cv">${card.v}</span><span class="cs">${card.s}</span></div>`;
  const cc = document.createElement('div'); cc.className='cc'; cc.style.cssText=color;
  if (FACES[card.v]) {
    const f=FACES[card.v];
    cc.innerHTML=`<div class="face-inner" style="${color}">
      <div class="face-top">${f.top}&nbsp;${card.s}</div>
      <div class="face-emoji">${f.emoji}</div>
      <div class="face-bot">${f.top}&nbsp;${card.s}</div></div>`;
  } else { cc.innerHTML=buildPips(card.v,card.s,color); }
  el.appendChild(cc);
  return el;
}

function buildPips(v,s,color){
  // Render spade and club with distinct emojis for clarity
  const displayS = s==='♠'?'♠':s==='♣'?'♣':s;
  const pip=(sz,r)=>`<i class="p p-${sz}" style="${color};${r?'transform:rotate(180deg)':''};font-style:normal;letter-spacing:0;">${displayS}</i>`;
  const lg=()=>pip('lg'),lgr=()=>pip('lg','r'),md=()=>pip('md'),mdr=()=>pip('md','r');
  const G=(cols,gap,...p)=>`<div class="pip-grid" style="grid-template-columns:${cols};gap:${gap};">${p.join('')}</div>`;
  const m={
    'A':`<i class="p p-xl" style="${color}">${s}</i>`,
    '2':G('1fr','16px 0',lg(),lgr()),
    '3':G('1fr','10px 0',lg(),lg(),lgr()),
    '4':G('1fr 1fr','9px 12px',lg(),lg(),lgr(),lgr()),
    '5':G('1fr 1fr','7px 12px',lg(),lg(),`<i class="p p-lg" style="${color};grid-column:1/-1;justify-self:center">${s}</i>`,lgr(),lgr()),
    '6':G('1fr 1fr','7px 12px',lg(),lg(),lg(),lgr(),lgr(),lgr()),
    '7':G('1fr 1fr','5px 12px',lg(),lg(),`<i class="p p-md" style="${color};grid-column:1/-1;justify-self:center">${s}</i>`,lg(),lg(),lgr(),lgr()),
    '8':G('1fr 1fr','4px 12px',md(),md(),md(),md(),mdr(),mdr(),mdr(),mdr()),
    '9':G('1fr 1fr','4px 11px',md(),md(),md(),md(),`<i class="p p-sm" style="${color};grid-column:1/-1;justify-self:center">${s}</i>`,mdr(),mdr(),mdr(),mdr()),
    '10':G('1fr 1fr','3px 10px',md(),md(),`<i class="p p-sm" style="${color};grid-column:1/-1;justify-self:center">${s}</i>`,md(),md(),mdr(),mdr(),`<i class="p p-sm" style="${color};grid-column:1/-1;justify-self:center;transform:rotate(180deg)">${s}</i>`,mdr(),mdr()),
  };
  return m[v]||`<i class="p p-lg" style="${color}">${s}</i>`;
}

function buildBack() {
  const el=document.createElement('div'); el.className='card-back'; return el;
}

function setStatus(m){ document.getElementById('statusBar').textContent=m; }
function wait(ms){ return new Promise(r=>setTimeout(r,ms)); }


/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   FUNCIONES ESPECIALES DE CARTAS – v8.0
   Corrige llamadas sin definición que rompían el flujo del juego
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/**
 * applyThree() – Carta 3: salta turno del oponente
 * En 1v1 vs IA: no-op (el flujo ya maneja el turno con startPlayerTurn/setTimeout(aiTurn))
 * En MP: avanza mpCurrent 2 posiciones (salta al siguiente jugador)
 */
function applyThree() {
  if (mpMode && mpPlayers.length > 0) {
    mpCurrent = (mpCurrent + mpDirection * 2 + mpPlayers.length) % mpPlayers.length;
    updateMpScoreBar();
  }
  // En modo 1v1: el caller ya hace startPlayerTurn() o setTimeout(aiTurn) según corresponda
}

/**
 * applyTen(isPlayer) – Carta 10: invierte dirección
 * isPlayer = true si fue el jugador quien jugó la carta; false si fue la IA
 * En 1v1 vs IA: no-op (el flujo maneja el turno externamente)
 * En MP: invierte mpDirection y avanza 1 en la nueva dirección
 */
function applyTen(isPlayer) {
  if (mpMode && mpPlayers.length > 0) {
    mpDirection *= -1;
    mpCurrent = (mpCurrent + mpDirection + mpPlayers.length) % mpPlayers.length;
    updateMpScoreBar();
  }
  // En modo 1v1: el caller decide quién juega con startPlayerTurn / setTimeout(aiTurn)
}

/**
 * activateSilence() – Carta 7: activa el modo silencio
 * En 1v1 vs IA: la IA roba 1 carta extra como penalización
 * En MP: activa mpSilenceOn por 8 segundos (el jugador activo no puede usar cartas especiales)
 */
function activateSilence() {
  if (mpMode) {
    mpSilenceOn = true;
    const silEl = document.getElementById('silenceIndicator');
    if (silEl) silEl.style.display = 'block';
    if (mpSilenceTimer) clearTimeout(mpSilenceTimer);
    mpSilenceTimer = setTimeout(() => {
      mpSilenceOn = false;
      mpSilenceTimer = null;
      const el2 = document.getElementById('silenceIndicator');
      if (el2) el2.style.display = 'none';
    }, 8000);
  } else {
    // Modo 1v1: la IA roba 1 carta penalización
    if (ai && ai.length < 25 && deck.length > 0) {
      ai.push(deck.pop());
    }
    updateUI();
  }
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   DRAG & DROP CON POINTER EVENTS API – v8.0
   Compatible con mouse y touch (iOS/Android/Desktop)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
(function() {
  let dragSrcEl  = null;   // elemento DOM de la carta arrastrada
  let dragCardIdx = -1;    // índice en el array player[]
  let ghostEl    = null;   // elemento fantasma que sigue al puntero
  let dragActive = false;
  let startX = 0, startY = 0;
  const DRAG_THRESHOLD = 8; // px mínimos para considerar arrastre

  function initDragOnCard(el, idx) {
    el.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => {
      if (!playerTurn || gameOver) return;
      startX = e.clientX; startY = e.clientY;
      dragSrcEl  = el;
      dragCardIdx = idx;
      dragActive = false;
      el.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId);
    }, { passive: true });

    el.addEventListener('pointermove', (e) => {
      if (dragSrcEl !== el) return;
      const dx = e.clientX - startX, dy = e.clientY - startY;
      if (!dragActive && Math.sqrt(dx*dx + dy*dy) < DRAG_THRESHOLD) return;

      if (!dragActive) {
        dragActive = true;
        el.classList.add('dragging-card');
        // Crear fantasma
        ghostEl = el.cloneNode(true);
        ghostEl.className = el.className + ' card-ghost';
        ghostEl.style.width  = el.offsetWidth  + 'px';
        ghostEl.style.height = el.offsetHeight + 'px';
        ghostEl.style.position = 'fixed';
        ghostEl.style.pointerEvents = 'none';
        ghostEl.style.zIndex = '9999';
        document.body.appendChild(ghostEl);
      }

      if (ghostEl) {
        ghostEl.style.left = (e.clientX - el.offsetWidth/2)  + 'px';
        ghostEl.style.top  = (e.clientY - el.offsetHeight/2) + 'px';
      }

      // Highlight drop zone si está sobre el descarte
      const discardEl = document.getElementById('discardPile');
      if (discardEl) {
        const r = discardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const over = e.clientX>=r.left && e.clientX<=r.right && e.clientY>=r.top && e.clientY<=r.bottom;
        discardEl.classList.toggle('drag-over', over);
      }
      e.preventDefault();
    }, { passive: false });

    el.addEventListener('pointerup', (e) => {
      if (dragSrcEl !== el) return;
      const wasActive = dragActive;
      cleanupDrag(el);

      if (!wasActive) {
        // Fue un tap: comportamiento original de selección
        toggleCardSelect(dragCardIdx);
        return;
      }

      // Fue un arrastre: verificar si cae sobre el descarte
      const discardEl = document.getElementById('discardPile');
      if (discardEl) {
        const r = discardEl.getBoundingClientRect();
        const over = e.clientX>=r.left && e.clientX<=r.right && e.clientY>=r.top && e.clientY<=r.bottom;
        discardEl.classList.remove('drag-over');
        if (over && playerTurn && !gameOver) {
          // Seleccionar la carta y jugarla
          if (!selectedIndices.includes(dragCardIdx)) {
            selectedIndices = [dragCardIdx];
            updateUI();
          }
          setTimeout(playSelected, 80);
        }
      }
    });

    el.addEventListener('pointercancel', () => cleanupDrag(el));
  }

  function cleanupDrag(el) {
    dragSrcEl  = null;
    dragActive = false;
    el.classList.remove('dragging-card');
    if (ghostEl) { ghostEl.remove(); ghostEl = null; }
    const discardEl = document.getElementById('discardPile');
    if (discardEl) discardEl.classList.remove('drag-over');
  }

  // Parchear renderHands para que cada carta del jugador sea "draggable"
  const _origBuildCard = window.buildCard;
  // Sobreescribir después de que el DOM esté listo
  window._addDragToPlayerCards = function() {
    const playerZone = document.getElementById('playerHand');
    if (!playerZone) return;
    const cards = playerZone.querySelectorAll('.card');
    cards.forEach((cardEl, i) => {
      initDragOnCard(cardEl, i);
    });
  };

  // Hookar renderHands: después de renderizar, aplicar drag
  const _origRenderInterval = setInterval(() => {
    if (typeof renderHands === 'function') {
      const _origRender = renderHands;
      window.renderHands = function() {
        _origRender.apply(this, arguments);
        setTimeout(window._addDragToPlayerCards, 50);
      };
      clearInterval(_origRenderInterval);
    }
  }, 200);
})();

/* ═══ UTILIDAD: showToast mejorado (si no existe) ═══ */
if (typeof showToast === 'undefined') {
  window.showToast = function(msg, duration) {
    let t = document.getElementById('toast');
    if (!t) {
      t = document.createElement('div');
      t.id = 'toast';
      document.body.appendChild(t);
    }
    t.textContent = msg;
    t.classList.add('show');
    clearTimeout(window._toastTimer);
    window._toastTimer = setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), duration || 2500);
  };
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   🏅 SISTEMA DE LOGROS Y ESTADÍSTICAS EXTENDIDAS — v19.0
   ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   • 42 logros en 6 categorías (Básicos, Rachas, Maestría, Modos, Gestas, Cartas)
   • Rareza: common | uncommon | rare | epic | legendary
   • Stats: rachas, winrate, récords, historial por modo/dificultad
   • Notificación emergente animada al desbloquear
   • Persistencia 100% en localStorage
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── Claves de almacenamiento ── */
const LS_ACHIEV    = 'ol_achiev_v14';
const LS_STATS_EXT = 'ol_statsext_v14';

/* ── Variables de sesión (se resetean al iniciar partida) ── */
let sessionMaxCombo    = 0;   // mayor combo de cartas jugadas de una vez
let sessionEightCount  = 0;   // ochos jugados esta partida
let sessionSpecialCount= 0;   // cartas especiales (A,2,3,7,8,10,J) jugadas
let sessionMaxHand     = 0;   // máximo de cartas en mano del jugador
let sessionCamebackFrom= 0;   // máx cartas en mano antes de ganar

/* ── Cargar / guardar logros ── */
function loadAchiev() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_ACHIEV)) || {}; } catch(e) { return {}; }
}
function saveAchiev(data) {
  localStorage.setItem(LS_ACHIEV, JSON.stringify(data));
}

/* ── Cargar / guardar stats extendidas ── */
function loadStatsExt() {
  const def = {
    currentStreak: 0, bestStreak: 0,
    currentLoseStreak: 0, worstLoseStreak: 0,
    hardStreakCurrent: 0,               // racha en dif. difícil/experto
    winsByMode:  { clasico:0, rapido:0, dificil:0, torneo:0, cooperativo:0, diario:0, practica:0 },
    gamesByMode: { clasico:0, rapido:0, dificil:0, torneo:0, cooperativo:0, diario:0, practica:0 },
    fastestWin: null,                   // segundos
    shortestWinTurns: null,             // turnos
    perfectWins: 0,                     // victorias sin robar
    comebackWins: 0,                    // victorias con 10+ cartas en mano
    revengeWins: 0,                     // victoria tras 3 derrotas seguidas
    biggestCombo: 0,                    // mayor combo en una jugada
    totalEights: 0,                     // ochos jugados históricamente
    totalSpecials: 0,                   // cartas especiales jugadas históricamente
    suitWins: { '♠':0, '♥':0, '♦':0, '♣':0 }, // victorias por palo activo
    tournamentWins: 0,
    multiplayerGames: 0,
    firstPlayDate: null,
    lastPlayDate: null,
  };
  try { return Object.assign({}, def, JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_STATS_EXT)) || {}); }
  catch(e) { return def; }
}
function saveStatsExt(data) {
  localStorage.setItem(LS_STATS_EXT, JSON.stringify(data));
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   COMPROBAR Y DESBLOQUEAR LOGROS
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function checkAchievements(gameData) {
  const unlocked = loadAchiev();
  const stats    = loadStats();        // stats base existentes
  const statsExt = loadStatsExt();     // stats extendidas
  const newOnes  = [];

  ACHIEVEMENTS.forEach(a => {
    if (unlocked[a.id]) return;       // ya desbloqueado
    let triggered = false;
    try { triggered = a.check(stats, { ...statsExt, ...gameData }); } catch(e) {}
    if (triggered) {
      unlocked[a.id] = { unlockedAt: Date.now(), gameData };
      newOnes.push(a);
    }
  });

  if (newOnes.length) {
    saveAchiev(unlocked);
    // Mostrar notificaciones en secuencia (300ms entre cada una)
    newOnes.forEach((a, i) => {
      setTimeout(() => showAchievNotif(a), i * 3800);
    });
    // Actualizar badge del menú
    updateAchievBadge();
  }
  return newOnes;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   NOTIFICACIÓN VISUAL DE LOGRO DESBLOQUEADO
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const RARITY_CFG = {
  common:    { label:'Común',     color:'#aaa',    glow:'rgba(200,200,200,.35)', bg:'rgba(40,40,40,.95)' },
  uncommon:  { label:'Poco común',color:'#4CAF50', glow:'rgba(76,175,80,.40)',  bg:'rgba(20,45,20,.95)' },
  rare:      { label:'Raro',      color:'#2196F3', glow:'rgba(33,150,243,.45)', bg:'rgba(10,25,50,.95)' },
  epic:      { label:'Épico',     color:'#9C27B0', glow:'rgba(156,39,176,.50)', bg:'rgba(30,10,50,.95)' },
  legendary: { label:'Legendario',color:'#FFD700', glow:'rgba(255,215,0,.55)',  bg:'rgba(50,35,0,.96)'  },
};

let _achievNotifQueue = [];
let _achievNotifShowing = false;

function showAchievNotif(achiev) {
  const r   = RARITY_CFG[achiev.rarity] || RARITY_CFG.common;
  const el  = document.getElementById('achievNotif');
  if (!el) return;

  el.style.background   = r.bg;
  el.style.borderColor  = r.color;
  el.style.boxShadow    = `0 0 24px ${r.glow}, 0 4px 20px rgba(0,0,0,.6)`;
  el.querySelector('.an-icon').textContent  = achiev.icon;
  el.querySelector('.an-rarity').textContent= r.label;
  el.querySelector('.an-rarity').style.color= r.color;
  el.querySelector('.an-name').textContent  = achiev.name;
  el.querySelector('.an-desc').textContent  = achiev.desc;

  // Sonido de logro
  try {
    const ctx = getCtx();
    const master = getMaster(ctx);
    const t = ctx.currentTime;
    const notes = achiev.rarity === 'legendary'
      ? [523.25,659.25,783.99,1046.5,1318.51]
      : achiev.rarity === 'epic'
      ? [523.25,659.25,783.99,1046.5]
      : achiev.rarity === 'rare'
      ? [523.25,659.25,783.99]
      : [523.25,659.25];
    notes.forEach((f,i) => {
      makeOsc(ctx, f, 'sine', t+i*0.11, 0.01, 0.03, 0.5, 0.25, 0.18, master);
      makeFM(ctx, f, 3.5, 0.4, t+i*0.11, 0.28, 0.07, master);
    });
  } catch(e) {}

  el.classList.remove('an-hidden');
  el.classList.add('an-show');

  clearTimeout(el._hideTimer);
  el._hideTimer = setTimeout(() => {
    el.classList.remove('an-show');
    el.classList.add('an-hidden');
  }, 3600);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   ACTUALIZAR ESTADÍSTICAS EXTENDIDAS EN endGame
   Llamar ANTES de las funciones showResult/checkAchievements
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function updateStatsExtended(playerWon, timeSec, turnsN, pDrawsN, isTournamentWin, isMpMode) {
  const sx = loadStatsExt();
  const now = new Date().toISOString();
  if (!sx.firstPlayDate) sx.firstPlayDate = now;
  sx.lastPlayDate = now;

  if (!isMpMode) {
    // Racha de victorias/derrotas
    if (playerWon) {
      sx.currentStreak++;
      sx.currentLoseStreak = 0;
      if (sx.currentStreak > sx.bestStreak) sx.bestStreak = sx.currentStreak;
      // Racha en dificultad difícil/experto
      if (currentDiff === 'dificil' || currentDiff === 'experto') {
        sx.hardStreakCurrent++;
      } else {
        sx.hardStreakCurrent = 0;
      }
    } else {
      const wasOnLoseStreak = sx.currentLoseStreak;
      sx.currentLoseStreak++;
      sx.currentStreak = 0;
      sx.hardStreakCurrent = 0;
      if (sx.currentLoseStreak > sx.worstLoseStreak) sx.worstLoseStreak = sx.currentLoseStreak;
      // Revenge: gana después de 3 derrotas seguidas — se comprueba ANTES de resetear
    }
    // Modo
    if (!sx.winsByMode[currentMode]) sx.winsByMode[currentMode] = 0;
    if (!sx.gamesByMode[currentMode]) sx.gamesByMode[currentMode] = 0;
    sx.gamesByMode[currentMode]++;
    if (playerWon) {
      sx.winsByMode[currentMode]++;
      // Palo activo al ganar
      if (currentSuit && sx.suitWins.hasOwnProperty(currentSuit)) {
        sx.suitWins[currentSuit]++;
      }
      // Tiempo record
      if (sx.fastestWin === null || timeSec < sx.fastestWin) sx.fastestWin = timeSec;
      // Turnos record
      if (sx.shortestWinTurns === null || turnsN < sx.shortestWinTurns) sx.shortestWinTurns = turnsN;
      // Perfecto (sin robar)
      if (pDrawsN === 0) sx.perfectWins++;
      // Remontada
      if (sessionCamebackFrom >= 10) sx.comebackWins++;
      // Revenge
      if (sx.currentLoseStreak === 0 && wasOnLoseStreak >= 3) sx.revengeWins++;  
    }
  } else {
    sx.multiplayerGames++;
  }

  // Torneo
  if (isTournamentWin) sx.tournamentWins++;

  // Combo máximo histórico
  if (sessionMaxCombo > sx.biggestCombo) sx.biggestCombo = sessionMaxCombo;

  // Ochos y especiales
  sx.totalEights   = (sx.totalEights   || 0) + sessionEightCount;
  sx.totalSpecials = (sx.totalSpecials || 0) + sessionSpecialCount;

  saveStatsExt(sx);
  return sx;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   BADGE DE LOGROS EN EL MENÚ
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function updateAchievBadge() {
  const total    = ACHIEVEMENTS.length;
  const unlocked = Object.keys(loadAchiev()).length;
  const badge    = document.getElementById('achievBadge');
  if (!badge) return;
  badge.textContent = unlocked + '/' + total;
  badge.style.display = unlocked > 0 ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   RENDERIZADO DEL TAB DE LOGROS EN EL MODAL
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function renderAchievTab() {
  const el      = document.getElementById('recTab-achiev');
  if (!el) return;
  const unlocked= loadAchiev();
  const total   = ACHIEVEMENTS.length;
  const unlockedCount = Object.keys(unlocked).length;

  const CATS = {
    basics:  { label:'⭐ Básicos',     color:'#aaa'    },
    streaks: { label:'🔥 Rachas',      color:'#FF9800' },
    mastery: { label:'🎖️ Maestría',   color:'#2196F3' },
    modes:   { label:'🎮 Modos',       color:'#4CAF50' },
    feats:   { label:'💥 Gestas',      color:'#9C27B0' },
    cards:   { label:'🃏 Cartas',      color:'#f0c040' },
  };

  let html = `
    <div class="ach-progress-bar-wrap">
      <div class="ach-progress-bar" style="width:${Math.round(unlockedCount/total*100)}%"></div>
    </div>
    <div class="ach-progress-label">${unlockedCount} / ${total} logros desbloqueados
      (${Math.round(unlockedCount/total*100)}%)</div>`;

  Object.entries(CATS).forEach(([catKey, cat]) => {
    const catItems = ACHIEVEMENTS.filter(a => a.cat === catKey);
    html += `<div class="ach-cat-title" style="color:${cat.color}">${cat.label}</div>
             <div class="ach-grid">`;
    catItems.forEach(a => {
      const u   = unlocked[a.id];
      const r   = RARITY_CFG[a.rarity] || RARITY_CFG.common;
      const date= u ? new Date(u.unlockedAt).toLocaleDateString('es') : '';
      html += `
        <div class="ach-item ${u ? 'ach-done' : 'ach-locked'}"
             style="--glow:${r.glow};--border:${r.color};"
             title="${a.desc}${date ? ' · '+date : ''}">
          <span class="ach-ico">${u ? a.icon : '🔒'}</span>
          <div class="ach-info">
            <div class="ach-name">${u ? a.name : (a.secret ? '???' : a.name)}</div>
            <div class="ach-desc">${u ? a.desc : (a.secret ? 'Logro secreto' : a.desc)}</div>
            <div class="ach-rarity" style="color:${r.color}">${r.label}</div>
          </div>
          ${u ? `<div class="ach-check">✓</div>` : ''}
        </div>`;
    });
    html += '</div>';
  });
  el.innerHTML = html;
}

/* ── Renderizar tab de estadísticas extendidas (rachas, etc.) ── */
function renderStatsExtTab() {
  const el  = document.getElementById('recTab-stats');
  if (!el) return;
  const st  = loadStats();
  const sx  = loadStatsExt();
  const winRate   = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.wins/st.totalGames*100) : 0;
  const avgTime   = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.totalTime/st.totalGames) : 0;
  const avgTurns  = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.totalTurns/st.totalGames) : 0;
  const fmt = s => s && s>=60 ? Math.floor(s/60)+'m '+Math.round(s%60)+'s' : (s||0)+'s';

  // Barras por dificultad
  const diffs = [
    {k:'facil',  label:'Fácil',   color:'#4CAF50'},
    {k:'normal', label:'Normal',  color:'#2196F3'},
    {k:'dificil',label:'Difícil', color:'#FF9800'},
    {k:'experto',label:'Experto', color:'#f44336'},
  ];
  // Barras por modo
  const modes = [
    {k:'clasico', label:'Clásico',   color:'#f0c040'},
    {k:'rapido',  label:'Relámpago', color:'#00BCD4'},
    {k:'dificil', label:'IA Difícil',color:'#FF5722'},
    {k:'torneo',  label:'Torneo',    color:'#9C27B0'},
  ];

  let html = `
    <!-- Rachas -->
    <div class="stat-section-title">🔥 Rachas</div>
    <div class="stat-streak-row">
      <div class="streak-box streak-win">
        <div class="sk-val">${sx.currentStreak}</div>
        <div class="sk-lbl">Racha actual</div>
      </div>
      <div class="streak-box streak-best">
        <div class="sk-val">${sx.bestStreak}</div>
        <div class="sk-lbl">Mejor racha</div>
      </div>
      <div class="streak-box streak-lose">
        <div class="sk-val">${sx.currentLoseStreak}</div>
        <div class="sk-lbl">Derrotas actual</div>
      </div>
      <div class="streak-box streak-worst">
        <div class="sk-val">${sx.worstLoseStreak}</div>
        <div class="sk-lbl">Peor racha</div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <!-- Resumen global -->
    <div class="stat-section-title">📊 Resumen global</div>
    <div class="stat-grid">
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${st.totalGames}</div><div class="sl">Partidas</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv" style="color:#4CAF50">${winRate}%</div><div class="sl">Win rate</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${fmt(sx.fastestWin||null)}</div><div class="sl">Victoria más rápida</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.shortestWinTurns||'—'}</div><div class="sl">Menos turnos</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.perfectWins}</div><div class="sl">Victorias perfectas</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.biggestCombo||0}</div><div class="sl">Mejor combo</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.comebackWins}</div><div class="sl">Remontadas</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.tournamentWins}</div><div class="sl">Torneos ganados</div></div>
    </div>

    <!-- Por dificultad -->
    <div class="stat-section-title">🎯 Por dificultad</div>
    <div class="chart-wrap">`;
  diffs.forEach(d => {
    const played = (st.gamesPlayed && st.gamesPlayed[d.k]) || 0;
    const won    = (st.winsByDiff  && st.winsByDiff[d.k])  || 0;
    const pct    = played > 0 ? Math.round(won/played*100) : 0;
    html += `<div class="stat-row">
      <span class="stat-lbl">${d.label}</span>
      <div class="stat-bar-wrap"><div class="stat-bar" style="width:${pct}%;background:${d.color};"></div></div>
      <span class="stat-val">${won}/${played}</span>
    </div>`;
  });

  html += `</div>
    <!-- Por modo -->
    <div class="stat-section-title">🎮 Por modo</div>
    <div class="chart-wrap">`;
  modes.forEach(m => {
    const played = (sx.gamesByMode && sx.gamesByMode[m.k]) || 0;
    const won    = (sx.winsByMode  && sx.winsByMode[m.k])  || 0;
    const pct    = played > 0 ? Math.round(won/played*100) : 0;
    html += `<div class="stat-row">
      <span class="stat-lbl">${m.label}</span>
      <div class="stat-bar-wrap"><div class="stat-bar" style="width:${pct}%;background:${m.color};"></div></div>
      <span class="stat-val">${won}/${played}</span>
    </div>`;
  });

  // Palos
  const suitSymbols = {'♠':'♠ Espada','♥':'♥ Corazón','♦':'♦ Diamante','♣':'♣ Trébol'};
  html += `</div>
    <div class="stat-section-title">♠ Victorias por palo</div>
    <div class="suit-wins-row">`;
  Object.entries(suitSymbols).forEach(([suit, label]) => {
    const cnt = (sx.suitWins && sx.suitWins[suit]) || 0;
    const isRed = suit==='♥'||suit==='♦';
    html += `<div class="suit-win-box" style="color:${isRed?'#e74c3c':'#eee'}">
      <div class="sw-val">${cnt}</div>
      <div class="sw-suit">${suit}</div>
    </div>`;
  });

  // Cartas históricas
  html += `</div>
    <div class="stat-section-title">🃏 Historial de cartas</div>
    <div class="stat-grid" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(3,1fr)">
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.totalEights||0}</div><div class="sl">Ochos jugados</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${sx.totalSpecials||0}</div><div class="sl">Especiales</div></div>
      <div class="stat-card"><div class="sv">${fmt(avgTime)}</div><div class="sl">Tiempo promedio</div></div>
    </div>
    <div style="font-size:.65rem;color:rgba(255,255,255,.28);text-align:center;margin-top:8px;">
      Primera partida: ${sx.firstPlayDate ? new Date(sx.firstPlayDate).toLocaleDateString('es') : '—'} &nbsp;·&nbsp;
      Última: ${sx.lastPlayDate  ? new Date(sx.lastPlayDate).toLocaleDateString('es')  : '—'}
    </div>`;

  el.innerHTML = html;
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   HOOK EN endGame: actualizar stats + verificar logros
   Se inyecta DESPUÉS de la función endGame original
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
const _origEndGame = window.endGame;
window.endGame = function(playerWon) {
  // Llama endGame original
  _origEndGame.call(this, playerWon);
};

/* ── Parchear endGame para añadir stats extendidas y logros ── */
// Este bloque se ejecuta DESPUÉS de que endGame esté disponible
(function patchEndGame() {
  // Esperar a que endGame esté definida
  const _waitEndGame = setInterval(() => {
    if (typeof endGame === 'function') {
      clearInterval(_waitEndGame);
      const __original = endGame;
      window.endGame = function(playerWon) {
        // Antes de llamar al original, capturar el estado pre-resultado
        const timeSec = Math.round((Date.now() - (gameStartTime||Date.now())) / 1000);
        const wasTournamentEnd = currentMode === 'torneo' &&
          ((playerWon && (tournamentScore.player||0) >= 1) ||
           (!playerWon && (tournamentScore.ai||0) >= 1));

        // Ejecutar lógica original
        __original.call(this, playerWon);

        // Actualizar stats extendidas (solo después del resultado)
        const isTournWin = currentMode === 'torneo' && playerWon &&
          (tournamentScore.player >= 2);
        const sxUpdated = updateStatsExtended(
          playerWon, timeSec, turns, pDraws, isTournWin, mpMode
        );

        // Datos de la partida para verificar logros
        const gameData = {
          won:         playerWon,
          timeSec,
          turns,
          pDraws,
          mpMode,
          mode:        currentMode,
          diff:        currentDiff,
          biggestCombo:   sessionMaxCombo,
          sessionEights:  sessionEightCount,
          sessionSpecials:sessionSpecialCount,
          totalEightsEver:  sxUpdated.totalEights,
          totalSpecialsEver:sxUpdated.totalSpecials,
          comebackWins:  sxUpdated.comebackWins,
          tournamentWins:sxUpdated.tournamentWins,
          winsByMode:    sxUpdated.winsByMode,
          suitWins:      sxUpdated.suitWins,
          perfectWins:   sxUpdated.perfectWins,
          bestStreak:    sxUpdated.bestStreak,
          hardStreakCurrent: sxUpdated.hardStreakCurrent,
          revengeWins:   sxUpdated.revengeWins,
        };
        const newAchievs = checkAchievements(gameData);
        // Mostrar logros desbloqueados en pantalla de resultado (si los hay)
        if (newAchievs.length > 0) {
          setTimeout(() => {
            const el = document.getElementById('resAchievs');
            if (el) {
              el.innerHTML = '<div class="res-achiev-title">🏅 Logros desbloqueados</div>' +
                newAchievs.map(a =>
                  `<div class="res-achiev-item">
                    <span>${a.icon}</span>
                    <span><b>${a.name}</b> — ${a.desc}</span>
                  </div>`
                ).join('');
              el.style.display = 'block';
            }
          }, 600);
        }
        // Actualizar badge
        updateAchievBadge();
      };
    }
  }, 80);
})();

/* ── Reset de variables de sesión al inicio de partida ── */
(function patchStartGame() {
  const _waitSG = setInterval(() => {
    if (typeof startGame === 'function') {
      clearInterval(_waitSG);
      const __origSG = startGame;
      window.startGame = async function() {
        // Reset sesión
        sessionMaxCombo     = 0;
        sessionEightCount   = 0;
        sessionSpecialCount = 0;
        sessionMaxHand      = 0;
        sessionCamebackFrom = 0;
        await __origSG.call(this);
      };
    }
  }, 80);
})();

/* ── Rastrear combos y cartas especiales en playSelected ── */
(function patchPlaySelected() {
  const _waitPS = setInterval(() => {
    if (typeof playSelected === 'function') {
      clearInterval(_waitPS);
      const __origPS = playSelected;
      window.playSelected = function() {
        const cards = selectedIndices.map(i => player[i]);
        if (cards.length > sessionMaxCombo) sessionMaxCombo = cards.length;
        // Rastrear ochos y especiales
        cards.forEach(c => {
          if (!c) return;
          if (c.v === '8') sessionEightCount++;
          if (['A','2','3','7','8','10','J'].includes(c.v)) sessionSpecialCount++;
        });
        // Rastrear mano máxima (para comeback)
        if (player.length > sessionCamebackFrom) sessionCamebackFrom = player.length;
        __origPS.call(this);
      };
    }
  }, 80);
})();

/* ── Inicializar badge al cargar ── */
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
  updateAchievBadge();
});
// También llamar inmediatamente en caso de que DOMContentLoaded ya pasó
setTimeout(updateAchievBadge, 200);


/* ── Helper tab directo ── */
function switchRecTabDirect(tab) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.tab-panel').forEach(p=>p.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.mtab').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const panel = document.getElementById('recTab-'+tab);
  if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
  const allTabs = document.querySelectorAll('.mtab');
  allTabs.forEach(b=>{ if(b.getAttribute('onclick')&&b.getAttribute('onclick').includes(tab)) b.classList.add('active'); });
  if (tab==='achiev') renderAchievTab();
  else if (tab==='stats') renderStatsExtTab();
}
