buildBg();
buildMenuDeck();
// Start menu music on first interaction
document.addEventListener('click', function _firstClick() {
  startMenuMusic();
  document.removeEventListener('click', _firstClick);
}, {once:true});

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   ADVANCED PARTICLE ENGINE v19.0 – OCHO LOCOS PRO
   Modules: Canvas Fireworks · DOM Confetti · 3D Stars · Achievements · Defeat
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

/* ── CANVAS FIREWORKS ENGINE ─────────────────────────────────────────────── */
(function() {
  const FW = {
    canvas: null, ctx: null, raf: null,
    rockets: [], particles: [], running: false,
    W: 0, H: 0,
    palettes: {
      victory:   ['#FFD700','#FF6B6B','#74B9FF','#A29BFE','#55EFC4','#FD79A8','#FDCB6E','#00CEC9','#E17055','#6C5CE7'],
      tournament:['#FFD700','#FFC300','#FF8C00','#FF4500','#DC143C','#GOLD','#FFFACD','#FFEAA7'],
      streak:    ['#FF4500','#FF6347','#FF7F50','#FFA500','#FFD700','#FFFF00'],
      legendary: ['#A29BFE','#6C5CE7','#FD79A8','#E84393','#FFD700','#FFFFFF']
    },
    shapes: ['circle','square','star','triangle','ring'],

    init() {
      this.canvas = document.getElementById('fw-canvas');
      if (!this.canvas) return;
      this.ctx = this.canvas.getContext('2d');
      this.resize();
      window.addEventListener('resize', () => this.resize());
    },

    resize() {
      if (!this.canvas) return;
      this.W = this.canvas.width  = window.innerWidth;
      this.H = this.canvas.height = window.innerHeight;
    },

    launch(x, y, palette, count=180) {
      if (!this.canvas) this.init();
      const pal = this.palettes[palette] || this.palettes.victory;
      const burst = [];
      for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
        const angle = (Math.PI * 2 * i) / count + Math.random() * 0.3;
        const speed = 2 + Math.random() * 8;
        const color = pal[Math.floor(Math.random() * pal.length)];
        const shape = this.shapes[Math.floor(Math.random() * this.shapes.length)];
        burst.push({
          x, y,
          vx: Math.cos(angle) * speed * (0.5 + Math.random()),
          vy: Math.sin(angle) * speed * (0.5 + Math.random()) - 2,
          ax: 0,
          ay: 0.12 + Math.random() * 0.06,
          color,
          shape,
          size: 3 + Math.random() * 5,
          life: 1,
          decay: 0.012 + Math.random() * 0.018,
          trail: [],
          spin: Math.random() * Math.PI * 2,
          spinV: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 0.3,
          twinkle: Math.random() > 0.7
        });
      }
      this.particles.push(...burst);
      // Flash effect
      const flash = document.createElement('div');
      flash.className = 'firework-flash';
      document.body.appendChild(flash);
      setTimeout(() => flash.remove(), 300);
    },

    launchRocket(tx, ty, palette) {
      if (!this.canvas) this.init();
      const pal = this.palettes[palette] || this.palettes.victory;
      this.rockets.push({
        x: this.W * (0.2 + Math.random() * 0.6),
        y: this.H + 10,
        tx, ty,
        vx: (Math.random() - 0.5) * 2,
        vy: -12 - Math.random() * 5,
        color: pal[Math.floor(Math.random() * pal.length)],
        palette,
        trail: [],
        exploded: false
      });
    },

    drawShape(ctx, p) {
      ctx.save();
      ctx.globalAlpha = p.life;
      ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
      ctx.strokeStyle = p.color;
      ctx.translate(p.x, p.y);
      ctx.rotate(p.spin);
      const s = p.size * (p.twinkle ? (0.7 + 0.3 * Math.sin(Date.now() * 0.01 + p.spin)) : 1);
      if (p.shape === 'circle') {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(0, 0, s, 0, Math.PI*2); ctx.fill();
      } else if (p.shape === 'square') {
        ctx.fillRect(-s, -s, s*2, s*2);
      } else if (p.shape === 'triangle') {
        ctx.beginPath();
        ctx.moveTo(0, -s*1.2);
        ctx.lineTo(s, s); ctx.lineTo(-s, s);
        ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      } else if (p.shape === 'star') {
        ctx.beginPath();
        for (let j = 0; j < 5; j++) {
          const a = (j * 4 * Math.PI / 5) - Math.PI/2;
          const r = j % 2 === 0 ? s*1.3 : s*0.55;
          if (j === 0) ctx.moveTo(r*Math.cos(a), r*Math.sin(a));
          else ctx.lineTo(r*Math.cos(a), r*Math.sin(a));
        }
        ctx.closePath(); ctx.fill();
      } else if (p.shape === 'ring') {
        ctx.beginPath(); ctx.arc(0, 0, s*1.2, 0, Math.PI*2);
        ctx.lineWidth = 2; ctx.stroke();
      }
      ctx.restore();
    },

    tick() {
      if (!this.ctx) return;
      this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.W, this.H);

      // Update & draw rockets
      this.rockets = this.rockets.filter(r => {
        r.trail.push({x: r.x, y: r.y, life: 0.8});
        r.x += r.vx; r.y += r.vy; r.vy += 0.3;
        // Draw trail
        r.trail.forEach((t, ti) => {
          t.life -= 0.06;
          this.ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, t.life);
          this.ctx.fillStyle = r.color;
          this.ctx.beginPath();
          this.ctx.arc(t.x, t.y, 2 * (ti/r.trail.length), 0, Math.PI*2);
          this.ctx.fill();
        });
        r.trail = r.trail.filter(t => t.life > 0);
        // Draw rocket head
        this.ctx.globalAlpha = 1;
        this.ctx.fillStyle = '#ffffff';
        this.ctx.beginPath();
        this.ctx.arc(r.x, r.y, 3, 0, Math.PI*2);
        this.ctx.fill();
        // Check if reached target
        if (r.y <= r.ty || r.vy >= 0) {
          this.launch(r.x, r.y, r.palette);
          return false;
        }
        return true;
      });

      // Update & draw particles
      this.particles = this.particles.filter(p => {
        p.trail.push({x: p.x, y: p.y, life: p.life * 0.5});
        p.x += p.vx; p.y += p.vy;
        p.vx *= 0.98; p.vy += p.ay;
        p.spin += p.spinV;
        p.life -= p.decay;
        // Draw trail
        p.trail.slice(-4).forEach((t, ti) => {
          t.life -= 0.08;
          this.ctx.globalAlpha = Math.max(0, t.life * 0.4);
          this.ctx.fillStyle = p.color;
          this.ctx.beginPath();
          this.ctx.arc(t.x, t.y, p.size * 0.4, 0, Math.PI*2);
          this.ctx.fill();
        });
        p.trail = p.trail.slice(-5);
        if (p.life > 0) this.drawShape(this.ctx, p);
        return p.life > 0;
      });

      if (this.rockets.length > 0 || this.particles.length > 0) {
        this.raf = requestAnimationFrame(() => this.tick());
        this.running = true;
      } else {
        this.running = false;
        this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.W, this.H);
      }
    },

    startLoop() {
      if (!this.running) {
        this.running = true;
        this.tick();
      }
    },

    stop() {
      if (this.raf) cancelAnimationFrame(this.raf);
      this.rockets = []; this.particles = [];
      this.running = false;
      if (this.ctx) this.ctx.clearRect(0, 0, this.W, this.H);
    }
  };
  window.FW = FW;
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => FW.init());
})();

/* ── DOM CONFETTI HELPERS ─────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function spawnConfettiLayer(container, count, opts={}) {
  const cls  = opts.cls || ['#f0c040','#ff6b6b','#74b9ff','#a29bfe','#55efc4','#fd79a8','#fdcb6e','#00cec9'];
  const shapes = ['','tri','star','circle','ribbon','ring'];
  const easings = ['ease-in','cubic-bezier(.25,.46,.45,.94)','linear','ease-in-out'];
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const p = document.createElement('div');
    const shape = shapes[Math.floor(Math.random() * shapes.length)];
    p.className = 'cp' + (shape ? ' ' + shape : '');
    const color = cls[i % cls.length];
    const w = shape === 'ribbon' ? 14 : 5 + Math.random() * 10;
    const h = shape === 'ribbon' ? 3  : w * (0.6 + Math.random());
    const dur = 2.2 + Math.random() * 3.8;
    const delay = (opts.stagger || 0) + Math.random() * (opts.spread || 2.5);
    const spin = 360 + Math.random() * 720;
    const tilt = Math.random() * 360;
    const ease = easings[Math.floor(Math.random() * easings.length)];
    const startX = opts.x != null ? opts.x + (Math.random()-0.5)*12 + '%' : Math.random()*100 + '%';
    p.style.cssText = [
      `left:${startX}`,
      `background:${shape === 'ring' ? 'transparent' : color}`,
      `--ring-color:${color}`,
      `width:${w}px`, `height:${h}px`,
      `--dur:${dur}s`, `--delay:${delay}s`,
      `--spin:${spin}deg`, `--tilt:${tilt}deg`,
      `--ease:${ease}`,
      `top:-20px`
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(p);
    setTimeout(() => p.remove(), (dur + delay + 0.5) * 1000);
  }
}

function spawn3DStars(container, count, opts={}) {
  const emojis = opts.emojis || ['⭐','✨','🌟','💫','🎆','🎇','🌠'];
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const s = document.createElement('div');
    s.className = 'star3d';
    s.textContent = emojis[i % emojis.length];
    const sz = 18 + Math.random() * 22;
    const tx = (Math.random() * 300 - 150) + 'px';
    const ty = (-60 - Math.random() * 280) + 'px';
    const dur = 2 + Math.random() * 2.5;
    const delay = Math.random() * (opts.maxDelay || 2.5);
    s.style.cssText = [
      `left:${opts.x != null ? opts.x : 5 + Math.random()*90}%`,
      `top:${opts.y != null ? opts.y : 10 + Math.random()*60}%`,
      `--sz:${sz}px`,
      `--tx:${tx}`, `--ty:${ty}`,
      `--dur:${dur}s`, `--delay:${delay}s`
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(s);
    setTimeout(() => s.remove(), (dur + delay + 0.5) * 1000);
  }
}

function spawnAshCloud(container, count) {
  const colors = ['#aaaaaa','#888888','#666666','#444444','#cc7722','#8b4513'];
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const a = document.createElement('div');
    a.className = 'ash';
    const dur = 2.5 + Math.random() * 2.5;
    a.style.cssText = [
      `left:${Math.random()*100}%`,
      `--c:${colors[i % colors.length]}`,
      `--dur:${dur}s`,
      `--delay:${Math.random()*2}s`,
      `--tx:${(Math.random()-0.5)*120}px`
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(a);
    setTimeout(() => a.remove(), (dur + 2 + 0.5) * 1000);
  }
}

function spawnEmbers(container, count) {
  const icons = ['🔥','💀','😈','⚰️','🌑','💔'];
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const e = document.createElement('div');
    e.className = 'ember';
    e.textContent = icons[i % icons.length];
    const sz = 14 + Math.random() * 14;
    const dur = 1.8 + Math.random() * 2.2;
    e.style.cssText = [
      `left:${Math.random()*100}%`,
      `--sz:${sz}px`,
      `--dur:${dur}s`,
      `--delay:${Math.random()*2.5}s`,
      `--spin:${(Math.random()-0.5)*360}deg`
    ].join(';');
    container.appendChild(e);
    setTimeout(() => e.remove(), (dur + 2.5 + 0.5) * 1000);
  }
}

/* ── ACHIEVEMENT BURST ────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function spawnAchievementBurst(anchorEl, rarity) {
  const palettes = {
    common:    ['#a0a0a0','#c0c0c0','#e0e0e0'],
    uncommon:  ['#55efc4','#00b894','#81ecec'],
    rare:      ['#74b9ff','#0984e3','#a29bfe'],
    epic:      ['#a29bfe','#6c5ce7','#fd79a8','#e84393'],
    legendary: ['#ffd700','#ffb300','#ff8c00','#ffffff','#a29bfe']
  };
  const pal = palettes[rarity] || palettes.common;
  const count = rarity === 'legendary' ? 40 : rarity === 'epic' ? 28 : rarity === 'rare' ? 20 : 14;
  const rect = anchorEl ? anchorEl.getBoundingClientRect() : {left:window.innerWidth/2, top:window.innerHeight/2};
  const cx = rect.left + (rect.width||0)/2;
  const cy = rect.top + (rect.height||0)/2;

  const layer = document.getElementById('particle-layer') || document.body;
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const p = document.createElement('div');
    p.className = 'achieve-burst';
    const angle = (2 * Math.PI * i) / count;
    const dist = 50 + Math.random() * 120;
    p.style.cssText = [
      `left:${cx}px`, `top:${cy}px`,
      `--c:${pal[i % pal.length]}`,
      `--r:${4+Math.random()*6}px`,
      `--tx:${Math.cos(angle)*dist}px`,
      `--ty:${Math.sin(angle)*dist}px`,
      `--dur:${0.8+Math.random()*1.2}s`,
      `--delay:${Math.random()*0.4}s`
    ].join(';');
    layer.appendChild(p);
    setTimeout(() => p.remove(), 2500);
  }

  // Also launch canvas burst
  if (window.FW) {
    const palette = rarity === 'legendary' ? 'legendary' : rarity === 'epic' ? 'legendary' : 'victory';
    window.FW.launch(cx, cy, palette, rarity === 'legendary' ? 120 : rarity === 'epic' ? 80 : 50);
    window.FW.startLoop();
  }
}

/* ── STREAK FIRE TRAIL ───────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function spawnStreakFire(streakCount) {
  const layer = document.getElementById('particle-layer') || document.body;
  const icons = streakCount >= 10 ? ['🔥','⚡','💥','🌟','🎆'] :
                streakCount >=  5 ? ['🔥','⚡','✨','💫'] : ['🔥','✨'];
  const count = Math.min(streakCount * 3, 25);
  for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
    const f = document.createElement('div');
    f.className = 'streak-fire';
    f.textContent = icons[i % icons.length];
    const sz = 14 + Math.random() * 14;
    f.style.cssText = [
      `left:${10 + Math.random()*80}%`,
      `bottom:${10 + Math.random()*30}%`,
      `--sz:${sz}px`,
      `--dur:${0.8+Math.random()*0.8}s`,
      `--delay:${i*0.07}s`
    ].join(';');
    layer.appendChild(f);
    setTimeout(() => f.remove(), 2000);
  }
}

/* ── MAIN VICTORY CELEBRATION ────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function launchVictoryParticles(domContainer, isTournament) {
  const layer = document.getElementById('particle-layer') || domContainer;

  // 1) Multi-wave confetti
  const confettiColors = isTournament
    ? ['#FFD700','#FFC300','#FF8C00','#FFFACD','#FFEAA7','#ff6b6b','#a29bfe']
    : ['#f0c040','#ff6b6b','#74b9ff','#a29bfe','#55efc4','#fd79a8','#fdcb6e','#00cec9'];

  // Wave 1 – immediate heavy burst
  spawnConfettiLayer(layer, 80, {cls: confettiColors, spread: 0.8, stagger: 0});
  // Wave 2 – delayed secondary wave
  setTimeout(() => spawnConfettiLayer(layer, 60, {cls: confettiColors, spread: 1.2, stagger: 0.3}), 800);
  // Wave 3 – finale
  setTimeout(() => spawnConfettiLayer(layer, 40, {cls: confettiColors, spread: 0.6, stagger: 0.1}), 2200);

  // 2) 3D stars
  spawn3DStars(layer, isTournament ? 20 : 14);

  // 3) Canvas fireworks
  if (window.FW) {
    const pal = isTournament ? 'tournament' : 'victory';
    const W = window.innerWidth, H = window.innerHeight;
    // Immediate center burst
    window.FW.launch(W*0.5, H*0.4, pal, isTournament ? 220 : 180);
    window.FW.startLoop();
    // Scheduled rockets
    const schedule = isTournament
      ? [[400,0.3,0.25],[700,0.7,0.2],[1100,0.5,0.35],[1500,0.25,0.3],[1900,0.75,0.25],[2400,0.5,0.2]]
      : [[500,0.3,0.3],[900,0.7,0.25],[1400,0.5,0.2],[1900,0.2,0.3],[2500,0.8,0.22]];
    schedule.forEach(([delay, xFrac, yFrac]) => {
      setTimeout(() => {
        if (window.FW) {
          window.FW.launchRocket(W*xFrac, H*yFrac, pal);
          window.FW.startLoop();
        }
      }, delay);
    });
    // Auto-stop after celebration
    setTimeout(() => { if (window.FW) window.FW.stop(); }, isTournament ? 8000 : 6000);
  }
}

/* ── DEFEAT PARTICLES ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function launchDefeatParticles(domContainer) {
  const layer = document.getElementById('particle-layer') || domContainer;
  spawnEmbers(layer, 22);
  spawnAshCloud(layer, 35);
}

/* ── PATCH showAchievNotif TO ADD BURST ─────────────────────────────────── */
(function patchAchievNotif() {
  const _orig = window.showAchievNotif;
  if (typeof _orig !== 'function') return;
  window.showAchievNotif = function(achiev) {
    _orig.call(this, achiev);
    // Trigger particle burst
    const el = document.getElementById('achievNotif');
    setTimeout(() => spawnAchievementBurst(el, achiev.rarity), 100);
    // Fire trail for streaks
    if (achiev.id && (achiev.id.includes('streak') || achiev.id.includes('racha'))) {
      const streak = (typeof sx !== 'undefined' && sx.currentStreak) || 3;
      setTimeout(() => spawnStreakFire(streak), 200);
    }
  };
})();

/* ── STREAK CELEBRATION HOOK ──────────────────────────────────────────────── */
function celebrateStreak(n) {
  spawnStreakFire(n);
  if (n >= 5 && window.FW) {
    const W = window.innerWidth, H = window.innerHeight;
    const pal = n >= 10 ? 'streak' : 'victory';
    window.FW.launch(W*0.5, H*0.3, pal, n >= 10 ? 160 : 100);
    window.FW.startLoop();
    setTimeout(() => { if (window.FW) window.FW.stop(); }, 4000);
  }
}

/* ── MINI-BURST for card actions ─────────────────────────────────────────── */
function cardBurst(x, y, type) {
  if (!window.FW) return;
  const palMap = {
    wild8:     'legendary',
    victory:   'victory',
    combo:     'streak',
    tournament:'tournament'
  };
  const count = type === 'wild8' ? 60 : type === 'combo' ? 45 : 30;
  window.FW.launch(x, y, palMap[type] || 'victory', count);
  window.FW.startLoop();
  setTimeout(() => { if (window.FW && !window.FW.rockets.length) window.FW.stop(); }, 3000);
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   MENU STATS PANEL — renderiza al abrir el menú
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════ */
function renderMenuStats() {
  try {
    const st  = loadStats();
    const sx  = loadStatsExt ? loadStatsExt() : {};
    const wr  = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round(st.wins / st.totalGames * 100) : 0;

    // Racha
    const stEl   = document.getElementById('msb-streak-val');
    const stPill = document.getElementById('msb-streak');
    const bsEl   = document.getElementById('msb-best-val');
    const wrEl   = document.getElementById('msb-wr-val');
    if (stEl) stEl.textContent = (sx.currentStreak || 0);
    if (stPill) stPill.classList.toggle('streak-active', (sx.currentStreak||0) >= 3);
    if (bsEl) bsEl.textContent = (sx.bestStreak || 0);
    if (wrEl) wrEl.textContent = wr + '%';

    // Por modo
    const modesEl = document.getElementById('msb-modes');
    if (modesEl) {
      const modes = [
        {k:'clasico', icon:'🃏', name:'Clásico',   color:'#f0c040'},
        {k:'rapido',  icon:'⚡', name:'Rápido',    color:'#00BCD4'},
        {k:'dificil', icon:'🤖', name:'IA Dif.',   color:'#FF5722'},
        {k:'torneo',  icon:'🏆', name:'Torneo',    color:'#9C27B0'},
      ];
      modesEl.innerHTML = modes.map(m => {
        const played = (sx.gamesByMode && sx.gamesByMode[m.k]) || 0;
        const won    = (sx.winsByMode  && sx.winsByMode[m.k])  || 0;
        const pct    = played > 0 ? Math.round(won / played * 100) : 0;
        return `<div class="msb-mode">
          <span class="msb-mode-icon">${m.icon}</span>
          <span class="msb-mode-name">${m.name}</span>
          <div class="msb-mode-bar-wrap">
            <div class="msb-mode-bar" style="width:${pct}%;background:${m.color};"></div>
          </div>
          <span class="msb-mode-pct">${pct}%</span>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');
    }

    // Por palo
    const suitsEl = document.getElementById('msb-suits');
    if (suitsEl) {
      const suits = [
        {s:'♠', name:'Espada', color:'#aaa'},
        {s:'♥', name:'Corazón', color:'#e74c3c'},
        {s:'♦', name:'Diamante',color:'#e74c3c'},
        {s:'♣', name:'Trébol', color:'#aaa'},
      ];
      suitsEl.innerHTML = suits.map(su => {
        const cnt = (sx.suitWins && sx.suitWins[su.s]) || 0;
        return `<div class="msb-suit">
          <span class="msb-suit-sym" style="color:${su.color}">${su.s}</span>
          <span class="msb-suit-cnt">${cnt}</span>
          <span class="msb-suit-lbl">${su.name}</span>
        </div>`;
      }).join('');
    }
  } catch(e) { console.warn('renderMenuStats error:', e); }
}

let _menuStatsOpen = true;

  const body   = document.getElementById('menuStatsBody');
  const toggle = document.querySelector('#menuStatsBar .msb-toggle');
  if (!body) return;

  body.classList.toggle('collapsed', !_menuStatsOpen);
  if (toggle) toggle.textContent = _menuStatsOpen ? '▲ ocultar' : '▼ ver estadísticas';
}

/* ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
   PLAYER PROFILE SYSTEM v19.0 — OCHO LOCOS PRO
   XP · Levels · Avatars · Leaderboard · Persistence

const LS_PROFILE   = 'ol_profile_v1';
const LS_LEADERBOARD = 'ol_leaders_v1';

/* ── XP TABLE: 100 levels, progressive scaling ── */
const XP_TABLE = (() => {
  const t = [0]; // level 0 placeholder
  for (let lv = 1; lv <= 100; lv++) {
    // Base: 100 XP * level * growth factor
    const xp = Math.round(100 * lv * (1 + lv * 0.08));
    t.push(xp);
  }
  return t; // t[lv] = XP needed to go from lv to lv+1
})();

function totalXpForLevel(lv) {
  // Total cumulative XP needed to REACH level lv
  let total = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < lv && i < XP_TABLE.length; i++) total += XP_TABLE[i];
  return total;
}

function levelFromTotalXp(totalXp) {
  let lv = 1, cumulative = 0;
  for (let i = 1; i < XP_TABLE.length; i++) {
    if (cumulative + XP_TABLE[i] > totalXp) break;
    cumulative += XP_TABLE[i];
    lv = i + 1;
  }
  return { level: Math.min(lv, 100), xpInLevel: totalXp - totalXpForLevel(lv), xpNeeded: XP_TABLE[Math.min(lv,99)] || 9999 };
}

/* ── RANKS (every 10 levels) ── */
const RANKS = [
  { name:'Hierro',    range:[1,10],   cls:'lv-iron',     color:'#aaa'    },
  { name:'Bronce',    range:[11,20],  cls:'lv-bronze',   color:'#cd7f32' },
  { name:'Plata',     range:[21,30],  cls:'lv-silver',   color:'#c0c0c0' },
  { name:'Oro',       range:[31,40],  cls:'lv-gold',     color:'#ffd700' },
  { name:'Platino',   range:[41,50],  cls:'lv-platinum', color:'#80deea' },
  { name:'Diamante',  range:[51,65],  cls:'lv-diamond',  color:'#82b1ff' },
  { name:'Maestro',   range:[66,80],  cls:'lv-master',   color:'#ce93d8' },
  { name:'Leyenda',   range:[81,100], cls:'lv-legend',   color:'#ff8a65' },
  { name:'Prestigio', range:[101,999],cls:'lv-prestige', color:'#ffd700' },
];

function getRank(level) {
  for (const r of RANKS) {
    if (level >= r.range[0] && level <= r.range[1]) return r;
  }
  return RANKS[RANKS.length - 1];
}

/* ── TITLE NAMES by level ── */
const TITLES = [
  [1,   'Novato'],        [5,  'Aprendiz'],     [10, 'Jugador'],
  [15,  'Experimentado'],[20, 'Competidor'],    [25, 'Táctico'],
  [30,  'Estratega'],    [35, 'Veterano'],      [40, 'Experto'],
  [45,  'Maestro'],      [50, 'Gran Maestro'],  [60, 'Campeón'],
  [70,  'Leyenda'],      [80, 'Inmortal'],      [90, 'Mítico'],
  [100, 'Transcendente'],[101,'⭐ Prestiǵio'],
];
function getTitle(level) {
  let t = TITLES[0][1];
  for (const [lv, name] of TITLES) { if (level >= lv) t = name; else break; }
  return t;
}

/* ── DEFAULT PROFILE ── */
function defaultProfile() {
  return {
    nickname: 'Jugador',
    avatar: '🎮',
    color: '#f0c040',
    totalXp: 0,
    prestige: 0,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    gamesHistory: [], // last 20 XP gains
  };
}

/* ── PERSISTENCE ── */
function loadProfile() {
  try {
    const raw = localStorage.getItem(LS_PROFILE);
    if (!raw) return defaultProfile();
    return Object.assign(defaultProfile(), JSON.parse(raw));
  } catch(e) { return defaultProfile(); }
}
function saveProfile(p) {
  localStorage.setItem(LS_PROFILE, JSON.stringify(p));
}

/* Leaderboard: array of {nickname, avatar, totalXp, color, date} */
function loadLeaderboard() {
  try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_LEADERBOARD)) || []; }
  catch(e) { return []; }
}
function saveLeaderboard(lb) {
  localStorage.setItem(LS_LEADERBOARD, JSON.stringify(lb));
}
function updateLeaderboard(profile) {
  const lb = loadLeaderboard();
  const existing = lb.findIndex(e => e.id === profile.id || e.nickname === profile.nickname);
  const entry = {
    id: profile.id || (profile.id = Date.now().toString(36)),
    nickname: profile.nickname,
    avatar:   profile.avatar,
    color:    profile.color,
    totalXp:  profile.totalXp,
    prestige: profile.prestige || 0,
    date:     new Date().toISOString(),
  };
  if (existing >= 0) lb[existing] = entry;
  else lb.push(entry);
  lb.sort((a,b) => (b.prestige||0)*1e9 + b.totalXp - ((a.prestige||0)*1e9 + a.totalXp));
  saveLeaderboard(lb.slice(0, 20));
}

/* ── XP CALCULATION per game ── */
function calcXpGain(playerWon, turnsN, pDrawsN, timeSec, diffKey, mode, isPerfect, isComeback) {
  if (!playerWon) {
    // Consolation XP
    return { base: 10, breakdown:[{label:'Participación',val:10}], total:10 };
  }
  const breakdown = [];
  let total = 0;

  const baseXp = { facil:40, normal:70, dificil:120, experto:200 }[diffKey] || 70;
  breakdown.push({ label: `Victoria (${diffKey})`, val: baseXp });
  total += baseXp;

  // Mode bonus
  const modeBonus = { clasico:0, rapido:15, dificil:20, torneo:35 }[mode] || 0;
  if (modeBonus) { breakdown.push({ label: `Modo ${mode}`, val: modeBonus }); total += modeBonus; }

  // Speed bonus
  if (timeSec < 30)      { breakdown.push({label:'⚡ Velocista (<30s)', val:40}); total+=40; }
  else if (timeSec < 60) { breakdown.push({label:'💨 Rápido (<60s)', val:20});    total+=20; }

  // Efficiency
  if (pDrawsN === 0)     { breakdown.push({label:'✨ Sin robar', val:30});         total+=30; }
  else if (pDrawsN <= 2) { breakdown.push({label:'👍 Pocos robos', val:10});        total+=10; }

  // Turns bonus
  if (turnsN <= 8)       { breakdown.push({label:'🎯 Ejecutor (≤8t)', val:25});    total+=25; }
  else if (turnsN <= 12) { breakdown.push({label:'🎯 Rápido (≤12t)', val:12});     total+=12; }

  // Perfect / comeback
  if (isPerfect)   { breakdown.push({label:'💎 Victoria perfecta', val:50}); total+=50; }
  if (isComeback)  { breakdown.push({label:'💪 Remontada',          val:35}); total+=35; }

  return { base: baseXp, breakdown, total: Math.round(total) };
}

/* ── ADD XP & CHECK LEVEL UP ── */
function addXpToProfile(xpAmount, breakdown) {
  const profile = loadProfile();
  const beforeLv = levelFromTotalXp(profile.totalXp);

  profile.totalXp += xpAmount;
  profile.gamesHistory = [{xp: xpAmount, date: new Date().toISOString()}, ...profile.gamesHistory].slice(0,20);

  // Handle prestige (beyond level 100)
  const afterInfo = levelFromTotalXp(profile.totalXp);
  let lvlUp = false;
  if (afterInfo.level > beforeLv.level) {
    lvlUp = true;
    if (afterInfo.level >= 100 && profile.totalXp >= totalXpForLevel(101)) {
      profile.prestige = (profile.prestige || 0) + 1;
      profile.totalXp = 0; // reset for prestige
    }
  }

  saveProfile(profile);
  updateLeaderboard(profile);
  updateProfileUI(profile);
  showXpGainPopup(xpAmount, breakdown, lvlUp, beforeLv.level, afterInfo.level);
  return { profile, lvlUp, oldLevel: beforeLv.level, newLevel: afterInfo.level };
}

/* ── XP POPUP ── */
let _xpPopupTimer = null;
function showXpGainPopup(total, breakdown, lvlUp, oldLv, newLv) {
  const popup  = document.getElementById('xpGainPopup');
  const brkEl  = document.getElementById('xpBreakdown');
  const totEl  = document.getElementById('xpPopupTotal');
  const lvlBan = document.getElementById('xpLvlupBanner');
  if (!popup) return;

  brkEl.innerHTML = breakdown.map(b =>
    `<div class="xp-popup-row"><span>${b.label}</span><span class="xv">+${b.val}</span></div>`
  ).join('');
  totEl.textContent = '+' + total + ' XP';

  if (lvlUp) {
    lvlBan.textContent = `🆙 ¡NIVEL ${newLv}! ${getRank(newLv).name}`;
    lvlBan.classList.add('show');
    try { sfxTournamentFanfare && sfxTournamentFanfare(); } catch(e){}
  } else {
    lvlBan.classList.remove('show');
  }

  popup.classList.add('show');
  clearTimeout(_xpPopupTimer);
  _xpPopupTimer = setTimeout(() => popup.classList.remove('show'), lvlUp ? 5500 : 3800);
}

/* ── UPDATE ALL UI ELEMENTS ── */
function updateProfileUI(profile) {
  if (!profile) profile = loadProfile();
  const info = levelFromTotalXp(profile.totalXp);
  const rank = getRank(info.level);
  const pct  = Math.round((info.xpInLevel / info.xpNeeded) * 100);
  const fullLv = profile.prestige ? info.level + ' ✦' + profile.prestige : info.level;

  // Menu chip
  const pcAvatar  = document.getElementById('pcAvatar');
  const pcName    = document.getElementById('pcName');
  const pcBadge   = document.getElementById('pcBadge');
  const pcXpBar   = document.getElementById('pcXpBar');
  const pcXpText  = document.getElementById('pcXpText');
  if (pcAvatar) pcAvatar.textContent = profile.avatar;
  if (pcName)   pcName.textContent   = profile.nickname;
  if (pcBadge) {
    pcBadge.textContent   = 'Nv.' + fullLv;
    pcBadge.className     = 'pc-level-badge ' + rank.cls;
  }
  if (pcXpBar) pcXpBar.style.width  = pct + '%';
  if (pcXpBar) pcXpBar.style.background = rank.color;
  if (pcXpText) pcXpText.textContent = info.xpInLevel + '/' + info.xpNeeded;

  // In-game HUD
  const phudAvatar = document.getElementById('phudAvatar');
  const phudName   = document.getElementById('phudName');
  const phudLevel  = document.getElementById('phudLevel');
  if (phudAvatar) phudAvatar.textContent = profile.avatar;
  if (phudName)   phudName.textContent   = profile.nickname;
  if (phudLevel) {
    phudLevel.textContent = 'Nv.' + fullLv;
    phudLevel.className   = 'phud-level ' + rank.cls;
  }
}

function switchPfTab(tab, btnEl) {
  _pfCurrentTab = tab;
  document.querySelectorAll('.pf-tab').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
  document.querySelectorAll('.pf-tab-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
  const panel = document.getElementById('pftab-' + tab);
  if (panel) panel.classList.add('active');
  if (btnEl) btnEl.classList.add('active');

  if (tab === 'avatar')      renderAvatarTab();
  if (tab === 'leaderboard') renderLeaderboardTab();
  if (tab === 'edit')        renderEditTab();
  if (tab === 'stats')       renderPfStatsTab();
}

/* ── RENDER MODAL ── */
function renderProfileModal(profile) {
  if (!profile) profile = loadProfile();
  const info  = levelFromTotalXp(profile.totalXp);
  const rank  = getRank(info.level);
  const title = getTitle(info.level);
  const pct   = Math.round((info.xpInLevel / info.xpNeeded) * 100);
  const fullLv = profile.prestige ? info.level + ' ✦' + profile.prestige : info.level;

  // Hero
  const ha = document.getElementById('pfHeroAvatar');
  if (ha) ha.childNodes[0].textContent = profile.avatar;

  const hn = document.getElementById('pfHeroName');
  if (hn) hn.textContent = profile.nickname;
  if (hn) hn.style.color = profile.color || '#fff';

  const ht = document.getElementById('pfHeroTitle');
  if (ht) ht.textContent = title + ' · ' + rank.name + ' ' + (info.level % 10 || 10);

  const ln = document.getElementById('pfLevelNum');
  if (ln) { ln.textContent = fullLv; ln.style.color = rank.color; }

  const tx = document.getElementById('pfTotalXp');
  if (tx) tx.textContent = profile.totalXp.toLocaleString();

  const pb = document.getElementById('pfPrestigeBadge');
  if (pb) {
    pb.style.display = profile.prestige ? 'inline-block' : 'none';
    pb.textContent = '✦ Prestigio ' + (profile.prestige || 0);
  }

  const xpc = document.getElementById('pfXpCurrent');
  if (xpc) xpc.textContent = info.xpInLevel.toLocaleString() + ' XP';

  const xpn = document.getElementById('pfXpNeeded');
  if (xpn) xpn.textContent = '→ ' + info.xpNeeded.toLocaleString() + ' para nivel ' + (info.level + 1);

  const xpf = document.getElementById('pfXpFill');
  if (xpf) {
    xpf.style.width = pct + '%';
    xpf.style.background = `linear-gradient(90deg, ${rank.color}, ${rank.color}aa)`;
  }

  // Render active tab
  if (_pfCurrentTab === 'stats') renderPfStatsTab();
}

function renderPfStatsTab() {
  const profile = loadProfile();
  const info    = levelFromTotalXp(profile.totalXp);
  const st      = loadStats ? loadStats() : {};
  const sx      = loadStatsExt ? loadStatsExt() : {};
  const wr = st.totalGames > 0 ? Math.round((st.wins||0)/st.totalGames*100) : 0;

  const grid = document.getElementById('pfStatsGrid');
  if (!grid) return;

  const stats = [
    { val: st.totalGames || 0,      lbl: 'Partidas' },
    { val: (st.wins || 0),          lbl: 'Victorias' },
    { val: wr + '%',                lbl: 'Win Rate' },
    { val: sx.bestStreak || 0,      lbl: '⭐ Mejor racha' },
    { val: sx.perfectWins || 0,     lbl: '💎 Perfectas' },
    { val: sx.tournamentWins || 0,  lbl: '🏆 Torneos' },
    { val: info.level,              lbl: '🎮 Nivel' },
    { val: profile.totalXp.toLocaleString(), lbl: '⚡ XP total' },
    { val: (sx.fastestWin || '—') + (sx.fastestWin ? 's' : ''), lbl: '⚡ Victoria rápida' },
  ];

  grid.innerHTML = stats.map(s =>
    `<div class="pf-stat-box">
      <div class="pf-stat-val">${s.val}</div>
      <div class="pf-stat-lbl">${s.lbl}</div>
    </div>`
  ).join('');

  // XP history
  const hist = document.getElementById('pfXpHistory');
  if (hist && profile.gamesHistory && profile.gamesHistory.length) {
    hist.innerHTML = `<div style="font-size:.6rem;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);letter-spacing:2px;text-transform:uppercase;margin-bottom:6px;">Últimas partidas</div>`
      + profile.gamesHistory.slice(0,10).map(h =>
        `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;padding:4px 8px;
          background:rgba(255,255,255,.03);border-radius:6px;margin-bottom:3px;
          font-size:.72rem;color:rgba(255,255,255,.55);">
          <span>${new Date(h.date).toLocaleDateString('es')}</span>
          <span style="color:var(--gold);font-weight:800;">+${h.xp} XP</span>
        </div>`
      ).join('');
  }
}

function renderAvatarTab() {
  const container = document.getElementById('avatarCategoriesContainer');
  if (!container) return;

  container.innerHTML = AVATAR_CATS.map(cat => `

          <div class="av-btn ${((_pfTempAvatar||profile.avatar)===av)?'selected':''}"
               onclick="selectAvatar('${av}', this)">${av}</div>
        `).join('')}
      </div>
    </div>
  `).join('');
}

function selectAvatar(av, btn) {
  _pfTempAvatar = av;
  document.querySelectorAll('.av-btn').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('selected'));
  if (btn) btn.classList.add('selected');
  // Live preview in hero
  const ha = document.getElementById('pfHeroAvatar');
  if (ha) ha.childNodes[0].textContent = av;
  const pcA = document.getElementById('pcAvatar');
  if (pcA) pcA.textContent = av;
  try { sfxButton && sfxButton(); } catch(e) {}
}

function saveProfileAvatar() {
  if (!_pfTempAvatar) return;
  const p = loadProfile();
  p.avatar = _pfTempAvatar;
  saveProfile(p);
  updateLeaderboard(p);
  updateProfileUI(p);
  showToast('✅ Avatar guardado: ' + _pfTempAvatar);
  try { sfxButton && sfxButton(); } catch(e) {}
}

  const p = loadProfile();

            style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:50%;background:${c};
                   cursor:pointer;border:2px solid ${c===p.color?'#fff':'transparent'};
                   transition:transform .15s;"
            title="${c}"></div>`
    ).join('');
  }
}

  saveProfile(p);
  const hn = document.getElementById('pfHeroName');
  if (hn) hn.style.color = color;
  const pcn = document.getElementById('pcName');
  if (pcn) pcn.style.color = color;
}

  saveProfile(p);
  updateLeaderboard(p);
  updateProfileUI(p);
  renderProfileModal(p);
  showToast('✅ Perfil guardado: ' + nick);
  try { sfxButton && sfxButton(); } catch(e) {}
}

function confirmResetProfile() {
  if (confirm('¿Reiniciar tu perfil? Se perderá todo tu XP y nivel. Las estadísticas de juego NO se borran.')) {
    const fresh = defaultProfile();
    fresh.id = loadProfile().id;
    saveProfile(fresh);
    updateProfileUI(fresh);
    renderProfileModal(fresh);
    showToast('🔄 Perfil reiniciado');
  }
}

function renderLeaderboardTab() {
  const container = document.getElementById('leaderboardList');
  if (!container) return;
  const lb      = loadLeaderboard();
  const profile = loadProfile();

  if (!lb.length) {
    container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);padding:20px;font-size:.8rem;">Aún no hay entradas.<br>¡Juega tu primera partida!</div>';
    return;
  }

  const medals = ['🥇','🥈','🥉'];
  const rankCls = ['gold','silver','bronze'];

  container.innerHTML = lb.map((entry, i) => {
    const info = levelFromTotalXp(entry.totalXp || 0);
    const rank = getRank(info.level);
    const isMe = entry.nickname === profile.nickname;
    const pos  = i + 1;
    return `
      <div class="lb-row ${isMe ? 'lb-me' : ''}">
        <div class="lb-rank ${rankCls[i]||''}">${medals[i] || '#'+pos}</div>
        <div class="lb-avatar">${entry.avatar || '🎮'}</div>
        <div class="lb-info">
          <div class="lb-name" style="color:${entry.color||'#fff'}">${entry.nickname}${isMe?' (Tú)':''}</div>
          <div class="lb-sub">Nv.${info.level} · ${rank.name}${entry.prestige?` · ✦${entry.prestige}`:''}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="lb-score">${(entry.totalXp||0).toLocaleString()} XP</div>
      </div>`;
  }).join('');
}

/* ── PATCH endGame to award XP ── */
(function patchEndGameForXp() {
  const _orig = window.endGame;
  if (typeof _orig !== 'function') return;
  window.endGame = function(playerWon) {
    _orig.call(this, playerWon);
    // Award XP after a short delay (so result screen shows first)
    setTimeout(() => {
      try {
        const timeSec  = Math.round((Date.now() - (window.gameStartTime||Date.now())) / 1000);
        const sx       = loadStatsExt ? loadStatsExt() : {};
        const isPerfect  = (window.pDraws || 0) === 0 && playerWon;
        const isComeback = playerWon && (player ? player.length + (window.pDraws||0) >= 10 : false);
        const xpResult = calcXpGain(
          playerWon,
          window.turns || 10,
          window.pDraws || 0,
          timeSec,
          window.currentDiff || 'normal',
          window.currentMode || 'clasico',
          isPerfect,
          isComeback
        );
        addXpToProfile(xpResult.total, xpResult.breakdown);
      } catch(e) { console.warn('XP award error:', e); }
    }, 600);
  };
})();

/* ── PATCH showMenu to refresh profile UI ── */
(function() {
  const _orig = window.showMenu;
  window.showMenu = function() {
    if (typeof _orig === 'function') _orig.apply(this, arguments);
    setTimeout(() => {
      updateProfileUI(loadProfile());
      if (typeof renderMenuStats === 'function') renderMenuStats();
    }, 80);
  };
})();

/* ── INIT on load ── */
(function initProfile() {
  const p = loadProfile();
  if (!p.id) { p.id = Date.now().toString(36); saveProfile(p); }
  updateLeaderboard(p);
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    setTimeout(() => updateProfileUI(p), 200);
  });
  // Also try immediately
  updateProfileUI(p);
})();

})();

/* ─────────── DAILY CHALLENGE ENGINE ─────────────────────────── */
const DAILY_RULE_POOL = [
  { id:'no_draw',      icon:'🚫', name:'Sin Robar',        desc:'No puedes robar cartas. ¡Juega con lo que tienes!',
    apply: () => { window._dailyNoRobar = true; } },
  { id:'speed',        icon:'⏱️',  name:'Contrarreloj',     desc:'Cada turno tiene solo 15 segundos.',
    apply: () => { window._dailySpeed = true; window._dailySpeedSec = 15; } },
  { id:'double_draw',  icon:'✌️',  name:'Doble Robo',       desc:'Al robar, tomas 2 cartas en vez de 1.',
    apply: () => { window._dailyDoubleDraw = true; } },
  { id:'mirror',       icon:'🪞',  name:'Modo Espejo',      desc:'La IA empieza con tus mismas cartas.',
    apply: () => { window._dailyMirror = true; } },
  { id:'bonus_8',      icon:'🎱',  name:'Super Ocho',       desc:'Los ochos comodín te dan un turno extra.',
    apply: () => { window._dailyBonus8 = true; } },
  { id:'no_pass',      icon:'🔒',  name:'Sin Pasar',        desc:'No puedes pasar turno: siempre juega o roba.',
    apply: () => { window._dailyNoPass = true; } },
  { id:'last_card',    icon:'🃏',  name:'Última Carta',     desc:'Comienzas con 1 sola carta (gana sin robar para bonus).',
    apply: () => { window._dailyLastCard = true; } },
  { id:'wild_only',    icon:'🌀',  name:'Solo Comodines',   desc:'Solo puedes jugar cartas especiales (8, A, 2, 3, 10).',
    apply: () => { window._dailyWildOnly = true; } },
];

function getDailySeed() {
  const d = new Date();
  return d.getFullYear() * 10000 + (d.getMonth()+1) * 100 + d.getDate();
}

function seededRand(seed, max) {
  let x = Math.sin(seed + 1) * 10000;
  return Math.floor((x - Math.floor(x)) * max);
}

function getTodayRules() {
  const seed = getDailySeed();
  const n    = 2; // 2 rules per day
  const rules = [];
  const used  = new Set();
  for (let i = 0; i < n; i++) {
    let idx;
    do { idx = seededRand(seed + i * 37, DAILY_RULE_POOL.length); } while (used.has(idx));
    used.add(idx);
    rules.push(DAILY_RULE_POOL[idx]);
  }
  return rules;
}

function renderDailyCard() {
  const panel = document.getElementById('dailyCardInfo');
  if (!panel) return;
  const rules = getTodayRules();
  const d = new Date();
  const dateStr = d.toLocaleDateString('es-ES', {weekday:'long', day:'numeric', month:'long'});
  let html = `<div class="dc-title">📅 Desafío del ${dateStr}</div>`;
  rules.forEach(r => {
    html += `<div class="dc-rule"><span class="dc-icon">${r.icon}</span>
             <strong>${r.name}</strong>: ${r.desc}</div>`;
  });
  html += `<div style="margin-top:6px;font-size:.7rem;color:#ffaa00;opacity:.8">
           ⭐ Bonus XP +80 si completas el desafío hoy</div>`;
  panel.innerHTML = html;
}

function applyDailyRules() {
  // Reset all daily flags
  window._dailyNoRobar = window._dailySpeed = window._dailyDoubleDraw = false;
  window._dailyMirror  = window._dailyBonus8 = window._dailyNoPass   = false;
  window._dailyLastCard = window._dailyWildOnly = false;
  if (currentMode !== 'diario') return;
  getTodayRules().forEach(r => r.apply());
}

function checkDailyCompleted() {
  const seed = getDailySeed();
  const key  = 'ol_daily_v14';
  const rec  = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(key) || '{}');
  return rec.seed === seed && rec.won;
}

function markDailyCompleted() {
  const key = 'ol_daily_v14';
  const seed = getDailySeed();
  localStorage.setItem(key, JSON.stringify({ seed, won: true, date: new Date().toISOString() }));
}

/* ─────────── PRACTICE MODE ─────────────────────────────────── */
let pracAiLevel = 30; // 1-100

const PRAC_LABELS = [
  {min:1,  max:15,  icon:'😴', label:'Novato',       diff:'facil'},
  {min:16, max:35,  icon:'😊', label:'Principiante', diff:'facil'},
  {min:36, max:55,  icon:'🙂', label:'Intermedio',   diff:'normal'},
  {min:56, max:72,  icon:'😐', label:'Avanzado',     diff:'normal'},
  {min:73, max:85,  icon:'😤', label:'Difícil',      diff:'dificil'},
  {min:86, max:95,  icon:'🤖', label:'Experto',      diff:'experto'},
  {min:96, max:100, icon:'💀', label:'Maestro',      diff:'experto'},
];

function getPracLabel(v) {
  return PRAC_LABELS.find(l => v >= l.min && v <= l.max) || PRAC_LABELS[2];
}

function updatePracSlider(v) {
  v = parseInt(v);
  pracAiLevel = v;
  const slider = document.getElementById('pracSlider');
  const lbl    = document.getElementById('pracAiLabel');
  if (slider) { slider.value = v; slider.style.setProperty('--pct', v + '%'); }
  const entry = getPracLabel(v);
  if (lbl) lbl.textContent = `${entry.icon} Nivel ${v} – ${entry.label}`;
}

function getPracDiff() {
  return getPracLabel(pracAiLevel).diff;
}

function buildPracticeHint(playedCard, aiSuggestion) {
  const hint = document.getElementById('practiceHint');
  if (!hint || currentMode !== 'practica') return;
  hint.style.display = 'block';
  hint.innerHTML = aiSuggestion
    ? `💡 <strong>Consejo IA:</strong> ${aiSuggestion}`
    : `✅ ¡Buena jugada! Jugaste ${playedCard?.v}${playedCard?.s}`;
  setTimeout(() => { hint.style.display = 'none'; }, 3000);
}

function getAiPracticeHint() {
  // Suggest best playable card to player
  const playable = player.filter(c => isPlayable(c));
  if (!playable.length) return 'No tienes cartas válidas. Roba una.';
  // Prefer special cards, then same suit
  const sp = playable.filter(c => ['8','A','2','3','10'].includes(c.v));
  const best = sp.length ? sp[0] : playable[0];
  return `Considera jugar <strong>${best.v}${best.s}</strong> — es tu mejor opción ahora.`;
}

/* ─────────── COOPERATIVE MODE ──────────────────────────────── */
let coopMode    = false;
let coopPartner = []; // partner's hand (human teammate)
let coopAi1     = []; // first AI opponent
let coopAi2     = []; // second AI opponent
let coopTurn    = 0;  // 0=player, 1=partner, 2=ai1, 3=ai2
let coopTeamWins = 0;
let coopAiWins   = 0;
const COOP_PLAYERS = ['🟢 Tú', '🔵 Compañero', '🔴 IA-1', '🔴 IA-2'];

function updateCoopHud() {
  const hud = document.getElementById('coopHud');
  if (!hud) return;
  hud.style.display = 'flex';
  hud.style.flexDirection = 'column';
  hud.style.alignItems = 'center';
  const names  = COOP_PLAYERS;
  const counts = [player.length, coopPartner.length, coopAi1.length, coopAi2.length];
  let html = `<div style="font-size:.7rem;margin-bottom:2px">🤝 COOPERATIVO – Turno: <strong>${names[coopTurn]}</strong></div>`;
  html += '<div class="coop-team">';
  names.forEach((n,i) => {
    const active = (i === coopTurn) ? ' active' : '';
    const team   = i < 2 ? '(Equipo)' : '(IA)';
    html += `<div class="coop-player${active}">${n} ${team} · ${counts[i]} cartas</div>`;
  });
  html += '</div>';
  hud.innerHTML = html;
}

async function coopAiPlay(hand, label) {
  const diff  = DIFFICULTIES[currentDiff];
  await wait(diff.thinkDelay * 0.7);
  // Find playable card
  const plays = hand.filter(c => isPlayable(c));
  if (!plays.length) {
    if (deck.length) {
      const drawn = deck.pop();
      hand.push(drawn);
      setStatus(`${label} robó una carta`);
      playSound('draw', 0.5);
    } else {
      setStatus(`${label} pasa`);
    }
    return;
  }
  // Simple AI: prefer special, then suit match
  const special = plays.filter(c => ['8','A','2','3','10'].includes(c.v));
  const chosen  = special.length ? special[0] : plays[0];
  hand.splice(hand.indexOf(chosen), 1);
  discard.push(chosen);
  currentSuit = chosen.s;
  playSound('place', 0.65);
  setStatus(`${label} jugó ${chosen.v}${chosen.s}`);
  if (chosen.v === '8') {
    // AI chooses suit with most cards
    const sc = {'♠':0,'♥':0,'♦':0,'♣':0};
    hand.forEach(c => { if(sc[c.s]!==undefined) sc[c.s]++; });
    currentSuit = Object.entries(sc).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1])[0][0];
  }
  // Check if this AI won
  if (hand.length === 0) {
    endGame(false); // AI team wins = player loses
    return;
  }
  updateUI();
}

async function coopNextTurn() {
  if (gameOver) return;
  coopTurn = (coopTurn + 1) % 4;
  updateCoopHud();
  if (coopTurn === 0) {
    // Player's turn
    playerTurn = true;
    drawnThisTurn = 0;
    setStatus('¡Tu turno! Selecciona carta(s)');
    updateUI(); updateDrawBtn();
  } else if (coopTurn === 1) {
    // Partner AI turn (acts like helpful AI)
    playerTurn = false;
    setStatus('Turno de tu compañero...');
    await coopAiPlay(coopPartner, '🔵 Compañero');
    if (!gameOver) {
      if (coopPartner.length === 0) { endGame(true); return; }
      coopNextTurn();
    }
  } else if (coopTurn === 2) {
    playerTurn = false;
    setStatus('Turno de IA-1...');
    await coopAiPlay(coopAi1, '🔴 IA-1');
    if (!gameOver) {
      if (coopAi1.length === 0) { endGame(false); return; }
      coopNextTurn();
    }
  } else if (coopTurn === 3) {
    playerTurn = false;
    setStatus('Turno de IA-2...');
    await coopAiPlay(coopAi2, '🔴 IA-2');
    if (!gameOver) {
      if (coopAi2.length === 0) { endGame(false); return; }
      coopNextTurn();
    }
  }
}

/* ─────────── PATCH startGame for new modes ─────────────────── */
const _v14OrigStartGame = window.startGame;

async function startGame() {
  // Reset all daily flags
  applyDailyRules();
  // Reset cooperative
  coopMode = false;
  coopPartner = []; coopAi1 = []; coopAi2 = [];
  coopTurn = 0;
  const coopH = document.getElementById('coopHud');
  if (coopH) coopH.style.display = 'none';
  const pHint = document.getElementById('practiceHint');
  if (pHint) pHint.style.display = 'none';

  if (currentMode === 'cooperativo') {
    await startCoopGame();
    return;
  }
  if (currentMode === 'practica') {
    // Override diff with practice slider diff
    const origDiff = currentDiff;
    currentDiff = getPracDiff();
    await _v14OrigStartGame();
    currentDiff = origDiff;
    // Show hint after a brief delay
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (!gameOver) buildPracticeHint(null, getAiPracticeHint());
    }, 1500);
    return;
  }
  if (currentMode === 'diario') {
    // Apply daily rule visual
    const rules = getTodayRules();
    const ruleNames = rules.map(r => r.icon + ' ' + r.name).join(' · ');
    await _v14OrigStartGame();
    showToast(`📅 Reglas de hoy: ${ruleNames}`, 4000);
    return;
  }
  await _v14OrigStartGame();
}

async function startCoopGame() {
  coopMode = true;
  deck=[]; player=[]; ai=[]; discard=[];
  coopPartner=[]; coopAi1=[]; coopAi2=[];
  turns=0; pDraws=0; aiDraws=0; drawnThisTurn=0;
  playerTurn=false; gameOver=false;
  selectedIndices=[]; firstCardIsEight=false;

  document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.remove('hidden');
  document.getElementById('drawBtn').disabled = true;
  document.getElementById('playBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('passBtn').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('drawInfo').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('suitInd').style.display  = 'none';
  document.getElementById('modeBadge').textContent   = '🤝 Cooperativo';
  document.getElementById('mpScoreBar').style.display = 'none';
  document.getElementById('diffBadge').style.display = '';
  document.getElementById('opponentLabel').textContent = '🔴 Equipo IA';

  // Build deck
  for (const s of SUITS) for (const v of VALS) deck.push({s,v});
  deck.sort(() => Math.random() - .5);
  gameStartTime = Date.now();
  mpAccumDraw=0; mpAccumType=null; mpSilenceOn=false;

  // Deal 8 cards to each of 4 "players"
  setStatus('Repartiendo cartas...');
  const hands = [player, coopPartner, coopAi1, coopAi2];
  for (let i=0; i<8; i++) {
    for (const h of hands) {
      h.push(deck.pop());
      playSound('deal', 0.45);
      await wait(45);
    }
  }

  // First discard
  let first;
  do { first = deck.pop(); } while (first.v === '8');
  discard.push(first);
  currentSuit = first.s;
  playSound('place', 0.75);

  coopTurn = 0;
  updateCoopHud();
  playerTurn = true;
  drawnThisTurn = 0;
  setStatus('🤝 ¡COOPERATIVO! Tu turno. Selecciona carta(s)');
  updateUI(); updateDrawBtn();
}

/* ─────────── PATCH endGame for cooperative/daily/practice ─── */
const _v14OrigEndGame = window.endGame;

function endGame(playerWon) {
  if (currentMode === 'cooperativo') {
    if (playerWon) coopTeamWins++; else coopAiWins++;
    const coopH = document.getElementById('coopHud');
    if (coopH) coopH.style.display = 'none';
  }
  if (currentMode === 'diario' && playerWon && !checkDailyCompleted()) {
    markDailyCompleted();
    // Add bonus XP
    setTimeout(() => {
      addXpToProfile({ xp: 80, label: '📅 Desafío Diario completado (+80 XP)' });
      showToast('🏅 ¡Desafío Diario completado! +80 XP bonus', 4000);
    }, 1200);
  }
  if (currentMode === 'practica') {
    const pHint = document.getElementById('practiceHint');
    if (pHint) pHint.style.display = 'none';
    // Don't save score in practice mode, but show result
  }
  _v14OrigEndGame(playerWon);
}

/* ─────────── PATCH playSelected for daily rules ─────────────── */
const _v14OrigPlaySelected = window.playSelected;

function playSelected() {
  // Daily: wild only rule
  if (window._dailyWildOnly && selectedIndices.length) {
    const special = ['8','A','2','3','10'];
    const ok = selectedIndices.every(i => special.includes(player[i].v));
    if (!ok) {
      showToast('🌀 Solo Comodines: solo puedes jugar cartas especiales (8,A,2,3,10)', 2500);
      return;
    }
  }
  _v14OrigPlaySelected();
  // Practice mode hint after play
  if (currentMode === 'practica' && !gameOver) {
    setTimeout(() => buildPracticeHint(null, getAiPracticeHint()), 600);
  }
  // Cooperative: after player plays, advance to next coop turn
  if (coopMode && !gameOver && !playerTurn) {
    coopNextTurn();
  }
}

/* ─────────── PATCH drawCard for daily rules ─────────────────── */
const _v14OrigDrawCard = window.drawCard;

function drawCard() {
  if (window._dailyNoRobar) {
    showToast('🚫 Sin Robar: no puedes robar cartas hoy', 2000);
    return;
  }
  _v14OrigDrawCard();
  // Double draw daily rule
  if (window._dailyDoubleDraw && !gameOver && deck.length > 0) {
    const extra = deck.pop();
    player.push(extra);
    pDraws++;
    setStatus(`✌️ Doble Robo: robaste 2 cartas (${extra.v}${extra.s} extra)`);
    updateUI();
  }
  // Practice hint
  if (currentMode === 'practica' && !gameOver) {
    setTimeout(() => buildPracticeHint(null, getAiPracticeHint()), 400);
  }
}

/* ─────────── DAILY SPEED TIMER ─────────────────────────────── */
let _dailyTimerInterval = null;
let _dailyTimerLeft = 15;

function startDailySpeedTimer() {
  if (!window._dailySpeed || !playerTurn) return;
  clearDailyTimer();
  _dailyTimerLeft = window._dailySpeedSec || 15;
  const bar = document.getElementById('statusBar');
  _dailyTimerInterval = setInterval(() => {
    _dailyTimerLeft--;
    if (bar) bar.textContent = `⏱️ ${_dailyTimerLeft}s restantes — ¡Juega rápido!`;
    if (_dailyTimerLeft <= 0) {
      clearDailyTimer();
      // Force draw card as penalty
      if (!gameOver && playerTurn) {
        showToast('⏱️ ¡Tiempo! Robas una carta de penalización', 1500);
        if (deck.length) { player.push(deck.pop()); pDraws++; updateUI(); }
        // End player turn
        playerTurn = false;
        setTimeout(() => { if(!gameOver) aiTurn(); }, 600);
      }
    }
  }, 1000);
}

function clearDailyTimer() {
  if (_dailyTimerInterval) { clearInterval(_dailyTimerInterval); _dailyTimerInterval = null; }
}

/* ─────────── PATCH startPlayerTurn for speed timer ─────────── */
const _v14OrigStartPlayerTurn = window.startPlayerTurn;

function startPlayerTurn() {
  if (_v14OrigStartPlayerTurn) _v14OrigStartPlayerTurn();
  if (currentMode === 'diario' && window._dailySpeed) {
    startDailySpeedTimer();
  }
}

/* ─────────── PATCH passTurn for daily no-pass rule ──────────── */
const _v14OrigPassTurn = window.passTurn;

function passTurn() {
  if (window._dailyNoPass) {
    showToast('🔒 Sin Pasar: debes jugar una carta o robar', 2000);
    return;
  }
  if (_v14OrigPassTurn) _v14OrigPassTurn();
}

/* ─────────── COOPERATIVE checkWin patch ────────────────────── */
const _v14OrigCheckWin = window.checkWin;

function checkWin() {
  if (coopMode) {
    // Win: player OR partner empties hand
    if (player.length === 0) { endGame(true); return; }
    if (coopPartner.length === 0) { endGame(true); return; }
    // Loss: any AI empties hand
    if (coopAi1.length === 0 || coopAi2.length === 0) { endGame(false); return; }
    return;
  }
  _v14OrigCheckWin();
}

/* ─────────── Show result patch for new modes ─────────────────── */
const _v14OrigShowResult = window.showResult;

function showResult(win, isTournament=false) {
  clearDailyTimer();
  if (currentMode === 'cooperativo') {
    const coopH = document.getElementById('coopHud');
    if (coopH) coopH.style.display = 'none';
  }
  _v14OrigShowResult(win, isTournament);
  // Update result sub for new modes
  if (currentMode === 'cooperativo') {
    const sub = document.getElementById('resSub');
    if (sub) sub.textContent = win
      ? `¡Equipo victoria! Tú + Compañero ganaron 🤝🏆`
      : `El equipo IA dominó el campo 🔴`;
  }
  if (currentMode === 'diario') {
    const rules = getTodayRules();
    const sub = document.getElementById('resSub');
    if (sub && win) sub.textContent = `¡Desafío Diario superado! ${rules.map(r=>r.icon).join('')} +80 XP`;
  }
  if (currentMode === 'practica') {
    const sub = document.getElementById('resSub');
    if (sub) sub.textContent = win
      ? `¡Buen trabajo practicando! Nivel IA: ${pracAiLevel}/100`
      : `Sigue practicando – Nivel IA: ${pracAiLevel}/100`;
  }
}

/* ─────────── ACHIEVEMENTS for new modes ────────────────────── */
// Add daily/coop/practice achievements check
const _v14OrigCheckAchievements = window.checkAchievements;

function checkAchievements(st, xe) {
  if (_v14OrigCheckAchievements) _v14OrigCheckAchievements(st, xe);
}

/* ─────────── Init: render daily card on page load ──────────── */
(function initNewModes() {
  // Render daily card info if the panel exists
  setTimeout(() => {
    renderDailyCard();
    updatePracSlider(30);
    // Show daily completed badge if already done today
    if (checkDailyCompleted()) {
      const btn = document.getElementById('mode-diario');
      if (btn) {
        const badge = btn.querySelector('.mode-new-badge');
        if (badge) { badge.textContent = '✅'; badge.style.background = '#2ecc71'; }
      }
    }
  }, 500);
})();

/* ─────────── RENDER cooperative hands in updateUI ─────────── */
const _v14OrigUpdateUI = window.updateUI;

function updateUI() {
  if (_v14OrigUpdateUI) _v14OrigUpdateUI();
  if (coopMode) {
    updateCoopHud();
    // Show partner's card count
    const opLbl = document.getElementById('opponentLabel');
    if (opLbl) opLbl.textContent = `🔴 IA-1(${coopAi1.length}) · IA-2(${coopAi2.length}) · 🔵 Comp(${coopPartner.length})`;
  }
}

/* ─────────── VERSION TAG ─────────────────────────────────── */
(function() {
  const vEls = document.querySelectorAll('[class*="version"], .logo-tag-v8, .footer-ver');
  vEls.forEach(el => {
    if (el.textContent.includes('v13') || el.textContent.includes('v14')) {
      el.textContent = el.textContent.replace(/v1[34]\.0/g, 'v19.0');
    }
  });
})();


/* ═══ APP NAVIGATION v19.0 ═══ */
function navTo(screen) {
  // Only home is reachable via bottom nav (game uses its own flow)
  sfxButton();
  if (screen === 'home') {
    // If in game, confirm
    if (!gameOver && document.getElementById('gameScreen').classList.contains('active')) {
      if (!confirm('¿Salir de la partida actual?')) return;
    }
    showMenu();
  }
}

// Sync bottom nav avatar with profile
function syncBottomNav() {
  const prof = loadProfile();
  const avatarEl = document.getElementById('bnavAvatar');
  if (avatarEl && prof && prof.avatar) avatarEl.textContent = prof.avatar;
}

// Sync achievement badge on bottom nav
function syncBnavBadge() {
  const badge = document.getElementById('bnavBadge');
  const mainBadge = document.getElementById('achievBadge');
  if (badge && mainBadge) {
    const n = mainBadge.textContent;
    const show = mainBadge.style.display !== 'none' && n !== '0';
    badge.style.display = show ? 'flex' : 'none';
    badge.textContent = n;
  }
}

// Override updateAchievBadge to also sync bottom nav
const _origUpdateAchievBadge = window.updateAchievBadge;
function updateAchievBadge(n) {
  if (_origUpdateAchievBadge) _origUpdateAchievBadge(n);
  syncBnavBadge();
}

// Override openProfileModal to sync nav
const _origOpenProfileModal = window.openProfileModal;
function openProfileModal() {
  if (_origOpenProfileModal) _origOpenProfileModal();
  // Mark profile nav item active
  document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const pb = document.getElementById('bnav-perfil');
  if (pb) pb.classList.add('active');
}
const _origCloseProfileModal = window.closeProfileModal;
function closeProfileModal() {
  if (_origCloseProfileModal) _origCloseProfileModal();
  // Restore home nav
  document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b=>b.classList.remove('active'));
  const hb = document.getElementById('bnav-home');
  if (hb) hb.classList.add('active');
}

// Init on load
(function appInit() {
  setTimeout(() => {
    syncBottomNav();
    syncBnavBadge();
    // Ensure homeScreen visible on load
    const hs = document.getElementById('homeScreen');
    const gs = document.getElementById('gameScreen');
    if (hs) hs.classList.add('active');
    if (gs) gs.classList.remove('active');
    const bn = document.getElementById('bottomNav');
    if (bn) bn.style.display = 'flex';
  }, 200);
})();

        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">2️⃣</span>
          <span><strong>Dos →</strong> El rival roba 2 cartas y pierde el turno.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">J/Q</span>
          <span><strong>J ó Q →</strong> Salta el turno del rival. ¡Juegas de nuevo!</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🔟</span>
          <span><strong>10 →</strong> Invierte el orden de turnos (en multijugador).</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🅰️</span>
          <span><strong>As (A) →</strong> El rival debe responder con un As o robar 3 cartas.</span>

      demo: null,
      reward: null,
    },

    /* ─── 10 · ROBAR CARTAS ─── */
    {
      id: 'draw_card',
      title: 'Robar Cartas',
      icon: '🃏',
      target: 'drawBtn',
      position: 'top',
      arrow: 'bottom',
      content: `
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🚫</span>
          <span>Solo puedes robar si <strong>no tienes ninguna carta válida</strong> para jugar.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🃏</span>

        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">⚠️</span>
          <span>Cada modo tiene un límite de robos por turno (Relámpago: 1, Clásico: 3).</span>
        </div>`,
      demo: null,
      reward: null,
    },

    /* ─── 11 · PASAR TURNO ─── */
    {
      id: 'pass_turn',

      demo: null,
      reward: null,
    },

    /* ─── 12 · LOGROS Y XP ─── */
    {
      id: 'achievements',
      title: 'Logros y Experiencia',
      icon: '🏅',
      target: null,
      position: 'center',
      arrow: 'none',
      content: `
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">⭐</span>
          <span>Cada partida te da <strong>XP</strong>. Acumula XP para subir de nivel y desbloquear rangos.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🏅</span>
          <span>Hay <strong>47 logros</strong> en 6 categorías: Básicos, Rachas, Maestría, Modos, Gestas y Cartas.</span>
        </div>
        <div class="tut-rule-row"><span class="tut-rule-icon">🔥</span>
          <span>Completa rachas de victorias para logros especiales y bonus de XP.</span>
        </div>`,
      reward: { icon: '🎓', text: '¡Tutorial completado! +50 XP bonus desbloqueado' },
      demo: null,
      actionBtn: null,
    },

  ]; // end STEPS

  const TOTAL = STEPS.length;

  /* ══════════════ HELPERS ════════════════════════════════════════════════ */

  function getEl(id) { return document.getElementById(id); }

  function saveProgress(idx) {
    try { localStorage.setItem(LS_KEY, JSON.stringify({ step: idx, ts: Date.now() })); } catch(e){}
  }

  function loadProgress() {
    try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(LS_KEY) || 'null'); } catch(e){ return null; }
  }

  function markDone() {
    try { localStorage.setItem(LS_DONE, '1'); } catch(e){}
    // Hide the "new" dot on trigger btn
    const dot = document.getElementById('tutNewDot');
    if (dot) dot.style.display = 'none';
  }

  function isDone() {
    try { return localStorage.getItem(LS_DONE) === '1'; } catch(e){ return false; }
  }

  /* ══════════════ SPOTLIGHT / HIGHLIGHT ════════════════════════════════ */

  function getTargetRect(step) {
    const candidates = [step.target, step.targetFallback].filter(Boolean);
    for (const sel of candidates) {
      let el = null;
      if (typeof sel === 'string') {
        el = document.getElementById(sel) || document.querySelector(sel);
      }
      if (el) {
        const r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
        const frame = getEl('appFrame');
        const fr = frame ? frame.getBoundingClientRect() : {top:0,left:0};
        return {
          top:    r.top    - fr.top,
          left:   r.left   - fr.left,
          width:  r.width,
          height: r.height,
          el: el
        };
      }
    }
    return null;
  }

  function updateHighlight(step) {
    const hl = getEl('tutHighlight');
    if (!hl) return;
    if (!step.target) { hl.className = 'tut-hl-none'; return; }
    const rect = getTargetRect(step);
    if (!rect) { hl.className = 'tut-hl-none'; return; }
    const pad = 7;
    hl.className = 'tut-highlight';
    hl.style.top    = (rect.top    - pad) + 'px';
    hl.style.left   = (rect.left   - pad) + 'px';
    hl.style.width  = (rect.width  + pad*2) + 'px';
    hl.style.height = (rect.height + pad*2) + 'px';
  }

  function updateSVGSpotlight(step) {
    const svg = getEl('tutSpotlight');
    if (!svg) return;
    const frame = getEl('appFrame');
    if (!frame) return;
    const fw = frame.offsetWidth, fh = frame.offsetHeight;
    svg.setAttribute('width', fw);
    svg.setAttribute('height', fh);
    svg.setAttribute('viewBox', `0 0 ${fw} ${fh}`);

    if (!step.target) {
      svg.innerHTML = '';
      return;
    }
    const rect = getTargetRect(step);
    if (!rect) { svg.innerHTML = ''; return; }
    const pad = 10, rx = 14;
    const x = rect.left - pad, y = rect.top - pad;
    const w = rect.width + pad*2, h = rect.height + pad*2;

    svg.innerHTML = `
      <defs>
        <mask id="spotMask">
          <rect width="${fw}" height="${fh}" fill="white"/>
          <rect x="${x}" y="${y}" width="${w}" height="${h}" rx="${rx}" fill="black"/>
        </mask>
      </defs>
      <rect width="${fw}" height="${fh}" fill="rgba(0,0,0,0.68)" mask="url(#spotMask)"/>
    `;
  }

  /* ══════════════ TOOLTIP POSITIONING ══════════════════════════════════ */

  function positionTooltip(step) {
    const tt = getEl('tutTooltip');
    if (!tt) return;
    tt.style.display = 'block';
    tt.className = 'arrow-' + (step.arrow || 'none');

    const frame  = getEl('appFrame');
    const fw     = frame ? frame.offsetWidth  : 390;
    const fh     = frame ? frame.offsetHeight : 844;
    const tw     = tt.offsetWidth  || 300;
    const th     = tt.offsetHeight || 200;
    const margin = 12;

    let top, left;

    if (step.position === 'center' || !step.target) {
      left = (fw - tw) / 2;
      top  = (fh - th) / 2;
    } else {
      const rect = getTargetRect(step);
      if (!rect) {
        left = (fw - tw) / 2;
        top  = (fh - th) / 2;
      } else {
        switch (step.position) {
          case 'bottom':
            top  = rect.top + rect.height + 14;
            left = rect.left + rect.width/2 - tw/2;
            break;
          case 'top':
            top  = rect.top - th - 14;
            left = rect.left + rect.width/2 - tw/2;
            break;
          case 'left':
            top  = rect.top + rect.height/2 - th/2;
            left = rect.left - tw - 14;
            break;
          case 'right':
            top  = rect.top + rect.height/2 - th/2;
            left = rect.left + rect.width + 14;
            break;
          default:
            top  = (fh - th) / 2;
            left = (fw - tw) / 2;
        }
        // Clamp to frame
        left = Math.max(margin, Math.min(left, fw - tw - margin));
        top  = Math.max(margin + 60, Math.min(top, fh - th - margin - 70));
      }
    }

    tt.style.left = left + 'px';
    tt.style.top  = top  + 'px';
  }

  /* ══════════════ RENDER STEP ════════════════════════════════════════════ */

  function renderStep(idx) {
    const step = STEPS[idx];
    if (!step) return;
    saveProgress(idx);

    // Update SVG spotlight + highlight
    updateHighlight(step);
    updateSVGSpotlight(step);

    // Content
    const titleEl   = getEl('tutTitle');
    const contentEl = getEl('tutContent');
    const badgeEl   = getEl('tutStepBadge');
    const demoEl    = getEl('tutDemoArea');
    const rewardEl  = getEl('tutReward');
    const progFill  = getEl('tutProgressFill');
    const stepCount = getEl('tutStepCount');
    const prevBtn   = getEl('tutPrevBtn');
    const nextBtn   = getEl('tutNextBtn');

    if (titleEl)   titleEl.textContent   = step.title;
    if (badgeEl)   badgeEl.textContent   = `${step.icon || '📖'} Paso ${idx+1}`;
    if (contentEl) contentEl.innerHTML   = step.content || '';
    if (progFill)  progFill.style.width  = Math.round(((idx+1)/TOTAL)*100) + '%';
    if (stepCount) stepCount.textContent = `${idx+1} / ${TOTAL}`;

    // Demo area
    if (demoEl) {
      if (step.demo && step.demo.html) {
        demoEl.innerHTML = step.demo.html;
        demoEl.style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        demoEl.innerHTML = '';
        demoEl.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }

    // Reward badge
    if (rewardEl) {
      if (step.reward) {
        rewardEl.innerHTML = `<div class="tut-reward-badge">
          <span class="tut-reward-icon">${step.reward.icon}</span>
          <span class="tut-reward-text">${step.reward.text}</span>
        </div>`;
        rewardEl.style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        rewardEl.innerHTML = '';
        rewardEl.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }

    // Buttons
    if (prevBtn) prevBtn.style.display = idx > 0 ? 'inline-flex' : 'none';
    if (nextBtn) {
      const isLast = (idx === TOTAL - 1);
      nextBtn.className = 'tut-btn ' + (isLast ? 'tut-btn-finish' : 'tut-btn-next');
      nextBtn.textContent = isLast ? '🎉 ¡Empezar a jugar!' : 'Siguiente →';
      nextBtn.onclick = isLast ? () => Tutorial.finish() : () => Tutorial.next();
    }

    // Position tooltip after brief delay (to let DOM settle)
    setTimeout(() => positionTooltip(step), 30);
  }

  /* ══════════════ PUBLIC API ═════════════════════════════════════════════ */

  function showOverlay() {
    const ov = getEl('tutorialOverlay');
    if (ov) { ov.classList.add('tut-active'); ov.style.pointerEvents = 'all'; }
  }

  function hideOverlay() {
    const ov = getEl('tutorialOverlay');
    if (ov) { ov.classList.remove('tut-active'); ov.style.pointerEvents = 'none'; }
    const tt = getEl('tutTooltip');
    if (tt) tt.style.display = 'none';
    const hl = getEl('tutHighlight');
    if (hl) hl.className = 'tut-hl-none';
    const svg = getEl('tutSpotlight');
    if (svg) svg.innerHTML = '';
  }

  return {

    showWelcome() {
      const w = getEl('tutWelcome');
      if (w) w.classList.add('open');
    },

    skipWelcome() {
      const w = getEl('tutWelcome');
      if (w) w.classList.remove('open');
      markDone();
    },

    start() {
      const w = getEl('tutWelcome');
      if (w) w.classList.remove('open');
      active = true;
      stepIndex = 0;
      showOverlay();
      renderStep(0);
    },

    resume() {
      const prog = loadProgress();
      const idx  = (prog && prog.step < TOTAL) ? prog.step : 0;
      active = true;
      stepIndex = idx;
      showOverlay();
      renderStep(idx);
    },

    next() {
      if (!active) return;
      if (stepIndex < TOTAL - 1) {
        stepIndex++;
        renderStep(stepIndex);
      } else {
        Tutorial.finish();
      }
    },

    prev() {
      if (!active || stepIndex <= 0) return;
      stepIndex--;
      renderStep(stepIndex);
    },

    skip() {
      if (confirm('¿Salir del tutorial? Puedes retomarlo desde el menú principal.')) {
        Tutorial.finish(false);
      }
    },

    finish(giveReward = true) {
      active = false;
      hideOverlay();
      markDone();
      if (giveReward) {
        // +50 XP bonus for completing tutorial
        setTimeout(() => {
          if (typeof addXpToProfile === 'function') {
            addXpToProfile({ xp: 50, label: '🎓 Tutorial completado (+50 XP)' });
          }
          if (typeof showToast === 'function') {
            showToast('🎓 ¡Tutorial completado! +50 XP · ¡A jugar!', 4000);
          }
          // Unlock first_game achievement prep
          if (typeof checkAchievements === 'function') {
            try { checkAchievements(null, null); } catch(e){}
          }
        }, 300);
      }
    },

    handleBackdropClick() {
      // Allow click-through on spotlight hole, block otherwise
    },

    /* Auto-show on first visit */
    autoCheck() {
      if (!isDone()) {
        setTimeout(() => Tutorial.showWelcome(), 900);
      } else {
        // Hide dot on trigger btn
        const dot = document.getElementById('tutNewDot');
        if (dot) dot.style.display = 'none';
      }
    },

    get isActive() { return active; },

  };

})();

/* ── Auto-check on page load ── */
(function() {
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => setTimeout(Tutorial.autoCheck, 1200));
  } else {
    setTimeout(Tutorial.autoCheck, 1200);
  }
})();

  const DECK_CATALOG = [

      price: 380, cssClass: 'deck-ice', icon: '❄️', rarity: 'epic',
      pattern: 'linear-gradient(135deg,#003366,#00bfff,#87ceeb)',
    },
  ];

  const THEME_CATALOG = [
    {
      id: 'casino', name: 'Casino Noche', desc: 'Clásico del casino',
      price: 0, bodyClass: '', icon: '🎰', rarity: 'free',

    },
