    },
    {
      id: 'sunset', name: 'Atardecer', desc: 'Calor del ocaso',
      price: 200, bodyClass: 'theme-sunset', icon: '🌅', rarity: 'uncommon',
      colors: ['#1a0a00','#3d1506','#f97316'],
    },
    {
      id: 'neon_city', name: 'Ciudad Neón', desc: 'Noche electrónica',
      price: 400, bodyClass: 'theme-neon', icon: '🌃', rarity: 'epic',
      colors: ['#050510','#0a0a20','#0ff'],
    },
    {
      id: 'royal', name: 'Real Púrpura', desc: 'Majestad total',
      price: 300, bodyClass: 'theme-royal', icon: '🔮', rarity: 'rare',
      colors: ['#0f0a1e','#1a0f3d','#c084fc'],
    },
    {
      id: 'forest', name: 'Bosque', desc: 'Paz natural',
      price: 280, bodyClass: 'theme-forest', icon: '🌲', rarity: 'rare',
      colors: ['#0a1a0a','#0f2e0f','#4ade80'],
    },
  ];

  /* Rarity display colors */
  const RARITY_COLOR = {
    free:      '#9ca3af',
    uncommon:  '#4ade80',
    rare:      '#60a5fa',
    epic:      '#c084fc',
    legendary: '#ffd700',
  };

  /* ── PERSISTENCE ── */
  function loadShopData() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(LS_SHOP);
      const base = { owned: ['classic','casino'], equipped: {deck:'classic', theme:'casino'}, spent:0, earned:0 };
      return raw ? Object.assign(base, JSON.parse(raw)) : base;
    } catch(e) { return { owned:['classic','casino'], equipped:{deck:'classic',theme:'casino'}, spent:0, earned:0 }; }
  }
  function saveShopData(d) { localStorage.setItem(LS_SHOP, JSON.stringify(d)); }

  function loadCoins() {
    try { return parseInt(localStorage.getItem(LS_COINS)) || 0; } catch(e){ return 0; }
  }
  function saveCoins(n) { localStorage.setItem(LS_COINS, String(Math.max(0,n))); }

  /* ── COIN MANAGEMENT ── */
  window.getCoins = function() { return loadCoins(); };

  window.addCoins = function(amount, reason) {
    if (!amount || amount <= 0) return;
    const prev = loadCoins();
    const next = prev + amount;
    saveCoins(next);
    const sd = loadShopData();
    sd.earned = (sd.earned||0) + amount;
    saveShopData(sd);
    updateCoinDisplays();
    showCoinBurst(amount, reason);
    // Check for new shop items available
    checkShopNewBadge();
  };

  window.spendCoins = function(amount) {
    const bal = loadCoins();
    if (bal < amount) return false;
    saveCoins(bal - amount);
    const sd = loadShopData();
    sd.spent = (sd.spent||0) + amount;
    saveShopData(sd);
    updateCoinDisplays();
    return true;
  };

  /* ── UI UPDATES ── */
  function updateCoinDisplays() {
    const n = loadCoins();
    const els = ['coinAmount','shopCoinBalance','earnBalanceDisplay'];
    els.forEach(id => {
      const el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) el.textContent = n;
    });
    const spentEl = document.getElementById('earnSpentDisplay');
    const earnEl  = document.getElementById('earnEarnedDisplay');
    const sd = loadShopData();
    if (spentEl) spentEl.textContent = sd.spent || 0;
    if (earnEl)  earnEl.textContent  = sd.earned || 0;
  }

  function checkShopNewBadge() {
    const sd = loadShopData();
    const coins = loadCoins();
    const badge = document.getElementById('shopNewBadge');
    if (!badge) return;
    // Show badge if can afford something not owned
    const canBuy = [...DECK_CATALOG,...THEME_CATALOG].some(item =>
      item.price > 0 && item.price <= coins && !sd.owned.includes(item.id)
    );
    badge.style.display = canBuy ? 'flex' : 'none';
  }

  /* ── COIN BURST ANIMATION ── */
  function showCoinBurst(amount, reason) {
    const burst = document.createElement('div');
    burst.className = 'coin-burst';
    burst.textContent = '+' + amount + ' 🪙';
    // Position near coin display
    const coinEl = document.getElementById('coinDisplay');
    if (coinEl) {
      const rect = coinEl.getBoundingClientRect();
      burst.style.left = rect.left + 'px';
      burst.style.top  = (rect.top - 10) + 'px';
    } else {
      burst.style.left = '50%';
      burst.style.top  = '40%';
    }
    document.body.appendChild(burst);
    setTimeout(() => burst.remove(), 1000);
    // Also show toast
    showShopToast('🪙 +' + amount + (reason ? ' – ' + reason : ''));
  }

  /* ── SHOP OPEN/CLOSE ── */
  window.openShop = function() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('shopModal');
    if (!modal) return;
    modal.classList.add('open');
    // Mark shop nav active
    document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    const sb = document.getElementById('bnav-shop');
    if (sb) sb.classList.add('active');
    // Render
    updateCoinDisplays();
    renderShopDecks();
    renderShopThemes();
    shopSwitchTab('decks');
    // Hide new badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('shopNewBadge');
    if (badge) badge.style.display = 'none';
  };

  window.closeShop = function() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('shopModal');
    if (modal) modal.classList.remove('open');
    // Restore home nav
    document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    const hb = document.getElementById('bnav-home');
    if (hb) hb.classList.add('active');
  };

  /* ── TAB SWITCHER ── */
  window.shopSwitchTab = function(tab) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.shop-tab').forEach(t => t.classList.remove('active'));
    document.querySelectorAll('.shop-panel').forEach(p => p.classList.remove('active'));
    const tabEl = document.getElementById('stab-' + tab);
    const panEl = document.getElementById('spanel-' + tab);
    if (tabEl) tabEl.classList.add('active');
    if (panEl) panEl.classList.add('active');
    if (tab === 'earn') updateCoinDisplays();
  };

  /* ── RENDER DECKS ── */
  function renderShopDecks() {
    const grid = document.getElementById('shopDecksGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    const sd = loadShopData();
    const coins = loadCoins();
    const equippedDeck = sd.equipped && sd.equipped.deck ? sd.equipped.deck : 'classic';

    grid.innerHTML = DECK_CATALOG.map(item => {
      const owned    = sd.owned.includes(item.id);
      const equipped = equippedDeck === item.id;
      const canAfford = coins >= item.price;
      const rarityColor = RARITY_COLOR[item.rarity] || '#fff';

      let badgeHtml = '';
      if (equipped) badgeHtml = '<span class="shop-item-badge badge-equipped">✓ Equipado</span>';
      else if (owned) badgeHtml = '<span class="shop-item-badge badge-owned">✓ Tuyo</span>';

      let priceHtml = item.price === 0
        ? '<div class="shop-item-price"><span class="pi">🆓</span> Gratis</div>'
        : `<div class="shop-item-price"><span class="pi">🪙</span> ${item.price}</div>`;

      let btnHtml = '';
      if (equipped) {
        btnHtml = '<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-equipped" disabled>✓ Equipado</button>';
      } else if (owned) {
        btnHtml = `<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-equip" onclick="shopEquipDeck('${item.id}')">⚡ Equipar</button>`;
      } else {
        const dis = canAfford ? '' : 'disabled';
        const title = canAfford ? '' : `title="Necesitas ${item.price - coins} 🪙 más"`;
        btnHtml = `<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-buy" ${dis} ${title} onclick="shopBuyDeck('${item.id}')">${canAfford ? '💰 Comprar' : '🔒 ' + item.price + ' 🪙'}</button>`;
      }

      return `
        <div class="shop-item ${equipped?'equipped':(owned?'owned':'locked')}" id="sitem-deck-${item.id}">
          ${badgeHtml}
          <div class="shop-item-preview ${item.cssClass}">
            <span style="font-size:1.6rem;filter:drop-shadow(0 0 4px rgba(0,0,0,.8));">${item.icon}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="shop-item-name">${item.name}</div>
          <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color:${rarityColor}">${item.rarity.toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div class="shop-item-desc">${item.desc}</div>
          ${priceHtml}
          ${btnHtml}
        </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }

  /* ── RENDER THEMES ── */
  function renderShopThemes() {
    const grid = document.getElementById('shopThemesGrid');
    if (!grid) return;
    const sd = loadShopData();
    const coins = loadCoins();
    const equippedTheme = sd.equipped && sd.equipped.theme ? sd.equipped.theme : 'casino';

    grid.innerHTML = THEME_CATALOG.map(item => {
      const owned    = sd.owned.includes(item.id);
      const equipped = equippedTheme === item.id;
      const canAfford = coins >= item.price;
      const rarityColor = RARITY_COLOR[item.rarity] || '#fff';
      const [c1,c2,c3] = item.colors;

      let badgeHtml = '';
      if (equipped) badgeHtml = '<span class="shop-item-badge badge-equipped">✓ Activo</span>';
      else if (owned) badgeHtml = '<span class="shop-item-badge badge-owned">✓ Tuyo</span>';

      let priceHtml = item.price === 0
        ? '<div class="shop-item-price"><span class="pi">🆓</span> Gratis</div>'
        : `<div class="shop-item-price"><span class="pi">🪙</span> ${item.price}</div>`;

      let btnHtml = '';
      if (equipped) {
        btnHtml = '<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-equipped" disabled>✓ Activo</button>';
      } else if (owned) {
        btnHtml = `<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-equip" onclick="shopEquipTheme('${item.id}')">⚡ Activar</button>`;
      } else {
        const dis = canAfford ? '' : 'disabled';
        btnHtml = `<button class="shop-btn-equip btn-buy" ${dis} onclick="shopBuyTheme('${item.id}')">${canAfford ? '💰 Comprar' : '🔒 ' + item.price + ' 🪙'}</button>`;
      }

      const previewStyle = `background:linear-gradient(160deg,${c1},${c2});`;
      const accentDot = `<div style="position:absolute;bottom:6px;right:6px;width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:50%;background:${c3};box-shadow:0 0 6px ${c3};"></div>`;

      return `
        <div class="shop-item ${equipped?'equipped':(owned?'owned':'locked')}" id="sitem-theme-${item.id}">
          ${badgeHtml}
          <div class="theme-preview" style="${previewStyle}position:relative;">
            <div style="font-size:1.6rem;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;height:100%;">${item.icon}</div>
            ${accentDot}
          </div>
          <div class="shop-item-name">${item.name}</div>
          <div class="shop-item-desc" style="color:${rarityColor}">${item.rarity.toUpperCase()}</div>
          <div class="shop-item-desc">${item.desc}</div>
          ${priceHtml}
          ${btnHtml}
        </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }

  /* ── BUY DECK ── */
  window.shopBuyDeck = function(id) {
    const item = DECK_CATALOG.find(d => d.id === id);
    if (!item) return;
    const sd = loadShopData();
    if (sd.owned.includes(id)) { shopEquipDeck(id); return; }
    if (!window.spendCoins(item.price)) {
      // Shake the item
      const el = document.getElementById('sitem-deck-' + id);
      if (el) { el.classList.add('shop-shake'); setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('shop-shake'),500); }
      showShopToast('❌ Monedas insuficientes (necesitas ' + item.price + ' 🪙)');
      return;
    }
    sd.owned.push(id);
    saveShopData(sd);
    shopEquipDeck(id);
    showShopToast('✅ ¡' + item.name + ' comprado!');
    renderShopDecks();
  };

  /* ── BUY THEME ── */
  window.shopBuyTheme = function(id) {
    const item = THEME_CATALOG.find(t => t.id === id);
    if (!item) return;
    const sd = loadShopData();
    if (sd.owned.includes(id)) { shopEquipTheme(id); return; }
    if (!window.spendCoins(item.price)) {
      const el = document.getElementById('sitem-theme-' + id);
      if (el) { el.classList.add('shop-shake'); setTimeout(()=>el.classList.remove('shop-shake'),500); }
      showShopToast('❌ Monedas insuficientes (necesitas ' + item.price + ' 🪙)');
      return;
    }
    sd.owned.push(id);
    saveShopData(sd);
    shopEquipTheme(id);
    showShopToast('✅ ¡Tema ' + item.name + ' activado!');
    renderShopThemes();
  };

  /* ── EQUIP DECK ── */
  window.shopEquipDeck = function(id) {
    const sd = loadShopData();
    if (!sd.owned.includes(id)) return;
    sd.equipped = sd.equipped || {};
    sd.equipped.deck = id;
    saveShopData(sd);
    applyActiveDeck();
    renderShopDecks();
    showShopToast('🃏 Mazo ' + (DECK_CATALOG.find(d=>d.id===id)||{name:id}).name + ' equipado');
  };

  /* ── EQUIP THEME ── */
  window.shopEquipTheme = function(id) {
    const sd = loadShopData();
    if (!sd.owned.includes(id)) return;
    sd.equipped = sd.equipped || {};
    sd.equipped.theme = id;
    saveShopData(sd);
    applyActiveTheme();
    renderShopThemes();
    showShopToast('🎨 Tema aplicado');
  };

  /* ── APPLY DECK TO CARD BACKS ── */
  window.applyActiveDeck = function() {
    const sd = loadShopData();
    const id = sd.equipped && sd.equipped.deck ? sd.equipped.deck : 'classic';
    const item = DECK_CATALOG.find(d => d.id === id);
    if (!item) return;
    // Inject/update a dynamic style for .card-back
    let styleEl = document.getElementById('activeDeckStyle');
    if (!styleEl) {
      styleEl = document.createElement('style');
      styleEl.id = 'activeDeckStyle';
      document.head.appendChild(styleEl);
    }
    styleEl.textContent = id === 'classic'
      ? ''  // default CSS handles it
      : `.card-back { background:${item.pattern} !important; border-color:rgba(255,255,255,.3) !important; }`;
  };

  /* ── APPLY THEME ── */
  window.applyActiveTheme = function() {
    const sd = loadShopData();
    const id = sd.equipped && sd.equipped.theme ? sd.equipped.theme : 'casino';
    const item = THEME_CATALOG.find(t => t.id === id);
    // Remove all theme classes
    THEME_CATALOG.forEach(t => { if (t.bodyClass) document.body.classList.remove(t.bodyClass); });
    if (item && item.bodyClass) document.body.classList.add(item.bodyClass);
    // Update app frame gradient
    const frame = document.getElementById('appFrame');
    if (frame && item) {
      const [c1, c2] = item.colors;
      frame.style.background = `linear-gradient(160deg,${c1} 0%,${c2} 100%)`;
    }
  };

  /* ── SHOP TOAST ── */
  function showShopToast(msg) {
    // Use global toast if available
    if (window.showToast) { window.showToast(msg); return; }
    const t = document.getElementById('shopToast');
    if (!t) return;
    t.textContent = msg;
    t.classList.add('show');
    clearTimeout(t._timer);
    t._timer = setTimeout(() => t.classList.remove('show'), 2500);
  }

  /* ── INIT ON LOAD ── */
  function shopInit() {
    updateCoinDisplays();
    applyActiveDeck();
    applyActiveTheme();
    checkShopNewBadge();
  }

  // Run after DOM ready
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', shopInit);
  } else {
    setTimeout(shopInit, 300);
  }

  /* ── EXPOSE FOR EXTERNAL USE ── */
  window.ShopSystem = {
    addCoins: window.addCoins,
    spendCoins: window.spendCoins,
    getCoins: window.getCoins,
    openShop: window.openShop,
    applyActiveDeck: window.applyActiveDeck,
    applyActiveTheme: window.applyActiveTheme,
    DECK_CATALOG,
    THEME_CATALOG,
  };

})(); // end IIFE


/* ═══ COIN ECONOMY HOOKS v19.0 ═══ */

/* Hook endGame to award coins on win */
(function() {
  const COIN_WIN = { facil:10, normal:15, dificil:25, experto:40 };
  const COIN_TOURNAMENT_WIN = 80;
  const COIN_DAILY_WIN = 50;
  const COIN_PERFECT = 30; // no draws used

  const _shopOrigEndGame = window.endGame;
  window.endGame = async function() {
    if (_shopOrigEndGame) await _shopOrigEndGame.apply(this, arguments);
    // Award coins based on result (gameWon is global)
    try {
      if (window.gameWon) {
        const diff   = window.currentDiff   || 'normal';
        const mode   = window.currentMode   || 'clasico';
        const drew   = window.drawsThisGame || 0;
        let coins = COIN_WIN[diff] || COIN_WIN.normal;
        let reasons = [];

        if (mode === 'torneo') { coins = Math.max(coins, COIN_TOURNAMENT_WIN); reasons.push('Torneo'); }
        if (mode === 'diario') { coins = Math.max(coins, COIN_DAILY_WIN); reasons.push('Desafío Diario'); }
        if (drew === 0)        { coins += COIN_PERFECT; reasons.push('Partida Perfecta'); }

        const reason = reasons.length ? reasons.join(' + ') : 'Victoria';
        window.addCoins(coins, reason);
      }
    } catch(e) { /* silent */ }
  };
})();

/* Hook checkAchievements to award coins per rarity */
(function() {
  const COIN_ACHIEV = { common:20, uncommon:35, rare:60, epic:100, legendary:150 };
  const _shopOrigCheckAch = window.checkAchievements;
  window.checkAchievements = function() {
    // Get achievements before
    const before = (() => {
      try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ol_achiev_v14') || '{}'); } catch(e){ return {}; }
    })();

    if (_shopOrigCheckAch) _shopOrigCheckAch.apply(this, arguments);

    // Get achievements after
    setTimeout(() => {
      try {
        const after = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ol_achiev_v14') || '{}');
        const ACHIEVEMENTS = window.ACHIEVEMENTS || [];
        ACHIEVEMENTS.forEach(a => {
          if (!before[a.id] && after[a.id]) {
            // Newly unlocked
            const rarity = (a.rarity||'common').toLowerCase();
            const coins = COIN_ACHIEV[rarity] || COIN_ACHIEV.common;
            window.addCoins(coins, 'Logro: ' + (a.name||a.id));
          }
        });
      } catch(e) { /* silent */ }
    }, 500);
  };
})();

/* Hook addXpToProfile for prestige bonus */
(function() {
  const _shopOrigAddXp = window.addXpToProfile;
  window.addXpToProfile = function(xpAmount, breakdown) {
    const result = _shopOrigAddXp ? _shopOrigAddXp.apply(this, arguments) : null;
    // Prestige bonus
    try {
      if (result && result.lvlUp) {
        const prof = window.loadProfile ? window.loadProfile() : null;
        if (prof && prof.prestige && prof.prestige > 0) {
          window.addCoins(200, '¡Prestigio ' + prof.prestige + '!');
        }
      }
    } catch(e) { /* silent */ }
    return result;
  };
})();

/* Award 100 coins when tutorial is completed (once) */
(function() {
  const LS_TUT_COIN = 'ol_tut_coin_v17';
  const _origTutComplete = window.Tutorial && window.Tutorial.complete;
  // Hook after Tutorial object is created (slight delay)
  setTimeout(() => {
    if (window.Tutorial && window.Tutorial.complete && !window._shopTutHooked) {
      window._shopTutHooked = true;
      const origComplete = window.Tutorial.complete;
      window.Tutorial.complete = function() {
        origComplete.apply(this, arguments);
        if (!localStorage.getItem(LS_TUT_COIN)) {
          localStorage.setItem(LS_TUT_COIN, '1');
          window.addCoins(100, 'Tutorial completado');
        }
      };
    }
  }, 500);
})();

/* Track draws per game for "perfect" bonus */
(function() {
  window.drawsThisGame = 0;
  const _shopOrigStartGame = window.startGame;
  window.startGame = async function() {
    window.drawsThisGame = 0;
    if (_shopOrigStartGame) await _shopOrigStartGame.apply(this, arguments);
  };
  const _shopOrigDrawCard = window.drawCard;
  window.drawCard = function() {
    window.drawsThisGame = (window.drawsThisGame||0) + 1;
    if (_shopOrigDrawCard) return _shopOrigDrawCard.apply(this, arguments);
  };
})();

    {lv:50, type:'special',  icon:'👑',  name:'GRAN FINAL S1 Premium', desc:'Título + 2000 monedas + mazo exclusivo', val:{coins:2000,deck:'royal',avatar:'🎖️',title:'⚡ CAMPEÓN S1 ⚡'}},
  ];

  /* ── PERSISTENCE ── */
  function loadBP() {
    try {
      const raw = localStorage.getItem(LS_BP);
      const def = {
        season: SEASON_ID,
        premium: false,
        bpXp: 0,
        level: 0,
        freeClaimed: [],   // array of levels claimed on free track
        premClaimed: [],   // array of levels claimed on prem track
        xpBoostsLeft: 0,
        xpBoostMult: 1.5,
        activeTitles: [],
        seasonStartMs: Date.now(),
      };
      if (!raw) return def;
      return Object.assign(def, JSON.parse(raw));
    } catch(e) {
      return { season:SEASON_ID, premium:false, bpXp:0, level:0,
               freeClaimed:[], premClaimed:[], xpBoostsLeft:0,
               xpBoostMult:1.5, activeTitles:[], seasonStartMs:Date.now() };
    }
  }
  function saveBP(d) { localStorage.setItem(LS_BP, JSON.stringify(d)); }

  /* ── XP CALCULATION ── */
  function bpLevelFromXp(totalXp) {
    const lv = Math.min(Math.floor(totalXp / BP_XP_PER_LV), BP_MAX_LV);
    const xpInLv = totalXp % BP_XP_PER_LV;
    const xpNeeded = BP_XP_PER_LV;
    return { level: lv, xpInLevel: xpInLv, xpNeeded };
  }

  /* ── ADD BP XP (called from game events) ── */
  window.addBpXp = function(amount, source) {
    const bp = loadBP();
    let finalAmt = amount;
    // Apply boost if active
    if (bp.xpBoostsLeft > 0) {
      finalAmt = Math.round(amount * (bp.xpBoostMult || 1.5));
      bp.xpBoostsLeft = Math.max(0, bp.xpBoostsLeft - 1);
    }
    bp.bpXp = (bp.bpXp || 0) + finalAmt;
    const prev = bp.level || 0;
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    bp.level = info.level;
    saveBP(bp);
    updateBpUI();
    // Show level-up notification
    if (info.level > prev) {
      for (let lv = prev + 1; lv <= info.level; lv++) {
        showBpLevelUpToast(lv);
      }
    }
    // Update chip
    updateBpChipIndicator();
    checkBpNavBadge();
  };

  /* ── UNLOCK PREMIUM ── */
  window.bpUnlockPremium = function() {
    const bp = loadBP();
    if (bp.premium) { showBpToast('✅ Ya tienes el Pase Premium'); return; }
    if (!window.spendCoins || !window.spendCoins(PREM_COST)) {
      showBpToast('❌ Necesitas ' + PREM_COST + ' 🪙 para el Pase Premium');
      const banner = document.getElementById('bpUnlockBanner');
      if (banner) { banner.classList.add('shop-shake'); setTimeout(()=>banner.classList.remove('shop-shake'),500); }
      return;
    }
    bp.premium = true;
    saveBP(bp);
    showBpToast('🎉 ¡Pase Premium activado! 30 días de recompensas exclusivas');
    updateBpUI();
    renderBpRewards();
    // Update status text
    const st = document.getElementById('bpPremStatus');
    if (st) st.textContent = '✓ Activo';
    const banner = document.getElementById('bpUnlockBanner');
    if (banner) banner.style.display = 'none';
  };

  /* ── CLAIM REWARD ── */
  window.bpClaimReward = function(level, track) {
    const bp = loadBP();
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    if (info.level < level) { showBpToast('⚠️ Necesitas nivel ' + level + ' del pase'); return; }
    if (track === 'prem' && !bp.premium) { showBpToast('👑 Necesitas el Pase Premium'); return; }

    const claimedKey = track === 'free' ? 'freeClaimed' : 'premClaimed';
    if ((bp[claimedKey] || []).includes(level)) { showBpToast('✅ Ya reclamaste esta recompensa'); return; }

    // Find reward
    const catalog = track === 'free' ? FREE_REWARDS : PREM_REWARDS;
    const reward = catalog.find(r => r.lv === level);
    if (!reward) return;

    // Apply reward
    applyBpReward(bp, reward, track);
    bp[claimedKey] = [...(bp[claimedKey]||[]), level];
    saveBP(bp);
    renderBpRewards();
    updateBpUI();

    // Animate
    const rowEl = document.getElementById('bprow-' + track + '-' + level);
    if (rowEl) { rowEl.classList.add('bp-claiming'); setTimeout(()=>rowEl.classList.remove('bp-claiming'),450); }

    // Star particles
    launchBpStars(level, track);

    // Show popup
    showBpRewardPopup(reward);
  };

  function applyBpReward(bp, reward, track) {
    const t = reward.type;
    const v = reward.val;
    if (t === 'coins') {
      window.addCoins && window.addCoins(v, 'Battle Pass Nv.' + reward.lv);
    } else if (t === 'xp_boost') {
      bp.xpBoostsLeft = (bp.xpBoostsLeft||0) + v;
      const mult = v >= 15 ? (v >= 25 ? 4 : 3) : 1.5;
      bp.xpBoostMult = mult;
      showBpToast('⚡ ' + v + ' partidas con XP ×' + mult + ' activadas');
    } else if (t === 'deck') {
      unlockShopItem('deck', v);
    } else if (t === 'theme') {
      unlockShopItem('theme', v);
    } else if (t === 'avatar') {
      // Add to profile avatars collection (just show toast, user can set it)
      showBpToast('🎭 Avatar ' + v + ' desbloqueado – cámbialo en Perfil');
    } else if (t === 'title') {
      bp.activeTitles = [...(bp.activeTitles||[]), v];
      showBpToast('🏷️ Título "' + v + '" desbloqueado');
    } else if (t === 'special') {
      // Multi-reward
      if (v.coins)   window.addCoins && window.addCoins(v.coins, 'Battle Pass Caja Nv.' + reward.lv);
      if (v.deck)    unlockShopItem('deck', v.deck);
      if (v.theme)   unlockShopItem('theme', v.theme);
      if (v.avatar)  showBpToast('🎭 Avatar ' + v.avatar + ' desbloqueado');
      if (v.title)   { bp.activeTitles = [...(bp.activeTitles||[]), v.title]; }
      if (v.boosts) {
        bp.xpBoostsLeft = (bp.xpBoostsLeft||0) + v.boosts;
        bp.xpBoostMult  = v.boostMult || 2;
      }
    }
  }

  function unlockShopItem(type, id) {
    const sdRaw = localStorage.getItem('ol_shop_v17');
    let sd;
    try { sd = sdRaw ? JSON.parse(sdRaw) : {owned:['classic','casino'],equipped:{deck:'classic',theme:'casino'},spent:0,earned:0}; }
    catch(e) { sd = {owned:['classic','casino'],equipped:{deck:'classic',theme:'casino'},spent:0,earned:0}; }
    if (!sd.owned.includes(id)) {
      sd.owned.push(id);
      localStorage.setItem('ol_shop_v17', JSON.stringify(sd));
      showBpToast('🎁 ' + (type==='deck'?'Mazo':'Tema') + ' "' + id + '" desbloqueado en la Tienda');
    }
  }

  /* ── RENDER REWARDS LIST ── */
  let _currentTrack = 'free';

  window.bpSwitchTrack = function(track) {
    _currentTrack = track;
    ['free','prem'].forEach(t => {
      const tb = document.getElementById('bptab-' + t);
      if (tb) tb.classList.toggle('active', t === track);
    });
    const banner = document.getElementById('bpUnlockBanner');
    if (banner) {
      const bp = loadBP();
      banner.style.display = (track === 'prem' && !bp.premium) ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }
    renderBpRewards();
  };

  function renderBpRewards() {
    const list = document.getElementById('bpRewardsList');
    if (!list) return;
    const bp = loadBP();
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    const curLv = info.level;
    const track = _currentTrack;
    const catalog = track === 'free' ? FREE_REWARDS : PREM_REWARDS;
    const claimed = track === 'free' ? (bp.freeClaimed||[]) : (bp.premClaimed||[]);

    const MILESTONES = [5,10,20,25,30,40,50];

    list.innerHTML = catalog.map(reward => {
      const lv = reward.lv;
      const reached = curLv >= lv;
      const isClaimed = claimed.includes(lv);
      const isCurrent = curLv === lv;
      const isMilestone = MILESTONES.includes(lv);
      const lockedPrem = (track === 'prem' && !bp.premium);

      // Level number classes
      let lvClass = 'bp-level-num';
      if (isCurrent) lvClass += ' current';
      else if (reached) lvClass += ' reached';

      // Row classes
      let rowClass = 'bp-level-row';
      if (isCurrent) rowClass += ' current';
      else if (reached) rowClass += ' reached';
      if (isMilestone) rowClass += ' milestone';

      // Reward card classes
      let cardClass = 'bp-reward-' + (track === 'free' ? 'free' : 'prem');
      if (reached && !isClaimed) cardClass += ' current';
      else if (reached && isClaimed) cardClass += ' reached claimed';
      if (lockedPrem) cardClass += ' locked-prem';

      // Icon class
      const iconClass = 'bp-rwd-icon icon-' + reward.type;

      // Claim button
      let btnHtml = '';
      if (isClaimed) {
        btnHtml = '<button class="bp-claim-btn claimed" disabled>✓</button>';
      } else if (reached && !lockedPrem) {
        btnHtml = `<button class="bp-claim-btn claimable" onclick="bpClaimReward(${lv},'${track}')">🎁 Clic</button>`;
      } else {
        btnHtml = `<button class="bp-claim-btn locked" disabled>${lockedPrem?'👑':'🔒'}</button>`;
      }

      // XP needed hint
      let xpHint = '';
      if (!reached) {
        const xpNeeded = lv * BP_XP_PER_LV - bp.bpXp;
        xpHint = `<div class="bp-rwd-desc" style="color:rgba(168,85,247,.5);">Faltan ${xpNeeded} XP</div>`;
      }

      return `
        <div class="${rowClass}" id="bprow-${track}-${lv}">
          <div class="${lvClass}">
            <span>${lv}</span>
            <span class="lv-text">${isMilestone?'⭐':''}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="${cardClass}">
            <div class="${iconClass}">${reward.icon}</div>
            <div class="bp-rwd-info">
              <div class="bp-rwd-name">${reward.name}</div>
              <div class="bp-rwd-desc">${reward.desc}</div>
              ${xpHint}
            </div>
            ${btnHtml}
          </div>
        </div>`;
    }).join('');
  }

  /* ── UPDATE HEADER UI ── */
  function updateBpUI() {
    const bp = loadBP();
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    const lv = info.level;
    const pct = Math.round((info.xpInLevel / info.xpNeeded) * 100);

    const setT = (id, v) => { const el=document.getElementById(id); if(el) el.textContent=v; };
    setT('bpCurrentLevel', 'Nv. ' + lv);
    setT('bpTotalXpDisplay', bp.bpXp);
    setT('bpNextXpDisplay', (lv + 1) * BP_XP_PER_LV);
    setT('bpXpInLevel', info.xpInLevel);
    setT('bpXpNeeded', info.xpNeeded);

    const bar = document.getElementById('bpXpBarFill');
    if (bar) bar.style.width = pct + '%';

    // Count claimable
    const freeCat = FREE_REWARDS.filter(r => r.lv <= lv);
    const premCat = PREM_REWARDS.filter(r => r.lv <= lv && bp.premium);
    const freeClaimable = freeCat.filter(r => !(bp.freeClaimed||[]).includes(r.lv)).length;
    const premClaimable = premCat.filter(r => !(bp.premClaimed||[]).includes(r.lv)).length;
    setT('bpClaimableCount', freeClaimable + premClaimable);

    // Season timer
    const now = Date.now();
    const diff = Math.max(0, SEASON_END.getTime() - now);
    const days = Math.floor(diff / 86400000);
    const hours = Math.floor((diff % 86400000) / 3600000);
    setT('bpSeasonTimer', days + 'd ' + hours + 'h');

    // Premium status
    const premSt = document.getElementById('bpPremStatus');
    if (premSt) premSt.textContent = bp.premium ? '✓ Activo' : '';

    // Premium banner
    const banner = document.getElementById('bpUnlockBanner');
    if (banner) {
      banner.style.display = (_currentTrack === 'prem' && !bp.premium) ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }

    // Boost indicator
    if (bp.xpBoostsLeft > 0) {
      const xpRow = document.getElementById('bpXpInLevel');
      if (xpRow && xpRow.parentElement) {
        let boostEl = document.getElementById('bpBoostPill');
        if (!boostEl) {
          boostEl = document.createElement('span');
          boostEl.id = 'bpBoostPill';
          boostEl.className = 'bp-xp-boost-active';
          xpRow.parentElement.appendChild(boostEl);
        }
        boostEl.textContent = '⚡ ×' + (bp.xpBoostMult||1.5) + ' (' + bp.xpBoostsLeft + ' partidas)';
      }
    }
  }

  /* ── CHIP INDICATOR ── */
  function updateBpChipIndicator() {
    const bp = loadBP();
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    const chip = document.getElementById('bpChipLevel');
    if (chip) chip.textContent = 'Nv.' + info.level;
  }

  /* ── NAV BADGE ── */
  function checkBpNavBadge() {
    const bp = loadBP();
    const info = bpLevelFromXp(bp.bpXp);
    const lv = info.level;
    const freeClaim = FREE_REWARDS.some(r => r.lv <= lv && !(bp.freeClaimed||[]).includes(r.lv));
    const premClaim = bp.premium && PREM_REWARDS.some(r => r.lv <= lv && !(bp.premClaimed||[]).includes(r.lv));
    const badge = document.getElementById('bpNavBadge');
    if (badge) badge.style.display = (freeClaim || premClaim) ? 'block' : 'none';
  }

  /* ── OPEN / CLOSE ── */
  window.openBattlePass = function() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('bpModal');
    if (!modal) return;
    modal.classList.add('open');
    updateBpUI();
    renderBpRewards();
    bpSwitchTrack('free');
    // Nav highlight
    document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    const bp = document.getElementById('bnav-bp');
    if (bp) bp.classList.add('active');
    // Hide new badge
    const badge = document.getElementById('bpNavBadge');
    if (badge) badge.style.display = 'none';
  };

  window.closeBattlePass = function() {
    const modal = document.getElementById('bpModal');
    if (modal) modal.classList.remove('open');
    document.querySelectorAll('.bnav-item').forEach(b => b.classList.remove('active'));
    const hb = document.getElementById('bnav-home');
    if (hb) hb.classList.add('active');
  };

  /* ── REWARD POPUP ── */
  function showBpRewardPopup(reward) {
    document.getElementById('bpPopupIcon').textContent  = reward.icon;
    document.getElementById('bpPopupName').textContent  = reward.name;
    document.getElementById('bpPopupDesc').textContent  = reward.desc;
    document.getElementById('bpRewardPopup').classList.add('show');
  }
  window.closeBpPopup = function() {
    document.getElementById('bpRewardPopup').classList.remove('show');
  };

  /* ── LEVEL-UP TOAST ── */
  function showBpLevelUpToast(lv) {
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (window.showToast) window.showToast('🎖️ ¡Battle Pass Nivel ' + lv + '! Nuevas recompensas disponibles');
    }, lv * 300);
  }

  /* ── STAR PARTICLES ── */
  function launchBpStars(lv, track) {
    const rowEl = document.getElementById('bprow-' + track + '-' + lv);
    if (!rowEl) return;
    const rect = rowEl.getBoundingClientRect();
    const cx = rect.left + rect.width / 2;
    const cy = rect.top  + rect.height / 2;
    ['⭐','✨','🌟','💫','🎉'].forEach((emoji, i) => {
      const el = document.createElement('div');
      el.className = 'bp-star-particle';
      el.textContent = emoji;
      const angle = (i / 5) * Math.PI * 2;
      const dist = 60 + Math.random() * 40;
      el.style.left = cx + 'px';
      el.style.top  = cy + 'px';
      el.style.setProperty('--dx', Math.cos(angle) * dist + 'px');
      el.style.setProperty('--dy', Math.sin(angle) * dist + 'px');
      document.body.appendChild(el);
      setTimeout(() => el.remove(), 750);
    });
  }

  /* ── BP TOAST ── */
  function showBpToast(msg) {
    if (window.showToast) { window.showToast(msg); return; }
  }

  /* ── INIT ── */
  function bpInit() {
    updateBpChipIndicator();
    checkBpNavBadge();
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', bpInit);
  } else {
    setTimeout(bpInit, 400);
  }

  /* ── EXPOSE ── */
  window.BattlePass = { addBpXp: window.addBpXp, openBattlePass: window.openBattlePass, loadBP };

})(); // end Battle Pass IIFE


/* ═══ BATTLE PASS XP ECONOMY HOOKS v19.0 ═══ */
(function() {
  /* Award BP XP on game events */
  const BP_XP = {
    win_facil:15, win_normal:25, win_dificil:40, win_experto:60,
    lose: 5, tournament_win:80, daily_win:70, perfect_win:20,
    achiev_common:10, achiev_uncommon:20, achiev_rare:35, achiev_epic:60, achiev_legendary:100,
  };

  /* Hook endGame for BP XP */
  const _bpOrigEndGame = window.endGame;
  window.endGame = async function(playerWon) {
    if (_bpOrigEndGame) await _bpOrigEndGame.apply(this, arguments);
    try {
      if (typeof window.addBpXp === 'function') {
        if (playerWon) {
          const diff = window.currentDiff || 'normal';
          const mode = window.currentMode || 'clasico';
          let xp = BP_XP['win_' + diff] || BP_XP.win_normal;
          if (mode === 'torneo')  xp = Math.max(xp, BP_XP.tournament_win);
          if (mode === 'diario')  xp = Math.max(xp, BP_XP.daily_win);
          if ((window.drawsThisGame||0) === 0) xp += BP_XP.perfect_win;
          window.addBpXp(xp, 'Victoria');
        } else {
          window.addBpXp(BP_XP.lose, 'Derrota');
        }
      }
    } catch(e) {}
  };

  /* Hook checkAchievements for BP XP */
  const _bpOrigCheckAch = window.checkAchievements;
  window.checkAchievements = function() {
    const before = (() => {
      try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ol_achiev_v14') || '{}'); } catch(e){ return {}; }
    })();
    if (_bpOrigCheckAch) _bpOrigCheckAch.apply(this, arguments);
    setTimeout(() => {
      try {
        const after = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('ol_achiev_v14') || '{}');
        const ACHIEVEMENTS = window.ACHIEVEMENTS || [];
        ACHIEVEMENTS.forEach(a => {
          if (!before[a.id] && after[a.id] && window.addBpXp) {
            const rarity = (a.rarity||'common').toLowerCase();
            const xp = BP_XP['achiev_' + rarity] || BP_XP.achiev_common;
            window.addBpXp(xp, 'Logro: ' + (a.name||a.id));
          }
        });
      } catch(e) {}
    }, 600);
  };
})();



/* ══ FLYING CARD DEAL ANIMATION v19.0 ══
   Lanza una mini-carta desde la zona del mazo hacia la mano del jugador o la IA */
function animDealCard(target) {
  try {
    const deckZone = document.getElementById('deckZone') ||
                     document.getElementById('tableZone');
    const handZone = target === 'player'
      ? document.getElementById('playerArea')
      : document.getElementById('aiArea');
    if (!deckZone || !handZone) return;

    const srcRect  = deckZone.getBoundingClientRect();
    const destRect = handZone.getBoundingClientRect();

    const fly = document.createElement('div');
    fly.className = 'deal-fly' + (target === 'player' ? ' player-card' : '');

    // Start at deck center
    fly.style.left = (srcRect.left + srcRect.width/2  - 24) + 'px';
    fly.style.top  = (srcRect.top  + srcRect.height/2 - 35) + 'px';
    fly.style.setProperty('--fly-dur', '0.38s');
    fly.style.setProperty('--fly-rot', ((Math.random()-.5)*20) + 'deg');

    document.body.appendChild(fly);

    // Trigger reflow then animate to destination
    fly.getBoundingClientRect();
    requestAnimationFrame(() => {
      fly.style.left = (destRect.left + destRect.width/2  - 24) + 'px';
      fly.style.top  = (destRect.top  + destRect.height/2 - 35) + 'px';
      fly.style.transform = 'rotate(0deg) scale(0.85)';
      fly.style.opacity = '0.9';
    });

    // After landing: pop & remove
    setTimeout(() => {
      fly.classList.add('landed');
      setTimeout(() => fly.remove(), 300);
    }, 420);

    // Add pop animation to last card in hand
    setTimeout(() => {
      const cards = handZone.querySelectorAll('.card, .card-back');
      if (cards.length) {
        const last = cards[cards.length - 1];
        last.classList.add('just-dealt');
        setTimeout(() => last.classList.remove('just-dealt'), 350);
      }
    }, 400);
  } catch(e) { /* silent – animation is optional */ }
}


/* ══ FIX: Ensure Shop / BattlePass / Profile always accessible ══ */
(function fixModalAccess() {
  // Make sure openShop, openBattlePass and openProfileModal
  // don't require any in-game state
  const _ensureHome = () => {
    // If game is active, don't block access to modals
    // Just show them over the current screen
    const gs = document.getElementById('gameScreen');
    return gs && gs.classList.contains('active');
  };

  // Patch navTo to also handle shop and bp
  const _origNavTo = window.navTo;
  window.navTo = function(screen) {
    if (screen === 'home') {
      if (_origNavTo) return _origNavTo(screen);
    }
    if (screen === 'shop')  { sfxButton(); openShop(); return; }
    if (screen === 'bp')    { sfxButton(); openBattlePass(); return; }
    if (screen === 'perfil'){ sfxButton(); openProfileModal(); return; }
    if (_origNavTo) _origNavTo(screen);
  };

  // Ensure profile modal z-index is high enough
  setTimeout(() => {
    const pm = document.getElementById('profileModal') ||
               document.querySelector('.profile-modal');
    if (pm) {
      pm.style.zIndex = '950';
    }
  }, 500);
})();


/* ══ FIX: runShuffleAnimation with smooth hide ══ */
(function patchShuffleHide() {
  const _origStartShuffle = window.startShuffle;
  if (!_origStartShuffle) return;
  // Patch the shuffle hide to use opacity transition
  window._smoothHideShuffle = function() {
    const ss = document.getElementById('shuffleScreen');
    if (!ss) return Promise.resolve();
    ss.classList.add('hiding');
    return new Promise(res => setTimeout(() => {
      ss.classList.remove('show','hiding');
      res();
    }, 420));
  };
})();

</script>
